Kwaadubɔfoɔ kyerɛɛ mu sɛ berɛ a wɔkyeree wɔn no, wɔhunuu atuo mmoba nsia ne sika GHC1,292,180, a ɛyɛ anhwea a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ sika kɔkɔɔ dɔteɛ, akokɔsradeɛ a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ sika kɔkɔɔ dadeɛ ne nsunsuo a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ mercury.
Obi a wosusuw sɛ ɔyɛ odwowtwafo a ɔde ne nsa akyerɛ no aguan afi polisifo nsam wɔ Kyebi a ɛwɔ Apueɛ Mantam mu.
Starr News agye atom wɔ Kyebi sɛ kuw bi a wɔfrɛ wɔn Anti Armed Robbery ne Personnel a wɔwɔ CID Adwumayɛbea ti no kyeree Ebenezer Gyimah din Peace wɔ Ayɛwohomumɔ bosome da a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmeɛnsa ne aduonu baako wɔ Abuakwa Atifi ne Kesee fam Mansini ahodoɔ mu.
Wɔde onipa a wɔde no asɛm too no so no kɔɔ Kyebi Zongo sɛ ɔrekɔhwehwɛ no nanso ɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ obeguan.
Da koro akyi no, Kyebi Polisifo nso kyeree odwowtwafo foforo a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔfrɛ noMusa Kamara a ɔyɛ 266, a na ɔka Polisifo ho a ɔpɛ sɛ wɔbɔ ne din wɔ Kibi Zongo wɔ June 25,2021 no.
Afei nso ɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ obeguan nanso wɔtoo no tuo wɔ ne kotodwe benkum mu maa polisifo dii no so.
Wɔde ɔmanehunufoɔ yi yɛɛ ntɛm de no kɔɔ Kyebi aban ayaresabea a wɔde no rekɔhyɛ polisifoɔ ase.
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ nnipa mmienu yi ka dwowtwafoɔ a wɔn ho yɛ hu wɔ Kibi, Akyem Tafo, Osiem, Anyinasin ne faako a ɛbɛn hɔ no ho.
Anyɛ yiye koraa no, wɔyɛɛ dwowtwafo ntua 10 ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ Kuropɔn abien no mu wɔ asram abiɛsa mu.
Ntua a adwowtwafoɔ no de baa wɔn so wɔ Ayɛwohomumɔ 6,2021 no kɔfaa ɔbea bi a basabasayɛfoɔ bɔɔ no tuo wɔ Akyem Ettukrom a ɛwɔ bunso a ɛwɔ Koforidua a ɛwɔ bunso kwantempɔn so.
Nanso nsɛmmɔnedifoɔ baanu a wɔfrɛ wɔn Haruna Amadu a wɔdii mfeɛ aduonu num ne Joseph Nyira a wɔdii mfeɛ aduonu num no, ankyɛ koraa na wɔkyeree wɔn.
Atuo abien a wɔnyɛɛ ho kyerɛwtohɔ, nkrante biako, sika a ɛwɔ GhC257.00, kɔmputa biako a ɛwɔ kɔmputa so, kotoku abiɛsa a nnipa baanu a wɔyɛɛ wɔn ayayade no nkrataa abien wom, nnipa baanu a wɔyɛɛ wɔn ayayade no SIM nkrataa a ɛwɔ kɔmputa so, ne sukuuni bag tuntum bi a wɔn a wosusuw sɛ wɔyɛ wɔn ayayade no hyɛɛt wom na woyii.
Wɔ May 24,2021 mu no, wɔbɔɔ onipa bi tuo bere a akorɔmfo tow hyɛɛ Koforidua so kɔɔ Akyem Kukurantumi kwan so wɔ Apueɛ Mantam mu no.
Adwowtwafoɔ no bɔɔ kwan mu bɛyɛ anɔpa 4:30 wɔ Barfuor Nkwanta a ɛbɛn Sorkode Dwaso junction kwan a polisifoɔ taa hwehwɛ kar a ɛrekɔ no mu.
Sɛnea onipa bi kyerɛ no, akorɔmfoɔ a wɔwɔ tuo kunkum Ghc50,000 no bɔɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔfow kar bɛyɛ 20.
Wukuada, April 28,2021 no, adwowtwafoɔ no kɔtow hyɛɛ Guest House ne baabi a wɔhyehyɛ mframa wɔ Akyem Kukurantumi bɛyɛ anɔpa nnɔnsia wɔ atuo a wɔtotoweeɛ mu no, wɔn nso bubuu adidibea a ɛwɔ ahɔho no fie no mu, na ɛsɛee Ghc137 fii baabi a wɔhyehyɛ mframa wɔ hɔ no.
Afei nso wɔfaa tuo biako a ɛwɔ banbɔfoɔ a ɔbɔɔ ne ho ban anadwo berɛ a na dwowtwa no rekɔ so no de too ɔfasu bi ho.
Wɔanyɛ nnipa a wowuwui no ho kyerɛwtohɔ biara.
Wɔyɛɛ BB mfonini ason a hwee nnim, BB mfonini biako a ɛwɔ nkwa, ne akwan abiɛsa wɔ hɔ.
Adwowtwafo no nyaa wɔn ti didii mu wɔ kar bi a wɔfrɛ no saloon w/o mu.
Dwowtwa no sii nnawɔtwe mmiɛnsa pɛ wɔ fango dwowtwa a ɛte saa ara akyi na Nuhu Yashawu a wadi mfe 32 wui wɔ Akyem Osiem a ɛbɛn hɔ no.
Onipa baako nso de tuo piraa dwowtwa a ɛkɔɔ so Dwoda, April 5,2021 wɔ bɛyɛ anɔpa nɔnna nɔnna nɔnna nɔnnan a wokurakura atuo mmiɛnsa ne sekan tow hyɛɛ Goodness Energy Filling dwumadibea a ɛwɔ mpɔtam hɔ no.
Adwowtwafo no de sika a wonnim sɛ ɛyɛ pɛtro gyinabea a wɔtɔn no anadwo no siei.
Adwowtwafo no faa Motorola telefon a na ɔbarima bi a wadi mfe 30 a ɔyɛ adwuma anadwo a wɔfrɛ no Adamu Zakari wɔ nso.

Abɛdiakyire a ɔyɛ Nhomasua Soafoɔ, na ɔyɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwani wɔ Assin South Rev. John Ntim Fordjour ama akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ awerɛhyɛ sɛ wɔn yiyedi ho asɛm hia aban paa.
Sɛnea ɔkyerɛ no, wɔreyɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ wɔde Teacher Welfare App bedi akyerɛkyerɛfo yiyedi ho nsɛm ho dwuma ntɛm ara.
Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire no kyerɛ sɛ akyerɛkyerɛfo yiyedi ho hia aban kɛse na ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ ɔbɛdi ɔhaw a ɛda nsow a ɛfa ɔkyerɛkyerɛfoɔ nkɔsoɔ, akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ adwuma ho nsɛnnennen, akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ adwuma ho nhyehyɛeɛ ne nneɛma foforɔ ho dwuma ntɛm so.
Ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so adi akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ahiadeɛ ho dwuma no, Ɔtwerɛtwerɛfoɔ Fordjour akyerɛ sɛ ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so adi akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ ahiadeɛ ho dwuma wɔ ɔmantam biara mu sɛ ɛka mmɔden a ɔbɔ sɛ ɔbɛma wɔn asetra atu mpɔn ho.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ dwumadie yi a Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Nhomasua so, Dr. Yaw Osei Adutwum yɛeɛ no bɛboa ma akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ yiyedi ne wɔn akwankyerɛ ho nsɛnnennen bebree no ano abrɛ ase.
Berɛ a ɔne nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfoɔ rekasa wɔ Ghana Ɔman Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ Nkabomkuo (GNAT) a ɛwɔ Nkran a ɔyɛ adwuma soafoɔ nanmusini ase no, John Ntim Fordjour bɔɔ ɔkyerɛkyerɛfoɔ nkabomkuo no soboɔ sɛ ɔwɔ ahotosoɔ sɛ aban bɛnya adwuma mu nsɛnnennen a ɛwɔ hɔ seesei no ano aduro.
Na dwumadi a wɔde dii dwuma sɛ sika a wɔde hyɛ nnwuma mu no asɛmti ne sɛ: “Beyond Teachers Foto; Ma a Wɔbɛma Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfo no Ayɛ Nea Ɛfata.”
Ɔrekasa akyerɛ GNAT mpanyimfoɔ ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma no, ɔkaa sɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa aboa ama ɔman no anya nkɔsoɔ wɔ sikasɛm mu. Ɔsan tĩĩ bɔ a aban ahyɛ sɛ ɔbɛdi ɔkyerɛkyerɛfoɔ yiyedi ho nsɛm ho dwuma wɔ berɛ mu no mu.
Ɔkyerɛɛ anigyeɛ wɔ nhyehyɛeɛ pa a GNAT yɛeɛ sɛ ɛbɛma nnipa a ɛwɔ mu no anya nkɔsoɔ no ho. Ɔkamfoo Ghana Medical Centre a ɛwɔ GNAT dwumadie mu fã kɛseɛ no ara. Ɔkamfoo GNAT nso sɛ ɔde ne sika hyɛɛ adan mu na ɔyɛɛ adwuma maa emufoɔ.
Ɔtwerɛfoɔ Ntim Fordjour hyɛɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ bɔ sɛ Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Nhomasua so no bɛtwerɛ apaawa 280,000 ama akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛbɛtu mpɔn.
Ɔfrɛɛ akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa sɛ wɔmmɛka Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Nhomasua so no ho mma wɔnhyehyɛ wiase nhomasua nhyehyɛeɛ.

Berɛ a ɔrekasa akyerɛ EIB Network Mfinimfini Mantam Kyerɛwfoɔ, Yaw Boagyan, Ɔmantam Polisifoɔ abadiakyire pro Sgt. Evans Isaac Entie kaa wɔ July 23, 2021, bɛyɛ anɔpa 9:30 a ɛyɛ kuw bi a ɛfiri Ghana Medical and Dental Council a ɛwɔ Nkran, a polisifoɔ a wɔfiri Assin Adadientem na wɔyɛɛ wɔn adeɛ maa wɔkyeree Samuel Odartei a wadi mfeɛ 56 no, ɔyɛɛ no oprehyɛn bɛboro mfeɛ nnum wɔ Assin Adadientem.
Bere a kuw no duu hɔ no, wohuu ne babea, Alberta Lanuekor a wadi mfe 36 a ɔyɛ ɔsɛmmɔnedini a ɔhyɛ atade nguguso a ɔhyɛ ɔyarefo bi kuru, na ayarefo afoforo twɛnee sɛ wɔbɛba.
Wɔkyeree wɔn baanu no de wɔn kɔɔ polisifo adwumayɛbea a wɔde nneɛma ahodoɔ a ɛyɛ adwuma te sɛ nnuru a wɔakyerɛw ama wɔn ne nea wɔtɔ ma wɔn bebree ka ho.

Amanyɔkuo a ɛwɔ Bomso amanyɔkuo mu, Isaac Appiah a ɔkaa sɛ bɔne a ɛrekɔ so no yɛ nokorɛ no kaa sɛ, wɔde nhwehwɛmufoɔ bɛkɔ Fida akɔhwehwɛ nnipa a wɔayera no.
Kumase a ɛyɛ Asante mantam no ahenkuro no ahu asiane kɛseɛ a ɛresɛe Ghana cedis ɔpepem pii nnansa a atwam no.
Kumase Kejetia Gua so nso nyaa ne kyɛfa wɔ nsuyiri no mu Wukuada bere a sotɔɔ bebree a ɛwɔ guasoɔ foforɔ no mu nsuyiri no sɛee nneɛma no.
Kumase kurow sohwɛfo Osei Asibey Antwi a ɔyare no ka kyerɛɛ Asante Mantam mu kasamafo Isaac Temmufo Bediako sɛ KMA mfiridwuma kuw no bɛyɛ nhyiamu a ɛfa nsuyiri a ɛrekɔ so wɔ Kumase no ho.
“Sɛ edu anɔpa yi a, mfiridwuma ho nimdeɛ ne nhyehyɛeɛ boayikuo no bɛyɛ nhyiamu a egye ntɛmpɛ wɔ nea ɛrekɔ so no ho. Efi bere a na mewɔ Kumase no, manhu sɛ nsuo refa kuro no mu saa pɛn. Mprempren ɛho hia sɛ yɛyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a emu da hɔ, yɛn nsuka no sua dodo sɛ yɛbɛsoa nsuo no.”
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ wɔ nhyiamu no akyi no, boayikuo no bɛkɔ akɔhwɛ sɛnea nhyiamu no bɛtumi aboa wɔn a wɔn ho akyere wɔn no. Afei nso, wɔbɛhwɛ nneɛma a nhyiamu no bɛtumi ayɛ ntɛm ara.

Ɛno akyi na basabasayɛfoɔ kyeree nnipa baasa biara a wɔbɔɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔyɛ adwowtwafoɔ no mu baanu wɔ Tanokrom, Effia-Kwesimintsim Kuropɔn no borɔn bi so, berɛ a wɔn a wɔkyeree wɔn sɛ wɔwɔ moto bi a ɛretu mmirika soɔ kyeree bag bi a ɛhyɛ ɔbea bi a ɔwɔ beae a ɛbɛn ‘Onyankopɔn yɛ Ɔdɔ chop bar’ mpɔtam.

Nnawɔtwe awiei a etwaam no, na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔte Anaji SSNIT ahyɛmma mu no de wɔn nna bɔ afɔre bere a nnipakuw bi a wɔte moto so faa mpɔtam hɔ kyerɛɛ sɛnea wɔte pɔnkɔ so kosi anɔpa no.

Mmea ne aguadifoɔ bi a wɔtɔn nneɛma wɔ Koforidua Mfinimfini fam gua so a na wɔtɔ nneɛma fĩ wɔ Fanteakwa rural Sikakorabea no de wɔn sika a wɔde asie no ho akasakasa foforɔ aba.
Wɔn a wɔn werɛ ahow no akɔ Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo ne Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie kasamafoɔ, Alban Bagbin ne Ghana Sikakorabea sɛ wɔmmɛboa wɔn mma wɔn nsa nka wɔn sika.
Wɔtew Fanteakwa Rural Sikakorabea a ɛyɛ Fanteakwaakwa North Amankwah Asiamah Mmarahyɛ Baguafo a wɔn bo afuw no dea no wɔ afe 2004 mu, nanso egui wɔ afe 2012 mu.
Ná Sikakorabea no wɔ n’adwumayɛbea ti wɔ Begoro ne baa dwumadibea wɔ Koforidua, Osiem, Suhum, Anyinam, ne ɔmantam no afã foforo.
Wobu akontaa sɛ nnipa bɛboro 1,000 na wɔde wɔn sika too mu.
Wɔn a wohu amane no yɛ akuafo, aguadifo, afirikafo, akyerɛkyerɛfo, asɔfo nketewa, faga adwumayɛfo ne nnwuma nketewa.
Sika a wɔde siei no de ahokyere baa wɔn a wɔn mu binom wuwui bere a nnwuma nketenkete hwee ase no so
Na wɔn a wɔtɔ no mu dodow no ara wɔ Ghana cedis ahanum (GHS500) ne Ghana cedis mpem aduonu ason (GHS27,000.00) a ɛwɔ sikakorabea a abubu no mu.
Wɔyɛɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ bebree ansa na wɔretow aba afe 2016 no. Nnipa a atoyerɛnkyɛm ato wɔn no hyɛɛ ɔsɔretia mmaranimfoɔ a ɔwɔ hɔ saa bere no sɛ ɔmfa wɔn sika a wɔde ato mu no mma. Wɔn a atoyerɛnkyɛm ato wɔn no bi nyaa wɔn sika nanso afoforɔ pii nnyaa wɔn de.
Bere a ɔrekasa akyerɛ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfoɔ a wɔwɔ Koforidua no, wɔn a wɔyɛɛ wɔn ayayadeɛ a wɔn dodoɔ yɛ aduonu 20 no, ɔkaa mmaranimfoɔ no anim sɛ ɔnhyehyɛɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛma watua nkurɔfoɔ ka.
Sɛnea wɔkyerɛ no, mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wɔbɛma wɔn sika abɔ wɔn no yɛɛ ɔkwa berɛ a wɔbɔɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ no soboɔ sɛ wɔantumi antie wɔn frɛ no.
Ɔdetɔnfo bi a wadi mfe 72 a wɔfrɛ no Elizabeth Amoah kaa n’asɛm no kyerɛɛ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfoɔ sɛ ɔhyɛɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no bɔ sɛ ɔbɛbɔ ne sika ho ban wɔ 2020 abatow no akyi nanso ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔbɛdi n’asɛm no so.
“Mekɔɔ Begoro wɔ 2020 ɔsatu berɛ mu sɛ merekɔpɛ me sika nanso Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ no paa me kyɛw na ɔhyɛɛ me bɔ sɛ ɔbɛtua wɔn ka wɔ abatow no akyi pɛɛ. Ɛyɛ awerɛhoɔ sɛ mɛka akyerɛ mo sɛ, Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ no nnii nkonim wɔ abatow no akyi.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ, “bɛyɛ dɛn na me GHC12,000,000,000,000 Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ bɛbɔ me apoo wɔ sika a mede asie mfeɛ bebree akyi na manantew kwa sɛ mmaranimfoɔ. Meresrɛ Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo ne Ɔkasafoɔ sɛ ɔnka nkyerɛ Amankwah Asiamah sɛ ɔmfa me sika mma me anaasɛ yɛmmoaboa yɛn ho ano wɔ Ahosɛpɛw Fie ne Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie nkɔhwehwɛ yɛn sika.”
Ɔfoforo nso kae sɛ, “Yɛresrɛ Ɔmanpanin Akufo Addo ne ɔkasafo Kennedy Agyapong sɛ ɔmfa ne ho nnye asɛm no mu sɛ ɔyɛ NPP kyitaafoɔ panin nanso Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ yi ne yɛn redi no bɔne. Wɔ 2020 abatwa mu no, me ne me babea kɔɔ Begoro sɛ yɛrekɔhwɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a ɔhyɛɛ yɛn abufuo no, misuiɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔne yɛn di no saa ara”
Aguadifo foforo pii nso de wɔn ho hyɛɛ tebea a ɛhaw adwene yi mu, a aware a egui nso ka ho esiane ahokyere a wɔde baa wɔn so no nti.
Mmarahyɛ Bagua a ɛwɔ Fanteakwa North Amankwah Asiamah a na ɔyɛ sikakorabea a ahwe ase no panyin no ampene so sɛ ɔbɛka basabasayɛ a aba nnansa yi ho asɛm
Nanso na wadi kan akyerɛ sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔde wɔn a wɔyɛɛ wɔn bɔne no bɔ bosea de boa Nana Akufo Addo ɔsatu a wɔbɔɔ ho amanneɛ wɔ afe 2012 mu no.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no kyerɛɛ mu sɛ, ɛnteɛ nso sɛ sikakorabea no de adwadifoɔ bɛboro 1,000 ka sɛ n’atadeɛ no bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛpopa adwadifoɔ no mu fã kɛseɛ no ara sika.
Adam Mutaw Kilu a kan no na ɔyɛ fagudeɛtu ne Anyinam ahoɔden Boayikuo a ɛwɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu panin no abɔ Ghana Mmaranimfoɔ panin ahohora wɔ ɛka dɔla ɔpepem 170 a wɔde bu atɛn no ho sɛ, sɛ wɔredi asɛm no wɔ Ghana a anka ɔbɛdi nkonim.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ anka AG no bɛfa akwan ne akwan bi so adi asɛm no mu nkonim.
“Yɛde ahwɛyiye hwɛɛ mu na yehui sɛ adu tebea horow no nyinaa ho na mmarahyɛ bagua no agye atom sɛ ɛyɛ tebea no ho nhwɛso. Enti me fam no, na ɛho nhia sɛ aban no twentwɛn adwuma no ase. Dabi! Na wonim sɛ sɛ ɛkɔ wiase baabiara a, aban no bedi nkogu. Afei ebia wosusuw sɛ wɔbɛdi ho dwuma wɔ Ghana. Ebia wobetumi ama wɔn ntini ahorow ayɛ nsakrae na ama wɔatumi apue.” Mmarahyɛ baguani no ka kyerɛɛ Francis Abban wɔ Morning Starr Yawda no.
Nanso, Kwaadubɔfoɔ Panin no abɔ Mahama aban nanmusini no soboɔ wɔ asɛm yi ho.
Nea Ɛde Asɛm no Bae
Amanaman Ntam Asɛnnibea a ɛhwɛ Arbitration so wɔ January 2021 mu no bɔɔ ka dɔla ɔpepem aduasa ne dɔla ɔpepem aduasa maa Ghana Aban wɔ GC GP nhyehyɛe a wɔatwa mu no ho.
Kan Anyinam Ahoɔden Soafoɔ Boakye Agyarko na ɔtwaa saa nhyehyɛeɛ no mu sɛ ɛyɛ anyinam ahoɔden ho nhyehyɛeɛ foforɔ a NPP de too dwa sɛ ɔman no nhia saa anyinam ahoɔden ho nhyehyɛeɛ no.
Atɛn a Amanaman Ntam Asɛnnibea a ɛhwɛ Arbitration so no bui no hyɛɛ Ghana aban no sɛ ɔntua “GPGC ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ
Na ɛsɛ sɛ Ghana Aban no nso tua GPGC sika a ɛyɛ “US$ 309,877.74 wɔ ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ Arbitration no ho, ɛne US$ 3,000,000 wɔ GPGC mmara mu nnyinasoɔ ne ɛka ne ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ ne dansefo a ɔwɔ nimdeɛ no ho, ɛne ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ US$ 3,309,877.74 wɔ ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ US dollars mmiɛnsa a wɔde hyɛɛ mu no ho.”
Nnipa a wɔte Ajumako Ochiso Mantam mu wɔ Mfinimfini Mantam mu no ani agye kɛse sɛ mpataa bebree aba wɔn asubɔnten [Ochi] a na anka ɛyɛ nsu a wɔnom kɛkɛ no mu.
Eyi sii Yawda anɔpa bere a osu tɔe no. Sɛnea nnipa a wɔtete hɔ kyerɛ no, na ahintasɛm no yɛ nhyira a efi anyame no hɔ.
Akannifoɔ a wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ no hyehyɛɛ nhyehyɛeɛ maa nnipa a wɔwɔ hɔ no kyɛɛ ɔman no mu na wɔde kɔɔ fie.
Bere a ɔrekasa akyerɛ Kasapa FM mantam mu kyerɛwfo, Yaw Boagyan, Wofa Yaw Obosu a na ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ asubɔnten no ano no, ɔkae sɛ eyi mmaa saa da fi bere a ɔbaa mpɔtam hɔ no, na ogye di nso sɛ ɛyɛ nhyira ma ɔmanfoɔ no.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ wɔde mpataa no bi bɛkɔ gua so akɔtɔn. “Sɛ mpataa yi ba asubɔnten korabea hɔ a, matumi afa mmerante ne mmabaa bɛboro aduonu ama wɔayɛ adwuma ama me atɔn wɔ Mankessim, Kasoa, gua so.
“Mente eyi ase efisɛ biribi a ɛte sɛɛ nsisii da wɔ Ajumako Ochiso Mantam mu.”
Nanso nnipa a wɔbaa hɔ no, wɔn mu binom srɛɛ Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Mpataayifoɔ ne Nsuo Mu Nsuo so sɛ wɔmmra mmɛboa wɔn na wɔmfa sakre mmiɛnsa mma wɔn na wɔmfa mpataa no nkɔ gua so.
“Yenni adwuma a yɛbɛyɛ wɔ A jumako Ochiso Mantam mu wɔ ha sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛn nsa bɛka adwuma a yɛde bɛhwɛ yɛn mma nhomasua ne wɔn afie. Enti yɛrefrɛ atumfoɔ sɛ wɔmmra mmɛboa yɛn mma yɛnni ɔhaw ahorow a yɛrehyia wɔ A jumako Ochiso Mantam mu no ho dwuma”
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafo a ɔwɔ Ajumako Ochiso South Maxwell Mensah nso de asɛm no kɔdan Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Mpataayifoɔ ne Asukɔtweaa ne Aban foforɔ sɛ wɔmmoa ɔmanfoɔ ma wɔmfa mpataa mma mpataa foforɔ wɔ asubɔnten no mu na wɔmfa nyɛ adwuma.
Ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ Panin a ɔda Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Anyinam Ahoɔden Bammɔ So, Nana Amoasi VII abɔ Mmaranimfoɔ Panin, Godfred Dame soboɔ sɛ ɔyɛ anibiannasoɔ wɔ Ghana atemmuo ka dɔla ɔpepem 170 a wɔde maa anyinam ahoɔden adwumakuo, The Ghana Power Generation Company (GC GP) no ho.
Wɔ nsɛm a wobisabisaa Nana Amoasi VII wɔ Morning Starr so wɔ Yawda no, ɔfrɛɛ Mmaranimfoɔ Panyin no sɛ ɔmmɛkyerɛ Ghanafoɔ nea enti a wamfa dɔla ɔpepem 170 annye atemmuo ka no.
“Yɛde hokwan kɔɔ asɛnnibea sɔre tiaa gyinaesi no, na yɛpaw sɛ yɛde Covid-19 bedi dwuma de ayi yɛn ho ano. Kwaadubɔfoɔ panin no nso yɛɛ anibiannaso. Wanyɛ ade yiye. Anka obetumi abɔ yɛn ho ban yiye sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛbɛhwɛ mu.”
Ne nsɛm no bae berɛ a Adwadie Asɛnnibea a ɛwɔ London no ampene asɛm a wɔde too Ghana anim wɔ atemmuo ka a ɛyɛ US$ 170 a wɔde bɔɔ adwumayɛfoɔ panin, The Ghana Power Generation Company (GC GP) ho no.
Sɛdeɛ London Asɛnnibea kyerɛ no, Ghana aban amfa mmara a Amanaman Nkabom Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Amanaman Ntam Aguadi Mmara so (UNCITRAL) a ɛwɔ London no gyinaeɛ a ɛtɔ so aduonu nsia wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ntwaam.
Wukuada, Ayɛwohomumɔ da a ɛtɔ so nnwɔtwe no, asɛnnibea no amma Ghana aban no kwan sɛ ɔmfa n’asɛm no nto nkyɛn, na ɔde kaa ho sɛ ɔman no nnyinasoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ wɔde bɛsɔre atia no yɛ “ɛyɛ mmerɛw.”
Aban no nam ne mmaranimfo Godfred Dame so bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛkata 2020 abatoɔ no ne COVID-19 yareɛ no so sɛ adeɛ a ɛbɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔntwentwɛn wɔn nan ase, nanso London asɛnnibea no yii wɔn ano.
Charles Kimmins QC ne Mark Tushingham gyinaa GPGC ananmu wɔ asɛnnibea hɔ, baabi a wɔkyerɛ sɛ Ghana aka akyi dodo sɛ ɔbɛkasa atia gyinaeɛ a wɔasi no.
Ghana de Khawar Qureshi QC a ɛwɔ Serle Court ne Volterra Fietta dii dwuma, na mfiase no ɔde Omnia Strategy dii dwuma. Wɔ asɛnni no mu no, GPGC de Crowns ne Ghanani adwumakuo Baasa, Kimathi ne partners dii dwuma, ɛne ɔsɛe ho abenfo a wɔwɔ FTI Consulting nso.
Afei nso na Ghana wɔ mmaranimfoɔ panin ne Amofa & Ayɔnkofoɔ a wɔwɔ Nkran.
John Beechey, a kan no na ɔyɛ Amanaman Ntam Nsɛmmɔnedifoɔ Asɛnnibea no panin ne Prof Albert Fiadjoe a ɔyɛ Ghanani nhomanimfoɔ a ɔwɔ nnipa mmiɛnsa asɛnnibea no gyinaa otumfoɔ no afã na ɔmaa US$ 170 million, a anigyeɛ a ɛwɔ mu ka ho.
Sɛ wɔka ne nyinaa bom a, U$134.35 million gyina hɔ ma ɛka a wɔbɔ sɛ wɔmfa nni dwuma ntɛm no, a ɛno ankasa yɛ US $69.36 million sɛ ɛka a wɔbɔ sɛ wɔmfa nni dwuma ntɛm, US$58.49 million sɛ ɛka a wɔbɔ sɛ wɔmfa nni dwuma, US$66.46 sɛ ɛka a wɔbɔ sɛ wɔmfa nni dwuma ɛna US$32,448 sɛ ɛka a wɔbɔ sɛ wɔmfa nni dwuma ɛna US$32,448 sɛ ɛka a wɔbɔ sɛ wɔmfa nkora nneɛma so na wɔ
Asɛnnibea no nso de US$614,353.86 hyɛɛ ɔman no sɛ ɛka a asɛnnibea no bɔɔ Ghana sɛ ɛyɛ US$ ɔpepem mmiɛnsa ɛka a GPGC bɔɔ wɔ asɛnni no mu.
Asɛnnibea no gyinaesi no mu nsɛntitiriw no bi ne nokwasɛm a ɛyɛ sɛ Ahenkora Boayikuw a ɛhyɛɛ wɔn nkuran sɛ wɔntwa nhyehyɛe no mu no nni nnyinasoɔ a ɛbɛma wɔagye atom sɛ GPGC no bɛyɛ dɔla ɔpepem aduosia pɛ wɔ ɛka a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔtɔ no ntɛm no mu.
Bere a asɛnnibea no reyi Ghana asɛm no afi hɔ no, ɛyɛɛ nhyehyɛeɛ sɛ wɔbɛtwa nhyehyɛeɛ no mu, na ɛkyerɛɛ sɛ adanseɛ a ɛwɔ anim no kyerɛ sɛ “GPGC wɔ tumi krataa a ɔde bɛsi ɛpo fitaa a Kpone-Katamanso Mantam Nhyiamu a ɛbaa so wɔ August 15, 2017 no.”
“ GOG [Aban no) ntumi nhyɛɛ mmara biara, a Energy Commission Act ka ho a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde tumi krataa foforɔ biara a ɛbɛma wɔasisi adan ka ho”
“Sɛnea kyerɛwtohɔ no kyerɛ seesei no, ɛda adi sɛ sɛnea na Oduruyɛfo Ahenkorah [ Energy Commission Expanyin saa bere no) reyɛ akwanside foforo a ɔhyɛɛ GPGC sɛ ɔnhwehwɛ tumi krataa a ɔde bɛma wɔn wɔ bere tiaa mu wɔ November 2017 mu no, anyinam ahoɔden soafoɔ bɛpɛ sɛ Ghana Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no pene gyinaeɛ a ɛbɛma wɔatwa EPA ne PPA ahodoɔ foforɔ a ɛgyina PPA Boayikuo a Ɔbenfo Ahenkorah kaa ho asɛm no so.”
Wɔ Britain mmara ase no, na aban no wɔ nnafua 28 a ɔde bɛkasa atia asɛnnibea no gyinaesi. Nanso, na ɔda hɔ nnansa pɛ a ɔde bɛkɔ asɛnnibea akɔpɛ bere tenten a ɔde bɛma no.
Omnia Strategy a ɛyɛ Britain mmaranim adwuma no de asɛm no too dwa sɛ ɔntrɛw mu na ɔsrɛɛ no nnafua 56—bu mmɔdenbɔ mmere no mmɔho mmienu.
Nanso, asɛnnibea no yɛɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛtɔ so mmienu wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmienu ne aduonu mmien
Mmara adwumakuo a ɛdaa ne ho adi sɛ ɔno nko ara ne amanaman ntam mmara adwumakuo a wahyira ne ho so wɔ wiase no kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɔtemmuafoɔ Panin foforɔ, Godfred Yeboah Dame, kaa ntam wɔ March da a ɛtɔ so nnum mu, na nnafua du akyi no, adwumakuo no nyaa akwankyerɛ sɛ ɔnni Ghana ananmu.
Nanso bere a asɛnnibea no rebu atɛn wɔ asɛm no ho wɔ Ayɛwohomumɔ bosome da a ɛtɔ so aduonu baako wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu no, na asɛnnibea no mpene so.
Ɔtemmufoɔ panin no, Ɔtemmufo Butcher annyae.
Ɔtemmufoɔ no kaa sɛ akyɛdeɛ a aban no de too dwa no yɛ “ɛho hia paa” efisɛ n’adesrɛdeɛ a ɔde too dwa sɛ wɔntoa so mmienu no baeɛ nnafua 38 wɔ mmara nhyehyɛeɛ no akyi ne nnafua 27 wɔ bere a ɛdi kan a wɔde too dwa no akyi.
Ɔkae sɛ sika kɛseɛ a wɔde kɔɔ asɛnnibea no nnyinasoɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde kɔ asɛnnibea mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmmubea no gyina so.
Ɔtemmufoɔ no kaa sɛ, “Yei a ɛyɛ sɛ wɔanka Aban Kwaadubɔfoɔ no ntam kɔsii March 5 no nkyerɛ sɛ aban no ntumi nyɛ ho biribi saa berɛ no.
Nea Ɛde Asɛm no Bae
Amanaman Ntam Asɛnnibea a ɛhwɛ Arbitration so wɔ January 2021 mu no bɔɔ ka dɔla ɔpepem aduasa ne dɔla ɔpepem aduasa maa Ghana Aban wɔ GC GP nhyehyɛe a wɔatwa mu no ho.
Kan Anyinam Ahoɔden Soafoɔ Boakye Agyarko na ɔtwaa saa nhyehyɛeɛ no mu sɛ ɛyɛ anyinam ahoɔden ho nhyehyɛeɛ foforɔ a NPP de too dwa sɛ ɔman no nhia saa anyinam ahoɔden ho nhyehyɛeɛ no.
Atɛn a Amanaman Ntam Asɛnnibea a ɛhwɛ Arbitration so no bui no hyɛɛ Ghana aban no sɛ ɔntua “GPGC ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔtɔ ne ɛboɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ
Na ɛsɛ sɛ Ghana Aban no nso tua GPGC sika a ɛyɛ “US$ 309,877.74 wɔ ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ Arbitration no ho, ɛne US$ 3,000,000 wɔ GPGC mmara mu nnyinasoɔ ne ɛka ne ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ ne dansefo a ɔwɔ nimdeɛ no ho, ɛne ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ US$ 3,309,877.74 wɔ ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ US dollars mmiɛnsa a wɔde hyɛɛ mu no ho.”
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔaguare abofra bi wɔ Sawaba wɔ Kumase wɔ Wukuada anwummere nsu a ɛtɔɔ wɔ Asante mantam mu ahenkuro no akyi.
Ná abofra no ne n’awofo de sakre abiɛsa na ɛretu kwan bere a wɔde wɔn ho kɔhyɛɛ nsuyiri bi mu maa sakre abiɛsa no twaam no.
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ kyerɛ no, nnipa a wɔte mpɔtam hɔ no tu kɔe sɛ wɔrekɔbɔ awofo no ho ban nanso wɔantumi anhu abofra no bere a nsu yiri faa no kɔe no.
“Wɔanhu abofra a wɔaguare no amu no. Awofo no mfa no ntɛm koraa. Sɛ osu tɔ a, ɛyɛ den sɛ wɔbɛfa Sawaba kwan no so. Nsuyiri no yiri ma yennim nea enti a sakre sotefo no bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛfa ɔkwan a ɛmaa abofra a wadi kan no wui no so”
Amanneɛbɔ afoforo nso kyerɛ sɛ Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo a na ofi Apueɛ Mantam mu reba no bataa nsuyiri no ho.
Polisifo abɔ obi a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔyɛ dwowtwafo a wagye dimmɔne, Iddrisu Adams din ne Koomi, a Asante Mantam mu Polisifo Panyin kyeree no wɔ korɔnbɔ ho mpɛn pii no tuo sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛma wagyae mmofra sohwɛ.
Nea wɔbɔɔ no sobo no wɔ ahyɛde no din mu, na wɔkyeree no wɔ June 22, 2021 mu denam polisifo dwumadie soronko bi so.
Wɔ June 23 wɔ 2021 mu no, wɔde no kɔɔ mmeae bi a ɔtoo ne din sɛ, sɛ ɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ obeguan a, ɔde ne nneɛma sie. Polisifo no yɛɛ ntɛm de tuo kyerɛɛ no.
Wɔde onipa a wɔbɔɔ no sobo no kɔɔ St. Martins Ayaresabea, baabi a wobuu no kumfɔ.
Polisifoɔ a woyii wɔn adi no kyerɛɛ sɛ wɔrehwɛ n’akyidifoɔ a wɔtu wɔn fo sɛ wɔmfa wɔn ho nhyɛ mu denam kɔmputa so kɔ Polisifoɔ Adwumayɛbea a ɛbɛn hɔ no.
Polisifoɔ no nso hyɛɛ ɔmanfoɔ bɔ sɛ wɔbɛtwe wɔn ho afi nsɛmmɔnedi ho na wɔako atia nsɛmmɔnedi, na wɔka kyerɛɛ ɔmanfoɔ sɛ wɔmmoa wɔn.
Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Ɔman Ahobammɔ so, Albert Kan Dapaah ada nsɛntitiriw bi a ɛfa kan Asante Mantam Mu Ahobammɔ Soafoɔ panin DCOP Opare-Addo a ɔyɛ Ɔman Ahobammɔ adwuma no ho adi.
Sɛdeɛ Kan Dapaah kyerɛ no, akwantuo no ho behiaeɛ berɛ a wɔbɔɔ mmɔden mpɛn pii sɛ wɔbɛma banbɔ Kwankyerɛfoɔ no agyae adwuma no, berɛ a ne dwumadi no baa awieɛ no, anyɛ yie.
Sɛnkyerɛwfoɔ a wɔapam no no ka kyerɛɛ Starr News sɛ NPP asoeɛ mufoɔ a wɔyɛ aniferefoɔ a wɔfrɛ wɔn Delta Force na wɔtow hyɛɛ no so sɛ wanni wɔn bɔhyɛ so wɔ ɔmantam no mu.
Nanso berɛ a ɔman bammɔ soafoɔ rebua nsɛmmisa a ɛwɔ South Dayi Mmarahyɛbɛdwani Roc Jackson-Nelson Dafeamekpo bisaeɛ no, ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ mmarima a wɔsomaa wɔn no yɛ ɔman bammɔ adwuma.
Nanso wankyerɛ nea enti a wɔmaa Owura Opare-Addo dwumadi no baa awiei sɛ ɔnhyɛ sɛ wɔmfa atumisɛm nni dwuma wɔ tebea no mu.
“Ɔno [ Opare-Addo yɛɛ nhyehyɛeɛ mfeɛ abiɛsa sɛ ɔbɛsom sɛ Asante mantam mu bammɔ adwumayɛfoɔ berɛ a wɔyɛɛ mfeɛ abien nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛfii aseɛ wɔ January da a ɛtɔ so nnum, 2018 no. Ne dwumadi foforɔ no fii aseɛ January da a ɛtɔ so dunsia wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu.
“H bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ ne dwumadi no baa awiei wɔ February 19, 2021, ɔman bammɔ nsɛm ho dwumayɛni. Bere a wɔde ne nhyehyɛe no baa awiei no, DCOP Opare-Addo tuaa hokwan a ɔwɔ sɛ ɔde yɛ ne dwumadi krataa no. Ɛno akyi no, ɔsom adwuma a wɔde too nsa frɛɛ no, Col Francis Arthur ( fatd) sɛ Asante mantam bammɔ nsɛm ho dwumayɛni foforo no. Aban no abɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛkwati ntua a Burkinabe asraafo de ba Ghana so bere a wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔresi asraafo atrae wɔ Bawku sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ahobammɔ bɛkɔ so wɔ ɔman no fã hɔ no
Amanneɛbɔ a Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo de too dwa no baa dapɛn biako pɛ akyi bere a wɔhyɛɛ bammɔ adwumayɛkuo ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ Burkina Faso sɛ wɔbɛtow ahyɛ wɔn so no.
Ná ɔrekasa wɔ nhyiamu bi a ɔne Bawku Naba yɛe sɛ ɔde n’akwantuo no bɛba awieeɛ wɔ Apueɛ Mantam mu.
“Sɛ wo mantam no bɛn Burkina Faso a, ɛda adi sɛ wɔde wɔn ani asi awudifoɔ ne nsɛmmɔnedifoɔ a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔsɛe yɛn asetra na wɔbɔ yɛn hu wɔ Ghana yi so.”
Ɔtoaa so”Bawku Naba, wunim akwan a aban nam so rehyɛ ahobammɔ nnwuma a ɛwɔ ha no den na wabɔ yɛn ho ban afi amumɔyɛfo ntua a efi Burkina Faso no ho.
“Na ɛyɛ me anigye sɛ mɛka akyerɛ mo sɛ yɛbɛhyehyɛ banbɔ wɔ ha na atumi adi amumɔyɛsɛm ho dwuma.”
Ne nyinaa mu no, Bawku Naba a ɔno nso yɛ Kusaug Atetesɛm Bagua panin, Asigiri Abugrago Azoka II kaa sɛ, Kusaug Atetesɛm Mantam mu Ahene ne Nnipa, na nokwarem no, Ghanafoɔ nyinaa ani sɔ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɔmanpanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo-Addo ayɛ no.
Ɔmampanyin Akufo-Addo de anigye rehyɛ Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo anuonyam wɔ nkonim a wadi wɔ amanyɔkuo mu, “wɔde Ghana nkrabea ahyɛ mo nsa mfeɛ anan a ɛtɔ so anan no,” ɔka kyerɛɛ Ɔmanpanin no sɛ “ Moayɛ adwumaden sɛ mubenya saa gyinabea a ɛyɛ anibereɛ no. Me yam a anka moanya Onyankopɔn nhyira wɔ nyansa ne akwahosan pa mu na moatumi ayɛ mo nhyehyɛeɛ no.”

“Nnipa a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no mu ɔha mu nkyem 55 na wɔka sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wotu kɔ ɔman foforo so, na wɔn mu ɔha mu nkyem 11 na wɔbɛkɔ ɔman no mu anaasɛ wɔbɛkɔ akɔ. Nnipa a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no mu fã kɛse no ara twee adwene sii adidibea pa, nhomasua ne asetra pa so sɛ nteaseɛ nti a ɛbɛma wɔafi ɔman no mu bere a hokwan wɔ hɔ.”
Ɛdefa sɛ ebia wɔwɔ anidasoɔ wɔ ɔman no daakye ho no, nhwehwɛmu no kaa sɛ: “Nnipa a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no mu bɛyɛ ɔha mu nkyem aduasa na wɔka sɛ wɔwɔ anidasoɔ wɔ Ghana wɔ mfeɛ aduonu a ɛreba no mu. Nnipa bɛboro du mu nkyem aduonu baanu na wɔhu ɔman no daakye sɛ ɛyɛ hu. Nhomasua ne hokwan ahodoɔ ho no, nhwehwɛmu no kaa sɛ: “Mmofra no mu fã kyerɛ sɛ wɔwɔ anidasoɔ. National Democratic Congress abɔ Ɔtemmufo Panyin Kwasi Anin - Yeboah soboɔ sɛ n’adesrɛ a ɔde kɔɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ Panin, Dominic Ayine anim no yɛ mmɔden a ɔbɔ sɛ ɔbɛbrɛ kasa mu ahofadi ase.
Wɔbɔɔ Dr. Ayine amanneɛ sɛ ɔkae sɛ Asɛnnibea Kunini no amfa ɔkwan a wɔfa so di asɛm no anyɛ adwuma. Wogye di nso sɛ ɛhaw no wɔ abisadeɛ a wɔn a wɔde wɔn kɔɔ asɛnnibea hɔ daa no ho.
Ɔkaa asɛm no wɔ dwumadie bi a Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Democratic Development (CDD) ne KNUST na ɛyɛeɛ ase.
Asɛm a Ɔtemmufo Panyin no de too dwa no hyɛɛ GLC no nkuran sɛ ɔnhwehwɛ mmaranimfoɔ no nsɛm mu na ɔmfa asotweɛ a ɛho hia no nni dwuma.
Bere a ɔrekasa akyerɛ Nsɛntwerɛfoɔ Nhyiamu Dwoda no, NDC Kyerɛwfoɔ panin, Johnson Asiedu Nketia kɔɔ Ɔtemmufoɔ Panin anim sɛ ɔmfa adesrɛ nto Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a ɔwɔ Bolgatanga Apueɛ no so.
“Sɛ ɔmanfoɔ de wɔn werɛ hyɛ asɛnni bagua mu a, ɛnsɛ sɛ ɛhyɛ yɛn. Mpɛn ahe na woate sɛ asɛnnibea bi aka akyerɛ obi sɛ mɛbu atɛn nanso merebɔ wo kɔkɔ sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ woka ho asɛm?” Owura Asiedu Nketia a wagye din sɛnea Ɔsahene Mosquito kaeɛ.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ, “Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie te sɛ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie anaa ɔpanyin nyɛ adeɛ a ɛsen ɔkasatia. Yɛn mmara ne amanyɔ mmara bɔ atɛntrenee mu ahofadi ho ban, na ɛnyɛ ɔtemmufo nyansa. Adwene a ɛne sɛ atɛntrenee nni ahohora no yɛ nsusuwii hunu a yɛrentumi nnyina ano.”
Owura Asiedu Nketia nso bɔɔ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no soboɔ sɛ ɔde n’ani asi NDC mmaranimfoɔ so na ɔfrɛɛ no sɛ ɔnnyae abayifoɔ hwehwɛ.
“Ɛnyɛ nwonwa sɛ ɛkame ayɛ sɛ mmaranimfoɔ a Ɔtemmufoɔ Panin, Kwasi Anin Yeboah de wɔn ho kɔbɔɔ Mmarahyɛ Bagua no nteɛso boayikuo ho nnansa yi no nyinaa de wɔn ho kɔbɔɔ NDC no. Dɛn na Ɔtemmufo Panyin no ani gye ho sɛ ɔbɛtwe NDC mmaranimfoɔ aso na wayɛ krado paa sɛ ɔbɛyɛ biribi a ɛho nhia atia wɔn”
Ghana abɛyɛ ɔman a ɛtɔ so mmienu a ɛpɛ asomdwoe paa wɔ Afrika. Afe 2021 mu no, Asoeɛ a Ɛhwɛ Sikasɛm ne Asomdwoe Ho Nsɛm So (IEP) de amanneɛbɔ a ɛfa wiase nyinaa Asomdwoeɛ Index ho too dwa.
Wiase Nyinaa Asomdwoeɛ Kyerɛwtohɔ no ne wiase nyinaa asomdwoeɛ ho nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛsen biara. Kyerɛwtohɔ no kyerɛ sɛ amantam ne nsasesin 163 na wɔn ankasa pɛ asomdwoeɛ. Kyerɛwtohɔ yi kyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ akontaabu mu nhwehwɛmu a ɛkɔ akyiri paa a ɛfa asomdwoeɛ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ wiase nyinaa, ɛso mfasoɔ a ɛwɔ so wɔ sikasɛm mu, ne sɛnea ɛbɛma nnipa anya asomdwoeɛ.
Nnansa yi, Ghana na ɔtɔ so 38 wɔ wiase no mu wɔ aman 163 a wɔyɛɛ mu nhwehwɛmu no mu. Ghana nyaa 1.715 a ɛgyina hɔ ma nkɔanim mmienu wɔ ɔman no gyinabea dedaw no mu.
Mauritius a ɛyɛ ɔman a ɛpɛ asomdwoe sen biara wɔ Afrika no na ɛto so 28 wɔ wiase nyinaa, na Botswana na ɛto so abiɛsa wɔ Afrika ne nea ɛto so 41 wɔ wiase nyinaa. Nigeria na ɛto so 146 wɔ wiase nyinaa wɔ Togo, Uganda, Kenya, The Republic of Congo ne Cameroon akyi.
Iceland da so ara yɛ ɔman a ɛwɔ asomdwoe sen biara wɔ wiase yi mu, ɛyɛ gyinabea a ɛwɔ fi afe 2008 mu. New Zealand, Denmark, Portugal, ne Slovenia na abɛka ho.
Afghanistan ne ɔman a asomdwoe nnim koraa wɔ wiase afe a ɛto so anan, na Yemen, Syria, South Sudan, ne Iraq na edii hɔ. Burkina Faso kyerɛɛ sɛnea wiase Asomdwoe Akontaabu no sɛee koraa wɔ afe 2021 mu.
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ no kyerɛ no, nnipa a wɔwɔ Afrika Sahara Anafo fam no mu fã hyiaa basabasayɛ nnansa yi. Wɔn a wɔte Namibia no hyiaa basabasayɛ a ɛsen biara wɔ wiase no mu ɔha mu nkyem 6.
South Sudan da so ara yɛ ɔman a asomdwoe nnim koraa wɔ ɔmantam no mu ne wiase aman a asomdwoe nnim koraa no mu biako, ɛmfa ho sɛ wɔanya nkɔanim wɔ asomdwoe mu wɔ afe 2021 mu no.
Asomdwoe a ɛsɛee kɛse wɔ ɔmantam no mu sii Burkina Faso. Na eyi nso yɛ ɔman biara mu nsakrae a ɛsen biara. Aban no gyinaesi a ɛne sɛ ɔde ntoboa bɛma akuw a wɔnyɛ asraafo a wɔnyɛ asraafo wɔ ɔko a ɔreko atia atuatewfo no na ɛmaa atuatew no kɔɔ so.
Amanneɛbɔ no sii so dua sɛ ɔmanko kɔɔ soro ɔha mu nkyem 10 wɔ wiase nyinaa, a efi komayare yare no. Nnipa 14,871 na wɔyɛɛ basabasa, wɔyɛɛ ɔsɔretia ne basabasayɛ ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ wiase nyinaa wɔ 2020 mu.
Amanneɛbɔ no kyerɛ sɛ Covid yɛ “adeɛ foforɔ” wɔ amanyɔsɛm mu basabasayɛ ne ɔmanko a ɛbɛba daakye no mu. Ɛkaa sɛ basabasayɛ a ɛbɛba daakye no bɛkɔ so ntɛmntɛm na ɛbɛma sikasɛm ayɛ yie. Aman a ɛka nnɔɔso na asomdwoeɛ papa biara nni hɔ no, ɛbɛkɔ so ayɛ yie ntɛm.
Eyi nyinaa akyi no, nnipa baanan biara mu baasa a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa te nka sɛ wɔwɔ ahobammɔ nnɛ sen mfe anum a atwam no. Nneɛma bi a ɛkyerɛ sɛ basabasayɛ anya nkɔanim kɛse fi bere a akontaabu no fii ase no, na aman 123 ahu sɛ awudi dodow so atew fi afe 2008 mu.
Index no daa no adi nso sɛ, sɛ wɔkyekyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a, wiase asomdwoe sɛee ɔha biara mu 0.07 wɔ 2021 Wiase Asomdwoe Index no mu. Ɛwom sɛ ɛyɛ ɔhaw ketewaa bi de, nanso eyi ne mfe 13 a atwam ni a wiase asomdwoe asɛe no mpɛn akron.
Amanneɛbɔ no de kaa ho sɛ, afe a etwaam no, aman 87 yɛɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ asomdwoeɛ mu ho kyerɛwtohɔ, na aman 73 nso yɛɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ wɔn nkɔsoɔ mu. Aman mmiɛnsa nso yɛɛ nsakraeɛ biara wɔ wɔn nkɔsoɔ mu. Middle East ne North Africa (MENA) mantam no da so ara yɛ baabi a asomdwoeɛ nnim koraa wɔ wiase. Aman nnum a asomdwoe nnim koraa wɔ wiase no mu baasa na ɛwɔ hɔ. Nanso ɛyɛ nkɔsoɔanimɛ a ɛsen biara wɔ afe a atwam no mu.
“ Europe ne beae a asomdwoe wɔ sen biara wɔ wiase. Aman du a asomdwoe wɔ hɔ sen biara no mu baawɔtwe na ɛwɔ hɔ, na ɔman biara nni hɔ a ɛwɔ Europa a ɛka ho sen biara.”
Ɔmanpanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akufo-Addo ahyɛ Ghanafoɔ bɔ sɛ wɔbɛnya nkɔsoɔ wɔ wɔn asetena mu wɔ ne man ase.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ mfeɛ anan a ɛdi hɔ no bɛnya Ghanani mmɔborɔni no asetena so nkɛntɛnso pa.
“M'adwenem yɛ me nãã sɛ mfeɛ anan a ɛbɛdi hɔ no bɛma Ghana manfoɔ asetra atu mpɔn,” ɔmampanyin-mampanyin no maa mmuaeɛ yi berɛ a ɔkɔɔ Nigeria no berɛ a ɔdii nkonim wɔ ɔmampanyin abatoɔ mu.
Owura Akufo-Addo rekasa akyerɛ Imo Mantam mu panin a ɔwɔ Nigeria Owelle Rochas Anayo Okorocha, Dwoada de kaa ho sɛ: “Ghanani sikasɛm asɛe wɔ mfeɛ abiɛsa anaa anan a atwa mu yi mu nanso yɛde nteɛsoɔ a ɛyɛ den ne nhyehyɛeɛ ahodoɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ ma ɔman no nya nkɔsoɔ.
Ɔmampanyin-panyin a ɔbɔɔ Incumbent Ɔmampanyin, John Dramani Mahama wɔ ɔmampanyin abatoɔ a ɛbaa awiei nnansa yi ara mu no abɛsra Nigeria, faako a ɔne ɔmampanyin a ɔyɛ fango adwuma, Muhammudu Buhari bɛbɔ nkɔmmɔ.
Owura Akufo-Addo nso hyɛɛ Imo Mantam mu amrado no bɔ sɛ wɔbɛhyɛ abusuabɔ a ɛda Afrika Atɔe fam aman abien ntam no mu den wɔ ne mmarahyɛ ase.
“Yɛn ani sɔ abusuabɔ a ɛda aman abien no ntam no. Ɛho hia sɛ abusuabɔ a ɛte saa da yɛn nkurɔfo ne yɛn akannifo ntam. Wɔma yɛn nkurɔfo nya awerɛhyem sɛ yɛrebɔ mmɔden sɛ yebedi wɔn haw ahorow ho dwuma na yɛaboa wɔn ma wɔanya nkɔso wɔ wɔn asetra mu”
Ɔmanpanin John Dramani Mahama asi Joseph Whittal so dua sɛ ɔyɛ Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ ne Atɛntrenee so (CHRAJ)
Wɔkaa Owura Whittal ntam wɔ nhyiamu tiawa bi ase wɔ Flagstaff House Benada awia.
Owura Whittal na ɔdi CHRAJ anim fi berɛ a Ɔmanpanin no yii Lauretta Vivian lamptey a ɔmaa ɔman no sikasɛm yɛɛ basaa.
Ɔmanpanin apaw Awuraa Josephine Nkrumah sɛ National Commission for Civic Education (NCCE) panin.
Awuraa Nkrumah a na ɔyɛ aban nanmusini abadiakyire abɛsi Owurayere Charlotte Osei ananmu no wdho abɛyɛ ɔman no Abatoɔ Asoeɛ a Ɔmanpanin de too dwa wɔ July afe a etwaam no mu panin.
Wɔpaw NPP kannifo Nana Addo Dankwa Akufo-Addo akyi adapɛn kakraa bi no.
Wɔbɛka ɔmampanyin no ntam January 7, 2017
GN Health Insurance Company Ltd, Groupe Nduom nnwumakuo 75 no mu baako afi aseɛ reyɛ Ambulance Services wɔ Ghana.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nnwuma afoforo a ɛbɛma wɔanya ayaresa a egye ntɛmpɛ ne ayarehwɛ a egye ntɛmpɛ ama wɔn a wɔn yare mu yɛ den.
GN Apɔmuden Ambulance Asoeɛ no nso de nnɔnhwerew 24 bɛhwɛ ayaresa ne amanehunu a ɛfa tebea a egye ntɛmpɛ ne nsɛm a wɔde gye nsɛm mu ho.
GN Apɔmuden Asoeɛ no guamtrani Issah Adam kaa sɛ, “ha nso Ɔmanpanin ne panin a ɔda Groupe Nduom ano, Dr. Papa Kwesi Nduom ne Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire, Owurayere Yvonne Nduom ne Akwankyerɛfoɔ no nyinaa ayɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛma Adwumakuo no mu adwumayɛfoɔ anya nkɔsoɔ.
Ɔkaa apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔreboaboa wɔn ano no ho asɛm sɛ “ei nso yɛ ade titiriw wɔ Groupe Nduom nhyehyɛeɛ no mu. Nea ɛka ayaresa adwuma a wɔde ma kwa ho no, wɔde Ambulance Ɔsom adwuma yi reka ho sɛ wɔbɛwie ayaresa Dwumadie nhyehyɛeɛ no ama adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ Nkran ne Mfinimfini Mantam mu no mfasoɔ.”
Nnipa a wowuwu wɔ Ghana no bɛboro ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem ɔha mu nkyem
“GN Apɔmuden bɛhwɛ ama yɛatete EMTs (Emergency Medical Technicians) ne Ambulance Drivers a wɔatete wɔn yiye na wɔahu nea wɔnyɛ wɔ tebea a egye ntɛmpɛ mu.
“Fard 350 ambulance no wɔ nnwinnade ne nneɛma a ɛho hia a wɔde bɛhwɛ ayarefo ansa na wɔakɔ ayaresabea. Yɛsrɛ wo hyɛ no nsow sɛ eyinom nyɛ ambulance a wɔde bɛhwɛ wɔn a wɔakɔ ayaresabea ansa na wɔakɔ ayaresabea kɛkɛ”
Ayaresabea no wɔ nnwinnade a ɛyɛ den paa a wɔde hwɛ wɔn a wɔwɔ ayaresabea ansa na wɔayɛ wɔn oprehyɛn. Wɔwɔ nnwinnade a ehia na wɔde adi tebea ahorow a egye ntɛmpɛ ho dwuma, efi mfiri a wɔde boa wɔn a wɔhome ne mfiri a wɔde dwudwo ɔyare mmoawa ano kosi nneɛma a ɛnyɛ den te sɛ kyɛnsee ne nsanyare ano aduru so.
Aban ahyɛ bɔ sɛ ɔbɛte ɛka a wɔbɔ sɛ wɔde bɛsa wɔn a wɔapirapira Yawda mframa bɔne a ɛpaee wɔ La no.
Nnipa baasia na wɔagye atom sɛ wɔawuwu wɔ mframa bɔne a ɛpaee wɔ baabi a ɛbɛn Trade Fair Centre a ɛwɔ Nkran no mu nanso nnipa bɛboro 20 na wɔapirapira wɔ akwan horow so.
Akwahosan Soafoɔ Alex Segbefia a ɔkɔsraa wɔn a wɔyɛɛ wɔn ayayadeɛ wɔ La General, Police ne Military ayaresabea 37 a wɔhwɛɛ wɔn a wɔyɛɛ wɔn ayayadeɛ wɔ hɔ no kamfoo nnuruyɛfoɔ sɛ wɔahwɛ wɔn a wɔyɛɛ wɔn ayayadeɛ.
“Mampanyin ada no adi pefee sɛ ɔman no bɛkata ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔn a wɔhyehyee wɔn wɔ saa asɛm yi mu no nyinaa so, enti yɛama ɛda adi pefee akyerɛ mpanyimfoɔ panin a ɔhwɛ ayarefoɔ yi so no sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhyehyɛ ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so ahwɛ wɔn no nyinaa ntɛm.
“Sɛnea wunim wɔ wɔn a wɔhyehye wɔn fam no, ɛho hia sɛ woguare daa, sesa w’ahosiesie, na wode gu nnuru a ekum yare mmoawa ne ɛyawdifo a wɔn ho yɛ den kɛse so, enti ɛsɛ sɛ ɔyarefo biara bɔ ka. Ɛsɛ sɛ wode adwumayɛfo foforo kɔ ayaresabea ha na wɔyɛ eyi wɔ sraadi mu”
Saa berɛ yi mu no, Ɔmanpanin John Dramani Mahama akɔ Ghanafoɔ nkyɛn sɛ wɔmmɔ mpaeɛ mma wɔn a pɛtroɔ a ɛtɔɔ wɔn so wɔ Yawda no.
Wɔ Intanɛt so dwumadie bi mu Fida no, ɔmampanyin a ɔpɛ nnipa no de ne ho kɔhyɛɛ ɔfasu a ɛwɔ Intanɛt so no mu sɛ ɔrekɔkyekye wɔn a wɔrehu amane no werɛ.
“M'awerɛkyekyeɛ ma mmusua a wɔn a wɔhwee wɔn wɔ mframa bɔne a ɛpaee nnɛra no mu no; yɛnkɔ so mmɔ mpaeɛ mma wɔn a wɔapirapira.”
Mframa bɔne adwumayɛbea bi a ɛbɛn Ghana International Trade Fair Centre a ɛwɔ Nkran no atopae ama nnipa baanum ahyehye wɔn awu.
Sɛnea obi a ɔde n’ani hui kyerɛ no, ogya no nso kaa ɔman dwumadibea ne aguadibea no afã bi.
Sɛnea Veronica Koomson kyerɛ no, ambulance ne odumgya adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ hɔ no bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛko atia ogya a ano yɛ den a ɛde nnipa a wɔrehuruhuruw no.
“Gya no redɛw na yɛreyɛ nea yɛbɛtumi biara sɛ yɛbɛdum no. Asraafoɔ a wɔyɛ odumgyafoɔ no nso wɔ ha na wɔreyɛ nea wɔbɛtumi biara sɛ wɔbɛma ogya yi adum,” Ghana Ɔman Ogya Adwuma kasamafoɔ, Prince Billy-Anaglatey ka kyerɛɛ Starr News’ Kemini Amanor Yawda.
Koomson kaa sɛ mframa gyinabea foforo a ɛbɛn baabi a ɛredɛw no, sɛ odumgyafo no anyɛ nhyehyɛe a wɔde bɛbɔ tebea no ho ban a, ɛda adi sɛ ɛbɛkɔ ogya mu.
Nanso Billy-Anaglatey kae sɛ ɔrentumi nkyerɛ sɛ obi awu, na ɔde kaa ho sɛ, “nnɛ deɛ ehia mo ne sɛ mubesiesie ogya no” sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛremfa ɔfoforɔ no ho.
Yennim nea ɛde ɔtopae no bae. Anyinam ahoɔden nhama ahorow nso sɔ gya wɔ beae hɔ.
Onipa biako awu wɔ akwanhyia a ɛyɛ hu a esii anadwo a etwa to wɔ Ekumfi Akoti a ɛwɔ Ekumfi mantam a ɛwɔ Mfinimfi Mantam mu no mu.
Nea wawu no yɛ Nigeriani a ɔhweree ne nkwa berɛ a lɔre a ɔreka no faa kwan mu na ogya tɔɔ mu no.
Ná lɔre a wɔde Cola nneɛma gu mu no nam kwan so fi Mankessim rekɔ Nigeria.
Sɛnea nnipa a wɔde wɔn ani hui kyerɛ no, kar no kɔhyɛɛ kwae bi a ɛbɛn hɔ mu bere a owufo no antumi anni ne ho so no.
Nanso, wɔn a wogyina hɔ no bɔɔ mmɔden gyee akwantufo baanu a na wɔwɔ kar no mu ansa na ogya retɔ mu no nkwa, na wɔhyew ofirikafo no ma owui amonom hɔ ara.
Mprempren wɔrehwɛ wɔn baanu no wɔ Cape Coast mantam ayaresabea.
Akyiri yi, Ghana Odumgya Adwumayɛfoɔ baa hɔ bɛhwɛɛ ɔtopaeɛ no.

Ahemfo bi a wɔwɔ Ga mpɔtam hɔ de nnawɔtwe ahyɛdeɛ a ɛbɛma wagyae n’ahengua.
Aban mpanyimfoɔ no bo afuw GP 760 Ɔhene no wɔ nsɛm a ɔkyerɛɛ wɔn ansa na wɔretow aba afe 2016 no ho.
Nii Ayibonte hyɛɛ bɔ sɛ sɛ ɔmampanyin John Mahama di nkogu wɔ ɔmampanyin abatoɔ no mu a ɔbɛyi n’ahengua no afi hɔ.
Nii Ayibonte ka kyerɛɛ ne manfoɔ ansa na wɔretow aba no sɛ akyinnye biara nni ho sɛ Mahama bɛdi nkonim wɔ abatowɔ no mu a ɛgyina adan ne nnwuma bebree so.
Nanso akraye bɔɔ Nkran Komapafoɔ panin a ɔwɔ Oak nsam berɛ a ɔde ne akongua too kyakya no.
Nii Ayibonte nkaa nea wabɔ ne tirim sɛ ɔbɛyɛ wɔ Nana Akufo-Addo nkonimdi kɛse no akyi no ho asɛm biara.
Ga Chiefs a ɔrehyɛ no sɛ ɔnkyere n’ahengua no nso adi yaw dedaw. Afei nso, wɔresɔre atia hokwan a ɔwɔ sɛ dimmɔne no.
Mmea mmienu wuiɛ na nnipa bɛboro 12 nso pirapiraeɛ berɛ a kar bi antumi ansi Daboya ne Busunu kwan a ɛwɔ Atifi Mantam mu no so na wɔde no kɔhyɛɛ nsuka mu Benada anwummere no, polisifoɔ agye atom.
Ná nnipa 14 na wɔde wɔn fi Sawla rekɔ Daboya akɔ Nkramofo ayeforohyia ase wɔ kar ketewa bi mu.
West Gonja mantam mu polisifo panyin, ASP Seidu Wemeh, kae sɛ bere a wɔde kar a ne nɔma yɛ AS 2304 - 15 kɔɔ kurow bi a ɛbɛn Daboya a ɛwɔ kwan mu mpofirim na ahohuru bere mu no, wɔde kar no kɔɔ nsuka bi mu kunkum nnipa baanu no amonom hɔ ara.
Wɔn a wowuwui no yɛ mmea mpanyimfo a wɔadi fi mfe 42 kosi 45.
Yennim nea ɛkɔfaa akwanhyia no baeɛ nanso sɛnea ASP Seidu kyerɛ no, polisifoɔ bɛtɔ wɔn bo ase ahwehwɛ sɛnea ofirikafoɔ no adwene teɛ ne sɛ nsa wom anaa.
Ɔkaa sɛ wɔde wɔn a wɔapirapira no mu fã kɛse no ara kɔɔ ɔmantam ayaresabea a ɛwɔ Tamale no, na wɔde biako pɛ na ɛhwɛɛ wɔn wɔ Damongo.
Akwanhyia a ɛkɔ so wɔ Daboya ne Busunu kwan so no ntaa nsi ɛmfa ho sɛ enye no.
Ɔmanfo apo amanneɛbɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ eyi ne bere a edi kan wɔ afe no mu a wɔayɛ akwanhyia ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ ɔkwan a wɔabu ani agu so no so.
Wɔka sɛ wɔnka akwanhyia dodow no ara ho asɛm.
Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ anyinam ahoɔden so, Dr Matthew Opoku Prempeh aka sɛ Aban no rebɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛma Ghana mfiridwuma atu mpɔn na wɔanya anyinam ahoɔden nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛdi mu te sɛ nuklea ne ahoɔden foforɔ.
Ɔkaa sɛ nnipa pii gye tom sɛ nuklea ahoɔden di dwuma titiriw bi wɔ anyinam ahoɔden a wɔsɛe no mu na ama mfiridwuma anya nkɔso ntɛmntɛm.
“Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ anyinam ahoɔden foforɔ yi bɛkɔ so anya nkɔanim kɛseɛ, nuklea ahoɔden yɛ adeɛ a ɛho hia paa wɔ nnɛyi anyinam ahoɔden mu, na ɛno nso ne adeɛ a ɛsen biara a ɛma anyinam ahoɔden a ɛwɔ mframa pa a wɔfrɛ no carbon no bɛyɛ ɔha mu nkyem 40”
Ɔtwee adwene sii Amanaman Ntam Anyinam Ahoɔden Asoeɛ amanneɛbɔ a ɛfa anyinam ahoɔden nhyehyɛe pa ho so sɛ, sɛ ɛnyɛ nuklea dwumadie a, anyinam ahoɔden nhyehyɛe pa a yɛbɛnya no bɛyɛ den kɛse, na ɛde mframa bɔne, ɛka ne ahobammɔ bɛba.
Dr. Opoku Prempeh kaa eyi ho asɛm wɔ ɔkasa bi a ɔkenkan maa no wɔ Stakeholders Nhyiamu a ɛfa Ghana Nuklea Ahoɔden Dwumadie a ɛwɔ Nkran no ho.
Asɛmti a ɛwɔ asɛmti yi ase ne sɛ: “Nuclear Energy Innovations: The Future Technologies for Clean Energy ne sɛnea wɔbɛsɛe Ghana anyinam ahoɔden nnwuma” no yɛɛ nhyiamu yi ho nhyehyɛe maa Ghana industries Fekuw (agi) ne Nuclear Power Ghana (NPG) yɛɛ biako.
Dr. Opoku Prempeh kae sɛ anyinam ahoɔden mfiri a wɔbɛdan akɔ mu no bɛsɛe nneɛma afoforo te sɛ akwantuo ne nneɛma a atwa yɛn ho ahyia ho fĩ.
“Wɔ Ghana anyinam ahoɔden mfidie, nneɛma boɔ a ɛkɔ so dɔɔso, nneɛma boɔ a ɛkɔ soro ma mfiridwuma, nneɛma boɔ a wotumi tɔ, nneɛma boɔ a wotumi de ho to so, ne nneɛma boɔ a wotumi de si pɛpɛɛpɛ ho gyinaeɛ no ama anyinam ahoɔden foforɔ a wɔde bɛyɛ adwuma.”
Ɔkaa sɛ, sɛ yesusuw nokwasɛm a ɛfa ɔman no ahoɔden, nneɛma bo, ne nneɛma afoforo a ɛfa ho, nuklea ahoɔden ho a, ebetumi ama yɛanya anyinam ahoɔden foforo a ɛho tew.
“Wɔ nuklea ahoɔden dwumadie foforɔ yi mu no, ɛnyɛ carbon anyinam ahoɔden a ɛwɔ fam nko na ɛbɛba, na mmom ɛbɛma yɛanya mfasoɔ kɛseɛ wɔ ne nyinasoɔ ne mfeɛ aduosia a ɛbɛba no mu.”
Ɔkaee sɛ wɔ afe 2007 mu no, kan Ɔmanpanin John Agyekum Kufuor teɛɛ boayikuo bi a Ɔbenfo Daniel Adzei-Bekoe na ɔhyehyɛ too hɔ sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ sɛ Ghana bɛtumi de nuklea ahoɔden ayɛ adwuma sɛ adeɛ foforɔ a wɔde bɛyɛ adwuma.
Na eyi yɛ bere a Ghana hyiaa anyinam ahoɔden ho nsɛnnennen no.
Ɔkaa sɛ, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ na ɔman no anyinam ahoɔden mfiridwuma anya nkɔanim no, aban ahodoɔ a ɛbaa ɛno akyi no aboa ama ɔman no anyinam ahoɔden ahobammɔ atu mpɔn na wɔde akwankyerɛ ne nneɛma ama nuklea ahoɔden dwumadie no.
Eyi ama NPG abɛyɛ Ghana nuklea dwumadibea a ɛdi kan no wura.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “NPG Boayikuo a ɛhyɛ Owura Fred Oware guamtenani ase no de asi wɔn ani so sɛ wɔbɛma wɔn nneɛma a ɛho hia a ɛbɛma wɔanya ahobammɔ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛfata wɔ nuklea akodeɛ ho nhyehyɛeɛ ne dwumadie a ɛtete saa mu wɔ ɔman no mu.
Sɛ anyinam ahoɔden ne nuklea ahoɔden da nkyɛn a, Ɔsoafoɔ no kaa sɛ, ɛbɛtumi ama wɔn a wɔde di dwuma wɔ ɔkwan a ɛkɔ akyiri so no anya ano aduru, na ɛbɛtumi ama wɔn a wɔde di dwuma wɔ nuklea ahoɔden mu te sɛ nuklea mfidie nketewa a wɔde di dwuma wɔ ɔkwan a ɛkɔ akyiri so no ayɛ nneɛma a wɔde di dwuma wɔ ɔkwan a ɛfata so.
Nuklea mfidie ama nnipa asetena atu mpɔn wɔ akwan pii so, na ɛreboa ama nneɛma akɔ so yie.”
"Nnuruyɛ, mfiridwuma ne kuayɛ mu mfiridwuma de nuklea mfidie redi dwuma wɔ wiase nyinaa, a Ghana ka ho.
Efi bere a wɔhyɛɛ ase bɛyɛ mfe anan a atwam ni no, tow a wotua wɔ mmosa ne nea wɔnnom nsa ho no anya nkɔanim kɛse.
Afe 2018 mu no, nnipa ɔpepem 28 kosi ɔpepem aduonu num a wɔhyehyɛɛ tow no dodow kɔɔ soro koduu ɔpepem 38.5 afe a edi hɔ no, na afe 2020 mu no, nnipa ɔpepem aduonu num a wɔhwɛɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛhyehyɛ tow no bɛyɛ ɔpepem aduɔwɔtwe num wɔ 2021 mu.
Ghana Revenue Authority (GRA) kae sɛ ɛne Ghana Food and Beverages Association (FABAG) ne wɔn a wɔyɛ nneɛma a ɛwɔ hɔ no reyɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ wɔbɛtua wɔn nneɛma a wɔde yɛ wɔn nneɛma wɔ baabi a wɔtɔn nneɛma no ho ka.
Ghanani nhomatintim adwumakuo, Buck Press ne ne yɔnko, DelaRue, a ɔyɛ Britain nhomatintim adwuma no, na ɛyɛ wɔn asɛyɛde sɛ wɔtwerɛ tow stampo ma GRA, na streamline Resources a ɛwɔ Tema Port no boa nnwumakuo a wɔnni tumi a wɔde bɛhyehyɛ stampo no ama ankorɛankorɛ biara.
Adwuma Kwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔhwɛ Excise Tow Stamp a ɛwɔ GRA, Owura Kwabena Apau Awuah Anto a ɔkaa eyi kyerɛɛ wɔn no kaa sɛ akwantuo no bɛte nneɛma mu amimdi ne korɔnbɔ so, faako a wɔn a wɔtɔn nneɛma ne wɔn a wɔyɛ nneɛma no bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔde stampo bɛtɔ nneɛma pɔtee bi nanso wɔde bɔɔ nneɛma a wɔmpene so ne adansedi krataa a efi Aduan ne Nnubɔne Asoeɛ (FDA) hɔ no.
Bere a Owura Anto rekasa wɔ beae a wotua tow wɔ Tema Port no, Yawda a etwaam no, ɔkae sɛ GRA panin ama wɔn a wɔtɔn nneɛma ne wɔn a wɔyɛ nneɛma no bɛyɛ 34 tumi krataa sɛ wɔn ankasa ntua wɔn nneɛma wɔ wɔn nnwuma mu. Guinness Ghana Limited ne Coca-Cola Bottling Adwumakuo no nso ka ho.
GGCL kuw a Ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ Panin, Owura Ato Afful na ɔdii wɔn anim no bi ne Daily Graphic samufoɔ, Owura Kobby Asmah; Ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ, Aguadifoɔ, Owura Franklin Sowa ne The Mirror samufoɔ, Awuraa Doreen Hammond.
Ná kuw no wɔ Tema sɛ wɔn ankasa bɛkyerɛ nkɔsoɔ wɔ towtua ho nhyehyɛeɛ kɛseɛ no mu na wɔne GRA ayɛ biako wɔ ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so anya nkɔanim wɔ saa nhyehyɛeɛ no mu.
Owura Anto kaa sɛ stamp nhyehyɛe a ɛyɛ anika yi bɛtew nneɛma a wɔde di dwuma ɔkwammɔne so na ama wɔatumi de nneɛma a ɛho tew nkutoo akɔ gua so ama ɔmanfo akwahosan ne ahobammɔ.
Saa ara nso na ɔkaeɛ sɛ nhyehyɛeɛ no bɛma wɔn a wɔtɔn nneɛma ne wɔn a wɔyɛ nneɛma no anya akatua a ɛfata, na ɛbɛma wɔn a wɔtɔn nneɛma ne wɔn a wɔyɛ nneɛma no anya akatua a ɛfata wɔ aguadi mu.
Owura Anto kae sɛ: “Nneɛma a yɛyɛ wɔ ha wɔ Tema adwumayɛbea ne adwumayɛbea afoforo 13 a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu baabiara a yɛwɔ adwumayɛbea a wɔtɔn nneɛma no ho nhia wɔn a wɔtɔn nneɛma no.”
Ɔkaa sɛ, wɔde nneɛma te sɛ stampo a wɔtɔ, nneɛma a wɔde yɛ adwuma, adwumayɛ, ɛka a wɔbɔ wɔ adwuma no ho ne nneɛma te sɛ nneɛma a wɔtwe nneɛma nketenkete no na ɛyɛɛ adwuma.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ bere a adwuma no fii ase afe 2018 no, aban no yɛɛ n'adwene sɛ ɔbɛma mfɛnsere bosome nsia sɛ ɔde stampo no bɛma kwa, nanso ɛno akɔ so abedu saa bere yi, enti ɛsɛ sɛ Asoafoɔ panin ahyɛdeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ mu no yɛ adwuma, na ɛkanyan wɔn ma wɔtua wɔn ka.
Owura Anto kae sɛ nhyehyɛeɛ no bɛkyerɛ sɛ GRA no bɛbɔ ka no nyinaa anaa ɛbɛyɛ ɛka a ɛda ɛne wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ mu no ntam.
“Wɔ aman te sɛ Kenya mu no, wɔn a wɔde nneɛma kɔ amannɔne no tua stampo no ho ka anaasɛ wɔde nneɛma no kɔ amannɔne kɔtɔn.
Ghana nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛfa tow gyegyeɛ nhyehyɛeɛ ho no de asɛyɛdeɛ a ɛwɔ wɔn a wɔde nneɛma kɔ amannɔne kɔtɔn anaa wɔn a wɔyɛ no ho no ato wɔn so.
Wɔ aman pii a wɔde nhyehyɛe a ɛte saa ara di dwuma mu no, mfiridwumayɛfoɔ wɔ adwumayɛbea ahodoɔ wɔ baabi a wɔyɛ adwuma no,” Owura Anto kaeɛ.
Ɛdefa nsɛnnennen a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ adwumayɛbea hɔ nnansa yi ara ho no, Owura Anto kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɛnyɛ wɔn a wɔtɔn nneɛma bebree nti na wɔyɛ Tema adwumayɛbea no, na mmom nnipa a wɔtɔn nneɛma bere ne bere mu nkutoo.
Nanso, ɔkaa sɛ, wɔn a wɔtɔn nneɛma bebree no, sɛ wɔbɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛkwati ɛka a wɔbɔɔ wɔ nneɛma no ho a, na wɔtaa de wɔn nneɛma no kɔ baabi a wɔtɔn nneɛma no, na ɛma wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase na wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase.
Saa ara nso na ɔkae sɛ, sɛ wɔsesa ɔsom adwuma sohwɛfo no adwene na wɔde stampo no yɛ adwuma wie a, na ɛma wɔtwentwɛn wɔn nan ase.
Nanso, mfiridwumayɛfo yɛɛ mfiri no ho adwuma sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi atwa stampo foforo no.
Wɔ ne nsɛm mu no, Owura Asmah ka kyerɛɛ GRA sɛ ɔnhyɛ nhomasua a ɛfa nhyehyɛeɛ ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu kena.
Ɔkaa sɛ, towtua ho nhomasua ho hia, efisɛ ɛbɛma nnipa nyinaa ahu sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ saa, na ɛbɛma nnipa ahu sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ saa bere tiaa bi.
Ɔkamfoo GRA mpanyimfoɔ ne ɔsom adwuma sohwɛfoɔ, Streamline Resources sɛ wɔyɛɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔde bedi nsɛnnennen no ho dwuma.
Ɔkaa sɛ GCGL no ne GRA no bɛyɛ biako ama wɔn adwene ayɛ kɛse, berɛ a wɔanya nhumu wɔ towtua ho nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛyɛ anika no mu.
“Megye di sɛ eyi ne bere a ɛfata ma GCGL ne GRA sɛ wɔbɛyɛ biako a ɛbɛma ɔmanfo ani agye, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛbɛtɔ biribi afi ɔmanfoɔ hɔ” Owura Asmah kaeɛ.

Thomas Amoani a wadi mfeɛ 19 a wawie Adeiso Presbyterian High School a Ghana Scholarships Kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ de ne nhomasua nyinaa maa no no akyerɛ anisɔ ama Ɔmanpanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo Addo.
Thomas Amoani a ɔwɔ A’s baawɔtwe wɔ afe a etwaam no West Africa Secondary School Examination mu no, ntɛm ara na wɔde nhomasua krataa maa no sɛ ɔmmɛyɛ adesua wɔ Brunel Sukuupɔn a agye din wɔ London no mu bere a wɔde akwankyerɛ maa Owura Kingsley Agyemang a ɔyɛ Ɔkyerɛwfo no.
Abarimaa a wadi mfeɛ 19 a ɔwɔ Asuaba a ɛbɛn Adeiso a ɔmmɔɔ mmɔden paa no bɛyɛ sikasɛm ne sikasɛm mu nhwehwɛmu wɔ ne sukuupɔn abodin krataa mu.
Bere a Thomas Amoani reka n’asɛm no, ɔkaa sɛnea na ɔtaa twa kwan kilomita 12 kɔ sukuu no ho asɛm.
Eyi twetwee Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo adwene, na ntɛm ara ɔsrɛɛ no sɛ ɔmma no nhomasua nyinaa.
Wɔ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ nhyehyɛeɛ tiawa bi a wɔyɛ maa no ansa na ɔrekɔ Scholarship Secretariat mu no, Kyerɛwtohɔ no kaa sɛ nidi a Ɔmanpanin de maa Thomas no bɛboa kɛse ama afoforɔ nso ayere wɔn ho wɔ nhomasua mu ɛmfa ho baabi a wofi.
“Madi kan ahu Thomasfoɔ bebree sɛ wɔbɛsɔre na metumi ama wɔn awerɛhyɛmu sɛ Scholarships Secretariat no bɛba abɛboa wɔn. Ɛsɛ sɛ Thomas asɛm no kanyan afoforɔ te sɛ ɔno. Na ɛsɛ sɛ mekamfo Ɔmanpanin Akufo-Addo wɔ ne ho a ɔde gyee nsɛm mu ntɛm so”
Bere a ɔrekɔ sukuupɔn no, Thomas Amoani a ontumi mfa n’anigye nsie no se wayɛ krado sɛ ɔbɛma Ghana frankaa so na ɔremma ɔman no nni huammɔ.
“Mansusuw ho da sɛ Owura Ɔmampanyin nam Kyerɛwtohɔfoɔ a ɔyɛ adwumaden no so bɛma me hokwan a ɛte saa. M’ani sɔ ahotosoɔ a mewɔ wɔ me mu no paa. Merenni me man Ghana huammɔ”
Brunel University London yɛ sukuupɔn a wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ Uxbridge mpɔtam a ɛwɔ London, England. Wɔhyehyɛe wɔ 1966 mu na wɔde too Victorian engineer Isambard Kingdom Brunel din sɛ sukuupɔn a ɛto so 93 a ɛsen biara wɔ mfiridwuma ne mfiridwuma mu wɔ wiase nyinaa, a ɛto so 32 wɔ Europa ahyehyɛde ahorow mu, na ɛto so 11 wɔ Britain ahyehyɛde ahorow mu sɛnea wiase yi dibea kyerɛ no.
Asɛm biara nni Ɔtemmufo Panyin, Ɔtemmufo Kwasi Anin Yeboah a ɔredi asɛm tia mmaranimfoɔ ne Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie a ɛwɔ Bolgatanga Apuei fam, Dr Dominic Akuritinga Ayine wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie (GLC) no ho.
Sɛnea ankorankoro mmaranimfo ne kan Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie a ɛwɔ Zebilla, Owura John Ndebugre kyerɛ no, nsɛm a National Democratic Congress (NDC) ne nnipa foforo reka atia anwiinwii no yɛ nsɛm a ɛsɛ sɛ wodi ho dwuma bere a Dr Ayine kɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie (GLC) Nteɛso Boayikuw anim no.
“M'adwene yɛ me sɛ ɔno [Atemmufo Panyin) ne onipa a ɛfata sɛ ɔbɔɔ soboɔ efisɛ asɛm a Oduruyɛfo Ayine kaeɛ a ɛde anwiinwii yi baeɛ ne sɛ, sɛ yɛbɛbɔ no mua a, ahotosoɔ a ɔwɔ sɛ atemmuo no bɛyɛ nea ɔpɛ no ano abrɛ ase ɔkwan bi so wɔ ɔkwan a wɔfaa so dii aban abatoɔdeɛ no abisadeɛ no ho dwuma anaa wɔhyɛɛ too hɔ no mu.”
Ɔtemmufoɔ Panin abɔ mmaranimfoɔ Dr Dominic Akuritinga Ayine amanneɛ akyerɛ GLC Nteɛso Boayikuo no sɛ ɔkaa nsɛm a ɔkyerɛɛ wɔ baguafoɔ nhyiamu a ɛfa Ɔmanpanin Abatoɔ Adesrɛ ne nkɛntɛnsoɔ a ɛwɔ wɔ Afrika Demokrase so no.
Wɔabɔ Oduruyɛfo Ayine soboɔ sɛ ɔrepɛ ahofadi a ɛwɔ Asɛnnibea Kunini no mu no ho kyim, ɛnam ɔkwan a Asɛnnibea Kunini no faa so buu atɛn wɔ 2020 ɔmampanyin abatoɔ abisadeɛ no mu.
Abisadeɛ no gyina nea Ɔbenfo Ayine gyinaa so kaeɛ wɔ nkɔmmɔbɔ no mu no so kyerɛ sɛ Asɛnnibea Kunini no amfa mmara a ɛfa ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so ayɛ adesrɛdeɛ no anni dwuma, na ɔkɔɔ so yii abisadeɛ no abisadeɛ anaa nneɛma a ɔde bɛma no no.
“Saa nsɛm yi tia Asɛnnibea Kunini no nnyinasoɔ sɛ ɔbɔɔ Dr. Ayine soboɔ sɛ ɔnkyerɛ nsɛm a ɛtete saa a ɔka tiaa Asɛnnibea Kunini no mufoɔ wɔ abatow dwumadie no mu. Ɔbenfo Ayine paa kyɛw kɛse berɛ a ɔde asɛm no kɔɔ Asɛnnibea no anim wɔ Contempt soboɔ no ho na ɔgye toom sɛ ɔkaa nsɛm a ɛmfata sɛ ɔyɛ mmaranimfoɔ ne kan Mmaranimfoɔ Panin no.”
Dr. Ayine de nkratafa dunwɔtwe rekyerɛ sɛ asɛm a ɔkaeɛ no ntia atɛnteneneefoɔ a wɔtenaa abatoɔ asɛnnibea no.
Ɔkyerɛ sɛ na ne nsɛm no yɛ nokware.
“Sɛnea maka wɔ mmuaeɛ yi mu no, sɛ́ mmaranimfo no, mewɔ asɛyɛde soronko sɛ mɛkasa atia mmaranimfo adwuma no. Esiane nteteeɛ ne osuahu a manya nti, me ho ye sen me man mufo dodoɔ no ara sɛ mɛkyerɛ mmerɛwyɛ a ɛwɔ atemmu mu ne dwuma a mmaranimfoɔ a ɔwɔ saa mmara mu no di.”
Ɔsan kyerɛɛ mu sɛ, sɛ ɔka asɛm bi a, ɛsɛ sɛ ɔkasa ma ɛfata.
Ɔsɔretia amanyɔkuo kɛseɛ, National Democratic Congress (NDC) a ɛwɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu ase wɔ Nkran Dwoada no hyɛɛ Ɔtemmufoɔ Panyin no sɛ ɔnyi asɛm a ɔde ato Dr Ayine so no mfi hɔ.
Esiane sɛ na Ɔtemmufo Panyin no mpene gyinabea ahorow a ɛne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no yi asɛm no fi asɛnnibea na onni hokwan sɛ ɔde asɛm a ɛte saa bɛto hɔ nti, Owura Ndebugre kae sɛ ɛnyɛ sɛ ɔreka bagua no muni bi anaa bagua no mufo a na wɔadi mfe ason pɛ ho asɛm. Na ɛnyɛ sɛ ɔreka wɔn nyinaa ho asɛm. Ɔkaa asɛnni bagua no nyinaa ne Ɔtemmufo Panyin no ho asɛm, ma enti ɛyɛ onipa a ɔfata sɛ ɔde asɛm no to
Bere a ɔrekasa wɔ radio so nsɛm a Graphic Online bisabisae wɔ Nkran so a egyina Citi FM so Benada anwummere (June 22, 2021) no, Owura Ndebugre kae sɛ: "M'adwene yɛ me sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no ho asɛm biara nni asɛm a ɛfa asɛm no ho"
Bere a yɛde ɛno retoto nea esii wɔ 1996 mu no ho no, Adehyeman no sɔre tiaa Mensah Bonsu, Stephen Quarcoo ne Tommy Thompson wɔ saa asɛm no mu a Mensah Bonsu sɔre tiaa ɔtemmufo bi, Ɔtemmufo Abban ma enti ɔbɔɔ sobo no na afei Ɔtemmufo Panyin no yii asɛm no fii hɔ kɔɔ asɛnnibea no.
Ɔhaw biara nni CJ anwiinwii no ho
"Enti misusuw sɛ ɛnyɛ ɔhaw biara sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no bɛbɔ sobo no.
Asɛm foforɔ no ne sɛ, Dominic Ayine yɛ Abɛɛfo Kwankyerɛfoɔ Panin abadiakyire, na ɔne ne panyin de nnipa kɔɔ nsɛmmɔnedifoɔ asɛnnibea, de wɔn kɔɔ ɔmanfoɔ asɛnnibea. Enti sɛ Abɛɛfo Kwankyerɛfoɔ panin pene so sɛ wɔmmɔ obi soboɔ a, obiara bɛtumi aka sɛ dabi, na saa nipa no reda ɔkasa mu ahofadi adi—ɛnde na ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔde no kɔ asɛnnibea.
Dabi, ɛsɛ sɛ wokɔ asɛnnibea kodi w’asɛm, na wudi w’asɛm, na woka sɛ wunni fɔ wɔ bɔne a wɔbɔɔ wo no ho.
Enti ɔkwan koro no ara so no, Ɔtemmufo Panyin no susuw sɛ asɛm no fa atɛmmuo no ahofadi ho.
Enti wokɔ hɔ a, nsɛm a NDC ne Dr. Ayine ankasa abɔ ho ban seesei ara no nyinaa yɛ nsɛm a ɛsɛ sɛ ɛkɔ so wɔ Nteɛso Boayikuw no mu,” Owura Ndebugre de kaa ho.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔbɛka mfasoɔ a ɛwɔ so no ho asɛm, ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ abien na ɛwɔ hɔ, ɛte sɛ animguaseɛ berɛ a asɛm no da so ara retwɛn, ɛne sɛ, sɛ woka nsɛm a ɛmfata kyerɛ atɛntenenee berɛ a asɛm no da so ara retwɛn a, ɛnde bere a wɔabu atɛn na woka nsɛm a ɛmfata kyerɛ asɛnnibea ahodoɔ no, wubetumi adi w’asɛm wɔ ho.
Sɛ woadi nkogu wɔ asɛnnibea a, wubetumi aka sɛ wo ne wo nyɛ adwene, nanso ka sɛ? Meka sɛ mempɛ sɛ me ne wo bɛbɔ nkɔmmɔ, na nea mereyɛ seesei ara ne sɛ me ne wo nyɛ adwene wɔ gyinabea a ɛne sɛ amanyɔkuo no nti na ɔrekyerɛ sɛ ɔwɔ hokwan sɛ ɔkyerɛ n’adwene, enti ɛnsɛ sɛ wodi asɛm no akyi.
Asɛm no ne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wokɔ Nteɛso Boayikuw no hɔ na woka kyerɛ wɔn sɛ woreyɛ adwuma no, nanso worentumi nka sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no ntumi nwiinwii, ɔno na ɔyɛ asɛnni boayikuw no ti, na woka sɛ ahotoso a wowɔ wɔ asɛnni boayikuw no mu no abrɛ ase esiane ɔkwan a wɔfaa so dii asɛm no nti.
Bere a wobisaa no adwene a ɛne sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no na ɔhwɛ GLC ne afei Nteɛso Boayikuw no so no, ɛyɛ n’asɛnnibea boayikuw ketewa bi, ma enti ɔde Ayine rekɔ n’ankasa “fese” sɛ wɔmmɛdi no asɛm, Owura Ndebugre buae sɛ, "yɛ wo sɛ wɔn a wɔbom yɛ Nteɛso Boayikuw no yɛ robɔt, na wɔrebɛgye akwankyerɛ afi Ɔtemmufo Panyin no hɔ. Sɛ woyɛ saa nneɛma yi a, ɛmmoa mma yɛn dodow amammu no nkɔ so. Ɔkasa mu ahofadi n
Ɔde Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie Nteɛso Boayikuw no dii dwuma, faako a mmarahyɛdwafie no atwe nnipa a wɔwɔ hɔ no, "wɔn a wɔnka wɔn nsusuwii anaa hokwan a wɔwɔ sɛ wotumi kasa no. Sɛ wokɔ na woka sɛ wɔafom a, mmarahyɛbɛdwafiefo nyinaa bra asɛe a wonni adanse biara a, wɔbɛtwe wo akɔ Hokwan Ahorow Boayikuw no mu—ɛdɛn nti na woreka sɛ wɔrentumi nnye wo kyim wɔ asɛm foforo mu?
“Merenka sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no yɛ nea ɛteɛ anaa nea ɛnteɛ.
Nea mereka ara ne sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no abɔ asɛm no, ɛdefa me ho no, ɔno na ɔfata sɛ ɔbɔ asɛm no efisɛ asɛm no tia asɛnni bagua no, ahofadi a asɛnni bagua no wɔ, na ɔno na ɔyɛ asɛnni bagua no ti na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde asɛm no kɔ asɛnnibea.
Anwiinwii no nkyerɛ sɛ wɔabu wo fɔ, ɛsɛ sɛ wokɔ hɔ kɔkyerɛkyerɛ nsɛm a woresusuw ho wɔ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ nhyiam ahorow ase ne nea ɛkeka ho no nyinaa mu, na ɛno ansa na asɛm no bɛda adi.
Sɛ wokɔ hɔ na adanse wɔ hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ woyɛ nyiyim a, ɛnna wubetumi afi ase anwiinwii, nanso misusuw sɛ saa bere yi de, ɛnkyɛ na mitu Ayine fo sɛ ɔmmɔ mmɔden nkɔ Nteɛso Boayikuw no anim na ɔmfa n’asɛm mma wɔn, ɛyɛ wɔn anigye sɛ wɔbɛkɔ akɔkyerɛ sɛ Ɔtemmufo Panyin no yɛ ɔtorofo.”
Ɔman Asomdwoeɛ Asoeɛ (NPC) ayɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛma biakoyɛ a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu ayɛ kɛseɛ berɛ a afe a etwaam no abatoɔ awieɛ no.
Sɛnea bagua no kyerɛ no, amammuisɛm mu mmarato yɛ ɔsɛmpɔw titiriw a na ebetumi de tebea a ɛyɛ den aba, enti na ɛho hia sɛ wodi ho dwuma wɔ asɛm no mu.
NPC kaa saa asɛm yi berɛ a wɔne amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ ne nnipa foforɔ a wɔwɔ Ada a ɛwɔ Nkran Mantam mu rebɔ nkɔmmɔ no.
Amanaman Nkabom asoeɛ ne Amanaman Nkabom Nkɔso Asoeɛ (UNDP) taa nkitahodie yi akyi.
Ná atirimpɔw no ne sɛ wɔbɛhyɛ wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ mu no nkuran ma wɔahyehyɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛbɛma biakoyɛ kɛse aba ɔman no mu, amammuisɛm mu abotare, asomdwoe ne ɔman denhyɛ.
Wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ mu no bi ne Ɔkyerɛwfo Panyin a ɔda Amanaman Nkabom Asoeɛ ano, Rt Hon Patricia Scotland; UNDP Ananmusini, Dr Angela Lusigi; Amanneɛbɔ asoafoɔ, Owura Kojo Oppong Nkrumah; ɔman no mu, Owura Ambrose Dery ne Ɔman Ahobammɔ, Owura Albert Kan-Dapaah.
Afoforɔ nso yɛ Abatoɔ Asoeɛ panin abɛdiakyire, Dr. Eric Bossman Asare; ɔyɛ Inspector-General of Police nanmusini, National Democratic Congress, the New Patriotic Party, the Convention People’s Party, tete atumfoɔ ne ɔmanfoɔ ahyehyɛde ahodoɔ.
Owura Dery kaa sɛ ɛmfa ho ahobammɔ nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔyɛ too hɔ ansa na wɔrebɛtow aba wɔ December mu no, basabasayɛ bebree da so ara rekɔ so a ɛkunkum nnipa binom na ɛmaa wɔsɛee agyapadeɛ no.
Ɔkaa sɛ polisifoɔ yɛɛ basabasayɛ 32 ho kyerɛwtohɔ wɔ amanyɔkuo anum mu wɔ ɔman no mu a emu nnipa baasia wuwuiɛ.
Owura Dery kaa sɛ aban no nnyae mmɔden a ɔbɔ sɛ ɔbɛma wɔn a wɔhyɛ basabasayɛ yi akyi no akɔ asɛnnibea.
Wɔ ne fam no, Owura Kan-Dapaah kaa sɛ amammuisɛm mu abotare ne adwene nhyehyɛeɛ da so ara yɛ ɔman no asetra, sikasɛm ne amammuisɛm nkɔsoɔ fã.
Rt Hon. Scotland kamfoo Ghana manfoɔ wɔ asomdwoeɛ a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ amanyɔsɛm ho ɔkasa mu wɔ ɔman no mu a ɔkaa sɛ Commonwealth abusua no nyinaa agye atom no.
Sɛdeɛ ɔkyerɛ no, Ghana na ɔdii kan wɔ dodoɔ amammuo mu, a ɔkaa sɛ ɛyɛ adesoa kɛseɛ wɔ nkurɔfoɔ mmati so nanso ɛyɛ adesoa sɛ nkurɔfoɔ de ahomasoɔ adi ho dwuma. Yɛde yɛn ani ato Ghana so berɛ nyinaa.
Nanso, ɔhyɛɛ mmara sɛ wɔmfa mmea ne mmerante ne mmabaa pii nkɔ ɔman no mu.
NPC panin, Ɔbenfo Ernest Adu-Gyamfi kaa sɛ n’atadeɛ reyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛma nkitahodie ne nkitahodie a ɛbɛkɔ so wɔ ɔman ahyehyɛdeɛ akɛseɛ mu no mu ayɛ den.
Ɔdaa anidasoɔ a ɛwɔ mu sɛ nsɛm a yɛasusuw ho yi bɛboa kɛse ama akuru a ɛde aba wɔ 2020 abatoɔ no akyi.
Ɔsoafoɔ panin a ɔwɔ Transeco fagudeɛtu ne fagudeɛtu mu, Owura Godwin Amarh asi adesuadan a ɛwɔ Akyem Ampapatia a ɛwɔ Atiwa Atɔeɛ Mantam mu wɔ Apueɛ Mantam mu.
Adesua dan no boɔ yɛ GH 295,000 na ɛyɛ Adwumakuo no Asetra mu Asɛyɛdeɛ (CSR) fã.
Bere a Owura Amarh rekasa wɔ nhyiamu ase no, osii so dua sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔde ntetee pa ma mmofra a wɔba fam sɛnea ɛbɛboa wɔn ma wɔanya nhomasua mu fapem a ɛyɛ den.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ yɛsɛe dwuma a nhomasua di wɔ ɔman biara mu nkɔso mu, enti adɛn nti na n’adwumakuo no de nhomasua di kan?
“Yɛn a yɛwɔ Transeco Mining and Minerals Company no asi gyinae sɛ yɛbɛhwɛ ama mmofra a wɔwɔ mpɔtam a yɛyɛ adwuma no anya nkyerɛkyerɛ ne adesua ho nhyehyɛe pa bere a wɔn nhomasua nkɔ anim. Ɛno nti na yɛde nhomasua adi kan wɔ yɛn adwuma no asetram asɛyɛde ho no.
Ɛyɛ me anigye sɛ masan aba Ampapatia abɛhwɛ sukuu yi so. Yɛn nyinaa nim sɛnea nhomasua ho hia na ama ankorankoro ne ɔman no anya nkɔso. Nea ɛbɛyɛ na wɔanya sukuufo a wɔn ho akokwaw wɔ nhomasua a ɛkɔ anim mu no, ɛsɛ sɛ wodi kan nya fapem a ɛyɛ den, ɛno nti na yɛasi saa Kindergarten yi no.
Owura Amarh kaa sɛ sukuu no nso yɛ anisɔ ma Ampapatia ahemfo ne nnipa a wɔne adwumakuo no anya abusuabɔ pa fi berɛ a wofii wɔn dwumadie aseɛ wɔ mpɔtam hɔ no.
Nea ɛne atesɛm ne nsusuwii bɔne a ɛne sɛ aban abara fagudeɛtu dwumadie wɔ ɔman no mu bɔ abira no, Owura Amarh bɔɔ atesɛm no gui na ɔkaa ho asɛm sɛ ɛnyɛ mfomso nko na mmom ɛyɛ atoro.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ, aban de nhyehyɛeɛ ne nhyehyɛeɛ foforɔ a ɛbɛma fagudeɛtu nketewa no asow aba na ɛnsɛe adeɛ aba.
“Aban mmaraa fagudeɛtufoɔ dwumadie na mmom akuw ahodoɔ a ɛbɛn nsuo ne kwaeɛ yɛ kɔkɔɔ a ɛnsɛ sɛ ankorɛankorɛ anaa adwumakuo biara tu fagudeɛtufoɔ. Enti nea aban reka ne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ fagudeɛtufoɔ nketewa tu fi fagudeɛtubea kɔkɔɔ no mu. Enti obiara a ɔne aban mmara nhyia no, ɔbɛdi ɔman no mmara so”
Enti otuu faga adwumayɛfoɔ nketewa fo sɛ wɔnkɔyɛ adwuma nanso wɔnhwɛ sɛ wɔbɛtu fagudeɛ wɔ mmeae bi.
Owura Amarh a ɔno nso yɛ mmɔho abien sɛ Ghana National Association of Small Scale Miners (GNASSM) Kyerɛwfo Panyin no tuu kuw no mufo fo sɛ wɔnnya nkɛntɛnso pa wɔ aman a wɔwɔ tumi krataa no so.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ adwumayɛfo nketewa a wotu fagudeɛ no bɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛsesa kyerɛwtohɔ a ɛne sɛ wɔyɛ adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔtwe wɔn ho fi ɔmanfoɔ nkyɛn kɛkɛ na wɔmfa hwee mma no.
Ɔkae sɛ, ɛwom sɛ fagudeɛtufoɔ nketewa pii reyɛ saa deɛ, nanso ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ pii.
“Yɛn adwuma no de nnipa pii yɛ adwuma wɔ nkurow a yɛyɛ adwuma no mu. Enti ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyere yɛn ho sɛ yebegyae adwuma. Minim yɛn adwumayɛfo pii a wɔasisi sukuu ahorow na afoforo aboa ɔmanfo ma wɔanya anyinam ahoɔden. Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛpiapia saa nsɛm no kɔ hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛbɛsesa kyerɛwtohɔ a ɛne sɛ faga nketewa nkutoo na wɔsɛe no”
Rebecca Ahyehyɛde no ne Abdul Samad Rabiu Africa Initiative (ASR Africa) ayɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛma wɔanya dɔla mpem ahanum.
Wobegye akwannya yi afi ASR Africa afe afe foto dɔla ɔpepem ɔha na wɔde aboa Rebecca Ahyehyɛde no nhomasua nhyehyɛe.
Bere a ɔrekasa wɔ nhyiamu no ase no, ASR Africa Kwankyerɛfoɔ panin, Owura Ubon Udoh, kamfoo nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ sɛ ɛbɛboa mmea ne mmofra a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu.
Ɔkamfoo fapem no nso sɛ ɛbata nnwumakuo nniso ne nneyɛe pa a atumi ama fapem no anya nhomasua, akwahosan ne mmea sikasɛm mu tumi.
“Yɛyɛɛ yɛn sukuu dwumadie wɔ fie na yɛdaa Rebecca Foundation no adi sɛ ɛyɛ adɔeɛ a ɛdi mu paa wɔ Ghana, na ɛhyɛɛ ASR Africa nkuran sɛ ɔmmoa Rebecca Foundation no.”
Ɔpanyin a ɔda Fekuw no ano, Owurayere Rebecca Akufo-Addo daa ASR Africa ase wɔ mmoa a wɔde maa fapem no ho.
Ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ ɔbɛhyɛ fapem no bɔ sɛ ɔde bɛboa mmofra ntetee wɔ ɔman no mu.

Sɛnea mmaranimfoɔ panin kyerɛ no, wɔde Owura Kanu a ɔyɛ Britania ne Nigeria man ba no too afiase Kwasida ɛdenam Interpol mmoa so na ɔsan kɔɔ Nigeria.
Wɔbɔɔ no soboɔ wɔ Nigeria, nanso afe 2017 mu no, ɔtwee ne ho fii ɔman no mu.
Wɔabɔ wɔn tirim sɛ ebia wɔkyeree no wɔ UK, faako a wogye di sɛ na ɔwɔ nnyinaso titiriw no.
“Yebetumi agyina so aka sɛ wɔankyere Nnamdi Kanu wɔ UK sɛ wabɔ ne tirim sɛ ɔbɛtwe wɔn afi hɔ” a Britain Asoeɛ Kɛseɛ kasamafoɔ ka kyerɛɛ BBC.
Mprempren ɔda Nigeria kokoam polisifo nkyɛn bere a wɔde asɛm tiawa bi kɔɔ asɛnnibea Benada no.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ n’asɛnni no bɛsan akɔ so wɔ July 26.
Afe 2009 mu no, abranteɛ a wadi mfeɛ aduonu nson no bɛnyaa dimmɔneɛ berɛ a ɔhyɛɛ Radio Biafra ase, na ɔnam asɛnka agua so kɔɔ Nigeria kɔsrɛɛ Biafra fahodie, na ɔhyɛɛ n’akyidifoɔ sɛ wɔnko ntia Nigeria man no.
Mfe nnum akyi no, ɔtew Indian People of Biafra (Ipob) a Nigeria atumfoɔ afrɛ no amumɔyɛfoɔ ahyehyɛde no.
Bere a wodii kan kyeree Owura Kanu afe 2015 no, nnipa pii sɔre tiaa no.
Bere a mihui sɛ wɔresiesie Independence Square no awie afe a etwaam no, m’ani gyei.
Wɔyɛɛ nsiesie yi, a mfonini ne kɔnkrit nnwuma ka ho, na wɔde asiesie Square no ama kan Ɔmanpanin Jerry John Rawlings ayiyɛ amanne.
Akwankyerɛfoɔ Adesuabea (IoD-Gh) akamfo Ghana Sikakorabea (BoG) sɛ wɔayɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛbɛboa adwumakuo nniso pa wɔ ɔman no mu.
Afei nso ahwehwɛ sɛ ahyehyɛde no ne sikakorabea no bɛyɛ biako sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛboa ama nnwumakuo a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu atumi adi nneɛma ho dwuma.
Adesuabea a ɛhwɛ BoG dwumadie so no, IoD-Gh panin, Owura Roc Jackson Kwesi Dogbegah kamfoo sikakorabea kɛseɛ panin, Ɔbenfo Ernest Addison sɛ ɔde nsakraeɛ akwankyerɛ ama sikasɛm nnwuma.
Ɔkaa sɛ BoG mmɔdenbɔ a Oduruyɛfo Addison di anim no akɔfa sikakorabea nnwumakuo a wɔn ho yɛ den na wɔn ho yɛ den.
Asɛm bi a efi ahyehyɛde no hɔ kyerɛɛ sɛ nsrahwɛ no ne sɛ ɔbɛkamfo sikakorabea no wɔ dwuma titiriw a wɔde reboa adwumakuo nniso a ɛwɔ Ghana na wɔahwehwɛ abusuabɔ pa a ɛda BoG ne ahyehyɛde no ntam.
Bere a Owura Dogbegah reka nneɛma atitiriw a YoD-Gh yɛ ho asɛm no, ɔkae sɛ YoD-Gh reyɛ nhyehyɛe a n’atirimpɔw ne sɛ ɔde bɛhyehyɛ mmara ama adwumakuo nniso wɔ Ghana.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ aban mmara a ɔman no bɛhyehyɛ no yɛ adwuma titiriw foforɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ ahyehyɛdeɛ no yɛ.
Ɔdaa no adi sɛ adwumakuo no ahyehyɛ mmɔdenbɔ a ɛfa mmɔdenbɔ kɛseɛ a wɔabɔ sɛ wɔde bɛhyɛ ankorɛankorɛ ne adwumakuo ahyehyɛdeɛ a ɛda nsow a ɛgyina hɔ ma akwankyerɛ pa wɔ adwumakuo ne adwumakuo ahyehyɛdeɛ mu, na wɔaboa kɛseɛ ama Ghana man no sikasɛm mu nkɔsoɔsoɔ.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ, Adesuabea no ne nnipa atitiriw a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ mu reyɛ adwuma no aboa ma wɔate Ghana Association of Integrated Thinking and Reporting a atirimpɔw no ne sɛ ɛbɛkanyan ɔkwan pa a ahyehyɛde ahorow fa so bɔ nneɛma a ɛsom bo ho amanneɛ.
BoG Amrado kaa sɛ nnwuma mu mpanyimfoɔ di dwuma titiriw bi wɔ sikasɛm mu.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ, nnwuma mu atumfoɔ bu wɔn ani gu wɔn nneyɛe so, na wɔn nneyɛe nso bu wɔn ani gu wɔn nneyɛe so sɛ nneɛma a ɛmaa sikakorabea ahodoɔ bi dii nkogu wɔ sikasɛm mu na wɔyɛɛ ho nhyehyɛeɛ.
Ɔsan kyerɛɛ hia a ɛho hia sɛ Ghana man no bɛboa nnwumakuo ahodoɔ a ɛdi nneɛma ho dwuma, na ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ sikakorabea no bɛboa adwumakuo no, ɛnkanka berɛ a nsɛm a ɛresisi wɔ sikakorabea no anya Ghana man no sikasɛm so nkɛntɛnso bɔne no.
Arteta na ɛsɛ sɛ ogye bere foforo
Sɛnea maka dedaw no, Arsenal nyɛɛ n'adwene sɛ ɔbɛbɔ Mikel Arteta ban na kuw no sohwɛfo bɛsan de no akɔhyɛ Gunners no nsa wɔ ɔsram a ɛreba no mu.
Obiara ntumi nkyerɛ sɛ Arsenal asi gyinae pa nanso bɔɔlbɔkuo no pɛ sɛ ɔde bɔɔlbɔfo a ne ho akokwaw kɛse ba ahohuru bere yi mu.
Wɔrebisa nsɛm a anibere wom afa adwumam panyin no mmɔdenbɔ ne wɔn a wɔhyɛ n’ankasa dan mu ntade mpo ho rehwɛ no na wɔresusuw ho sɛ ebia ɔno ne ɔbarima a ɔfata ma adwuma no anaa.
Arteta a wadi mfeɛ 39 agye din wɔ Pep Guardiola nkyɛn sɛ agumadi kyerɛfoɔ panin.
Nanso asram dunson akyi a wɔde ahwɛ Chelsea so no, na nnipa pii bɛka sɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo no mmɔdenbɔ nnu Unai Emery deɛ no. Ɔbarima a ɔde no sii n’ananmu na ɔpam no fii Europa League no mu.
Arteta kyerɛɛ Chelsea ne Tottenham kwan na bɔɔlbɔfoɔ no gyee wɔn fɛw so sɛ wɔn nkonimdifoɔ foforɔ nanso berɛ a wɔhwɛ Chelsea ne Tottenham anim no, wɔn ho yera wɔn na wɔn ho yera wɔn.
Yɛn werɛ remfi Super League asiane no bere tenten
Nanso metumi aka akyerɛ mo sɛ Kroenke wuranom no nkɔ baabiara
Arteta na ɛsɛ sɛ osiesie ɛtwene, ɔhyehyɛ kuw a ɛyɛ den na ɔfa ne nnɛɛdɛe no ɛbere a ɛreba no mu, anyɛ saa a Gunners a wɔyɛ ahantan no bɛhwe ase ahyew no.
De Gea rennye ntom sɛ ɔyɛ Ɔkannifo
Ɛmfa ho sɛ Manchester United goalkeeper David De Gea yɛɛ nhyehyɛe kosii 2023 mu no, n’adwumayɛfoɔ no resɔ nsuo no ahwɛ akuw a wɔbɛpɛ sɛ wɔde wɔn nsa hyɛ aseɛ.
Meretie wɔ Old Trafford mu sɛ ɛmfa ho sɛ me ne Dean Henderson a ɔwɔ hɔ seesei no wɔ abusuabɔ pa no, De Gea renkɔ so ntra benkyi no so nkosi bere bi.
Merekyerɛ anigye afi Atletico Madrid, Paris Saint Germain ne Real Madrid.
Ɛwom sɛ ebinom a wɔwɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu gye di sɛ bɛyɛ mfeɛ mmienu a atwa mu no, aberanteɛ a wadi mfeɛ aduasa no abɔ mmɔden paa wɔ n’adwuma mu deɛ, nanso ɛyɛ nokorɛ.
Adwuma sohwɛfo Solskjaer kaa sɛ, “Adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔhwɛ Goalkeeper dwumadie so no yɛ adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔn ho yɛ den paa.
Wɔyɛ adwuma de siesie wɔn ho, ɛsono sɛnea wɔyɛ wɔn ade wɔ apɔwmu - teɛteɛ mu, ɛsono sɛnea wɔyɛ wɔn ade wɔ apɔwmu - teɛteɛ mu, ɛnna ɛsono sɛnea wɔyɛ wɔn ade wɔ apɔwmu - teɛteɛ mu, ɛnna ɛsono sɛnea wɔyɛ wɔn ade wɔ apɔwmu - teɛteɛ mu.
Sɛnea ɛte no, wɔma nkitahodi ne honhom kɔ so wɔ baabi a wɔhwɛ ma wɔde botae sisi wɔn ani so no.
Ɛyɛ akansi a ɛfata.”
Migye di sɛ nea ɔkyerɛ agumadi no yɛ nokware, nanso sɛ De Gea annye No1 a wɔakyerɛw wɔ ne hyɛɛt no akyi na wɔagyaw no wɔ benkyi no so wɔ agumadi a ɛho hia mu a, mɛka akyerɛ no sɛ obefi Old Trafford akɔ.
Mesan de West Brom kɔɔ hɔ bio
Bere a yɛsan kɔɔ Premier League no, yɛne West Bromwich Albion dii nkra bio.
Adeɛ a ɛbɛboa ma wɔagyae akansi no ntɛm ara ne sɛ wɔbɛka akyerɛ Sam Allardyce a ɔyɛ odumgyafoɔ no sɛ ɔntena hɔ.
N’abam bui sɛ wahwere ne din sɛ wamfa ne ho anhyɛ kuw biara mu da na sɛ mpanyimfo a wɔwɔ West Brom no pɛ sɛ wodi n’akyi a, wɔwɔ adwuma pii yɛ.
Ainsley Maitland-Niles, Conor Gallagher ne Okay Yokuslu bɛsan akɔ wɔn awofo akuw mu bere a wɔagye bosea no nanso Matheus Pereira, Callum Robinson, Hal Robson - Kanu ne Karlan Grant betumi akyerɛ wɔn ho anigye wɔ akuw a ɛba fam no mu.
Ɔbarima a Ne Ho Yɛ Den Sen Biara Wɔ Kuropɔn Mu
Hena na ɔbɔ mmirika sen biara wɔ Manchester City bɔɔlbɔ kuw no mu?
Dabi, ɛnyɛ Raheem sterling.
Adwuma sohwɛfo Pep Guardiola hyehyɛɛ su bi a na ɛsɛ sɛ agumadifoɔ no mu biara de bɔɔl no si bɔɔl no so na ɔde bɔɔl no si bɛyɛ mita 10.
Nnipa bi atu mmirika denneennen wɔ Kurow no mu, nanso Gabriel Yesu daa no adi sɛ ɔno na ɔyɛɛ ntɛm sen obiara.
Nea eye sen biara no nnya mfii Havertz
Thomas Tuchel ato kai Havertz ayeyi dwom na ɔtwee adwene sii ne botae abien a ɔde sii Fulham so nnansa yi ara no so.
Tuchel gye tom sɛ efi bere a kai fi Bayer Leverkusen kɔɔ Stamford Bridge no, nneɛma nkɔ yiye mma Germanfo.
Tu a otu fii amannɔne kɔɔ ɔman foforo so a na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔdi anohyeto ahorow a ɛwɔ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ adwuma no maa nneɛma mu yɛɛ den na nokwarem no, ɔkyeree Covid-19 na ɛho behiae sɛ ɔsan di apɔwmuden ho dwuma.
Tuchel gye di sɛ akansifoɔ a ɛdi kan ne nea ɛdi hɔ ansa na nnipakuo no reba no bɛyɛ nea ɔbɛtumi biara wɔ akansifoɔ no anim.
Solskjaer de ne ho rehyɛ nkonimdi mu bio
Ebetumi aba sɛ Manchester United ne wɔn a wɔhwɛ bɔɔlbɔ so no rehyia ɔhaw kɛse a wɔde kyerɛ sɛ wɔn ani nnye wɔn wuranom ho, nanso wɔn a wɔwɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu no wɔ gyidi foforo, biakoyɛ foforo ne ahotoso foforo sɛ wobetumi anya.
Ɔbarima a ɔhwɛ adwuma no so ne Ole Gunner Solskjaer na bere a ɔne United adwumayɛfoɔ ne aboafoɔ pii akasa nnawɔtwe yi mu no, obiara gye tom sɛ ɛbere aso sɛ ɔkamfo adwuma sohwɛfoɔ no sɛ watumi ayɛ pii wɔ asram dunwɔtwe a atwa mu.
Solskjaer yɛɛ nhyehyɛe de ne nsa hyɛɛ Bruno Fernandes ne Edinson Cavani ase, na wɔn baanu nyinaa ada wɔn ho adi sɛ wɔyɛ nkaefo pa a wɔka United States nhyehyɛe no ho.
cavani asi so dua sɛ ɔbɛtra hɔ bere foforo, na ɛyɛ gyidi a ɔwɔ wɔ Solskjaer mu no na akyerɛ no nea ɔnyɛ.
Paul Pogba ani agye na ɔne adwumam panyin no ntam abusuabɔ mu ayɛ den paa.
Nnansa yi sɛ United hwe ase wɔ akansi bi mu a, wɔsɔre wɔn akyi, wɔko ntɔkwaw na mpɛn pii no wodi nkonim.
Ade biako wɔ hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛda Abɛɛfo Kwankyerɛfoɔ Panin abɛdiakyire Ed Woodward ase, na ɛno ama Solskjaer anya bere de ayɛ adwuma no yie.
Solskjaer ne fapem a ɛho hia sen biara ne nea ɛyɛ den sen biara wɔ Amanaman Nkabom no mu, na akasatiafoɔ, adwumayɛfoɔ ne wɔn a wɔn ani gye ho no gye di sɛ eyi yɛ bere pa mfiaseɛ ma Reds.
