Kane redwennwen ho sɛ ɔbɛkɔ
Bere a na me ne Leeds redi agoru wɔ dapɛn awiei no, mekɔɔ so yɛɛ komm.
Harry Kane taa tu mmirika dodo, sɛ ɛboro saa mpo a, ɔtaa tu mmirika no sen obi foforo biara, na ɔde ahyɛde ne akwankyerɛ ma agumadifo afoforo sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛbɔ no yiye.
Ná ɔmpɛ Leeds asɛm koraa, enti misusuw sɛ mahu no pɛn.
Misusuw sɛ eyi yɛ sɛnkyerɛnne a ɛkyerɛ sɛ Harry nnye ntom koraa sɛ ɔwɔ Spurs na ɔrehwehwɛ ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so afi mu.
Mpataku a wɔn ho pere wɔn sɛ wobenya adwumayɛfo
Awiei koraa no, Nuno Espirito Santos agye atom sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde ne nsa hyɛ krataa a ɔde bɛkɔ akɔyɛ adwuma foforo ase.
Winger Pedro Neto ne mfinimfini mmɔdenbɔfo Ruben Neves ne nnipa atitiriw a wɔde wɔn ani asi mmerɛwyɛ a ɛwɔ Wolves mu no so.
Fabio Silva ne Raul Jimenez ka wɔn a wɔaka wɔn ho asɛm sɛ Jimenez agyae adwuma fi November mu bere a ɔbobɔɔ ne tikora akyi no.
Mpataku de botae 13 na esisi wɔn ani so saa bere yi sen afe a etwaam no.
Wolves boayikuw no ahyɛ Nuno bɔ sɛ ɔde ne nsa bɛhyɛ bɔ sɛ ɔde ne nsa bɛhyɛ bɔɔlbɔni bi ase.
Wɔbɛka akyerɛ Jimenez wɔ kwan so wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so dunwɔtwe mu sɛ ɔbɛdi agoru abien a etwa to wɔ saa bosome yi mu a ɛyɛ dwoodwoo.
Wɔde asram abien atete no, nanso wɔbaraa no sɛ ɔmmfa bɔɔl no nni dwuma na ɔne ne mfɛfo nni nkitaho.
Owura Alex kamfo McTominay
Sɛ Owura Alex Ferguson ka Manchester United ho asɛm a, ɛfata sɛ yetie no bere nyinaa.
N’ani gye Scott McTominay ho kɛse na owura no ka sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ mfinimfini mmirikatufo no di agoru biara wɔ United.
Sir Alex kae sɛ, “Scott McTominay abɛyɛ United States agodifoɔ akɛseɛ no mu baako”
“Sɛ wohwɛ United sɛ ɔrepaw wɔn kuw ama agoru bi a ɛho hia a, McTominay din wɔ mu.
Ɔyɛ obi a ɔwɔ suban pa na ɔtete afoforo.
Mede me nsa hyɛɛ ase bere a na ɔyɛ abofra a wadi mfe ason anaa awotwe no
Na n’ani kyerɛ mfinimfini ankasa.”
Ayeyi kɛse bɛn na bɔɔlbɔfo betumi anya?
Bɔɔlbɔ mu nokwasɛm ahorow abiɛsa a ɛyɛ nwonwa
* Manchester United ntɔɔ fam wɔ PL no mu afe ne asram anan!
* Sɛ wɔanni nkonim wɔ wɔn bɔɔlbɔ a edi hɔ no mu a, Sheffield United bɛyɛ kuw a edi kan fi 1904 - 5 mu a wɔadi nkonim wɔ bɔɔlbɔ abien mu.
Ɔbenfo Madzorera kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ no nso ma nkurɔfoɔ te yareɛ no ho asɛm, na wɔfrɛ nkurɔfoɔ wɔ telefon so wɔ ɔman no afanan nyinaa sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛfrɛ nkurɔfoɔ berɛ biara aka yareɛ no ho asɛm.
Wɔrehyɛ nyansa nso sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ahotew mu nhwehwɛmu, sen sɛ anka wɔbɛtwɛn obi a wosusuw sɛ ɔyare mmoawa no ma ɔde wɔn akɔ ayaresabea.
Caps United States guamtrani Lewis Uriri se wɔadi ɔhaw a wɔrehyia wɔ wɔn bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu ho dwuma, na agumadifoɔ a wɔn ho yɛ nwonwa no afi ase reyɛ ahoboa ama wɔn Castle Premier Soccer League akansi no.
Bere a Uriri ne Studio rekasa no, ɔkae sɛ wɔde wɔn sika a ɛda nsow maa agodifoɔ no.
Nanso ɔkae sɛ ɔsram a etwaam no akatua bɛma wɔn a wɔbɔ bɔɔl nnansa yi ara. Ɔkae nso sɛ nnipa bi wɔ hɔ a wonnim wɔn a wɔrehyɛ wɔn a wɔbɔ bɔɔl wɔ Caps United no ma wɔagyae bɔɔl bɔ.
Uriri kaa sɛ wakasa akyerɛ agumadifoɔ no, na ɔsan kaa nea enti a wɔtwentwɛnee wɔn nan ase sɛ wɔbɛtua agumadifoɔ no ka no ho asɛm sɛ ɛyɛ den ma ɔman no mufoɔ nyinaa sɛ wɔbɛyɛ saa na aban no ankasa nso antua afe a etwaam no mu sika.
Wɔn a wɔhyɛ nna mu hokwan ho nkuran no kyerɛ sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara a ɛfa nyinsɛn a wotu gu ho mu na ama wɔatumi abɔ mmeawa ne mmea nkwa ho ban.
Sayendisa Ndlovu a ɔwɔ SayWhat ɔmanfo nnim nyinsɛn a wotu gu ho mmara no, na ɔka sɛ ɛho hia sɛ aban bɔ mmara no dawuru.
Ndlovu ka kyerɛɛ studio 7 sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara no mu sɛnea wɔkyerɛw no bere tenten a atwam no. Ɔkae sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara no mu na wɔde nneɛma foforo a ebetumi ama wɔapɔn yafunu aka ho.
Ndlovu kaa nneɛma bi te sɛ adwenemyareɛ, HIV / AIDS anaa dɛmdi ho asɛm sɛ ɛyɛ nneɛma a yebetumi asusuw ho sɛ ɛde nyinsɛn a wotu gu ba.
Ndlovu kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu nso sɛ, sɛnea mmara kyerɛ no, ɛnyɛ aban ayaresabea ahorow nkutoo na ɛsɛ sɛ wotu nyinsɛn gu, na saa ara nso na ɛnhwehwɛ sɛ ɔyarehwɛfo anaa oduruyɛfo a ɔhwɛ abofra bi betu no agu wɔ mmara kwan so.
Awuraa Tendaishe Changamire, a ɔyɛ ɔmanfoɔ ahofadi dwumadie wɔ Right Here Right Now dwumadie ase no nso ahwehwɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ mmara no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a nyinsɛn a wɔbɛsɛe no no bɛyɛ kɛse.
Awuraa Changamire se nhwehwɛmu pii kyerɛ sɛ mmeawa nkumaa nam nyinsɛn a wotu gu so rehwere wɔn nkwa.
Ɛwom sɛ mmerante ne mmabaa pii repiapia sɛ wɔnyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara no mu de, nanso mmea mpanyimfo bi sɔre tia, na wɔka sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ nyinsɛn a wotu gu ho mmara ma ɛyɛ nea wogye tom kɛse, na wɔka sɛ ɛbɛma mmerante ne mmabaa ahwere obu wɔ asetra mu.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie bi yɛɛ Pregnancy Act no ho nhyehyɛe wɔ 1977 mu ansa na ɔman no anya ahofadi koraa.
Polisifoɔ akyere MDC-T a Nelson Chamisa di anim no mufoɔ bebree berɛ a wɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛkɔ amanyɔkuo no adwumayɛbea ti wɔ Harare wɔ Morgan Tsvangirai House no.
Eyi bae bere a MDC kuw a Awuraa Thokozani Khupe di wɔn anim kyeree mfinimfini no.
Mfeɛ mmienu a atwam ni no, Asɛnnibea Kunini no abɔ Awuraa Khupe soboɔ sɛ ɔnyɛ adwuma wɔ Morgan Tsvangirai wu akyi.
Polisifoɔ a wɔda afiase no bi ne Chamisa asoafoɔ mmienu, Tendai Biti ne Lynett Karenyi Kore ne David Chimhini, Lovemore Chinoputsa, Gladys Hlatywayo ne afoforɔ.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ nneduafoɔ yi nam kwan so rekɔ amanyɔkuo no adwumayɛbea ti, baabi a na polisifoɔ atwa wɔn ho ahyia.
Studi7 ntumi ntee nnipa dodow a wɔakyere wɔn afi polisifo nkyɛn, na soboɔ a wɔabɔ wɔn sɛ polisi kasamafoɔ a wɔfrɛ no Paul Nyathi no, na ɛnyɛ ne tɛlɛfon so.
Chamisa kasamafo, Fatzai Mahere, kae sɛ kyere a wɔkyeree no no maa ne ho dwiriw no.
Tebea a ɛwɔ MDC no mu yɛ den bere a Asɛnnibea Kunini bi buu atɛn afe yi sɛ Chamisa ne Awuraa Khupe mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no nni amanyɔ mmara mu, na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no berɛ a Awuraa Khupe yɛ ɔsoafoɔ panin no.
Wɔ atemmu no akyi no, Awuraa Khupe yii mmarahyɛbɛdwafie ne mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu nnipa baanan adi sɛ nkurɔfo no nnyina wɔn amanyɔkuo no ananmu.
Wɔn a wɔayi wɔn adi ne Thabitha Khumalo, Prosper Mutseyami, Lilian Timveous ne Charlton Hwende.
Zimbabwefo binom a wɔwɔ aman ahodoɔ mu se wɔhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔmfi ɔman no mu esiane Robert Mugabe a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔde akuma na ɛredi adeɛ no nti.
Amanyɔsɛm ho ɔbenfo bi a ɔkyerɛ ade wɔ Bergen Sukuupɔn a ɛwɔ Norway, ne Zimbabwe Yibuya / Mayibuye Zimbabwe ahyehyɛde no muni, Dr. Victor Chimhutu ka sɛ ɛwom sɛ na wobu Owura Mugabe sɛ ɔka Afrika biakoyɛ ho deɛ, nanso Zimbabwe abusua bi ammu no saa.
Dr Chimhutu se apam a Owura Mugabe ne Afrika akannifo afoforo ayɛ no yɛ nneɛma a ama wanya obu kɛse afi Afrika akannifo hɔ no mu biako.
Wɔka sɛ wɔbɛkae Owura Mugabe nso sɛ wadidi Atɔe famfoɔ no atɛm na wakasa atia aman mpanyimfoɔ te sɛ United States ne Britain.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ, sɛ Zanu PF amanyɔkuo no mufo bu wɔn ani gu ɔsɔretia amanyɔkuo no so anaa wɔkasa tia wɔn mpo a, ɛnyɛ ɔno na ɔhwee wɔn na ɔde wɔn siei.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛma Owura Mugabe ahome Kwasida, ɛwom sɛ wonnya nhuu baabi a ɔwɔ de.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ ne ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ aban ayaresabea ahodoɔ aka akyerɛ aban sɛ sɛ wɔantua wɔn ka ansa na December aba awieɛ a, wɔbɛgyae adwuma no ɔsram a ɛreba no mfiaseɛ.
Ɔmampanyin a ɔda Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Fekuw ano, Fortune Nyamande a ɔkaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛdeɛ no ka Zimbabwe Ayarehwɛfoɔ Fekuw no ho no kyerɛw krataa kɔmaa aban sɛ wɔrekɔ.
Ɔbenfoɔ Nyamande kaa sɛ ɔkyerɛw kɔɔ aban nkyɛn sɛ efi January 1 afe a ɛreba no.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔne ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ aban ayaresabea ahodoɔ ayɛ saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi esiane akwantuo ho ka a wɔnnya nnya nnyaa wɔn ɔsram akatua ne ɛka a aban hyɛɛ bɔ sɛ wɔbɛtua nti.
Oduruyɛfo Nyamande nso kasa tiaa sɛnea aban de nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfo di dwuma de bu atesɛm nkrataa a wɔde di dwuma no animtiaa.
Sikasɛm Soafoɔ Patrick Chinamasa abɔ amanneɛ dedaw sɛ aban ntumi ntua n’adwumayɛfoɔ bi ka afe yi esiane sɛ wɔnni sika nti.
Dr. Nyamande kaa sɛ, “Mr Chinamasa de atesɛm nkrataa abɔ yɛn akatua mu nsakraeɛ no ho amanneɛ, enti yɛbɛfa akwan korɔ no ara so.”
Wɔabɔ agumadi akyerɛfoɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔtua wɔn ka Dwoda no amanneɛ Benada nanso wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ ɔmanfoɔ, a nnuruyɛfoɔ ne ayarehwɛfoɔ ka ho, bɛnya wɔn ka January 5 afe a ɛreba no.
Nanso aban adwumayɛfo pii a wɔne Studi 7 kasae no kae sɛ wonni ahotoso sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka wɔn sika wɔ bere foforo no mu.
Yɛantumi ne Akwahosan Soafoɔ, David Parirenyatwa ne Adwumayɛ Soafoɔ, Priscah Mupfumira anhu akwan a wɔbɛfa so abɔ wɔn ho ban.
Ɔsɔretiafoɔ panin MDC amanyɔkuo no nwiinwii sɛ polisifoɔ rehunahuna emufoɔ.
Zimbabwe Mmaranimfoɔ a ɔhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ so no se nnansa yi wɔakyere nnipa 47, a wɔn mu fã kɛse no ara yɛ MDC akyitaafoɔ ne adesuafoɔ foforɔ baason a wɔwɔ Allen Wilson Sukuu mu wɔ Harare sɛ wɔkasa tia mmara.
Wɔn a wɔda afiase no bi ne Makomborero Haruzivishe, a kan no na ɔyɛ ZINASU sukuu panin a ɔne ne yɔnko Allan Moyo kɔɔ asɛnnibea nnɛ no.
Yɛantumi ankɔ polisi kasamafoɔ, Abɛɛfo Kwankyerɛfoɔ panin Paul Nyathi nkyɛn efisɛ wɔannya wɔn fon no ho mmuaeɛ.
Mmaranimfo Innocent Gonese, MDC mmaranimfoɔ, kaeɛ sɛ Haruzivishe ne Moyo bɛsan akɔ asɛnnibea Dwoada abɛsusu asɛnnibea no gyinaesi no ho.
Amanaman Nkabom Wiase Nyinaa Akwahosan Ahyehyɛde (WHO) aka akyerɛ China sɛ corona ɔyare mmoawa a akunkum nnipa 233 wɔ China no abɛyɛ ɔyaredɔm a abu so wɔ wiase nyinaa.
Nnanu a atwa mu no, wobu akontaa sɛ nnipa bɛyɛ 2,000 na wɔanya corona ɔyare mmoawa no bi, na nnipa 9,800 na wɔanya bi wɔ aman 244 mu wɔ wiase nyinaa.
WHO panin a wɔfrɛ no Dr Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus kaa sɛ ɛwom sɛ na wɔwɔ ahotoso sɛ China rebɔ mmɔden asiw yareɛ no ano deɛ, nanso na wosuro sɛ sɛ ɛtrɛw kɔ wiase afã foforɔ a, ɛbɛtumi akunkum nnipa pii.
Akwahosan Soafoɔ Dr Obadiah Moyo se Zimbabwe resɔ nnipa bɛboro 200 a wɔfi China anaa aman a wɔanya komayare mmoawa no ahwɛ.
Nnipa a wɔreyɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ Zimbabwe no de nnafua 14 na ɛda wɔn fie.
Kan akwahosan soafoɔ Dr. Henry Madzorera se Zimbabwe hia sika pii na ɔde abɔ ɔyareɛ no ho ban.
Kan ɔmampanyin Robert Mugabe amu bɛba Harare Wukuda awia na wɔabɔ n’ayi ho amanneɛ.
Ɔmanpanin nhyiamu bi akyi no, Awuraa Monica Mutsvangwa a ɔyɛ Amanneɛbɔ Soafoɔ no na ɔde too dwa.
Awuraa Mutsvangwa kaa sɛ aban boayikuo ahodoɔ resiesie wɔn ho ama Owura Mugabe ayie.
Bere a wobisaa no nea enti a egyee bere tenten ansa na mobɛka Mugabe ayi no ho asɛm no, Mutsvangwa ne Amannɔne Nsɛm Soafoɔ Sibusiso Moyo kaa sɛ ɛyɛ nwonwa sɛ ɔbɛka n’ayi ho nhyehyɛeɛ ho asɛm bere a Mugabe abusua a ɛwɔ Singapore no aba ɔman no mu no.
Ɔkaa sɛ aban no ne Ɔmanpanin Mugabe abusua no nyinaa reyɛ adwuma abom.
Saa berɛ yi mu no, Ɔhene Katizagombo kasamafoɔ, Gibson Jenami kaa sɛ akyinnyegyeɛ biara nni hɔ bio wɔ Mugabe ayie no ho, berɛ a na Aban a Emmerson Mnangagwa di wɔn anim no na ɛdi kan wɔ saa dwumadie yi mu.
Saa berɛ yi ara mu no, wɔbɛma Ɔsahene Kɛseɛ Trust Mugoba a ɔno nso wuiɛ nnawɔtwe a atwa mu no ahome Wukuada wɔ heroes Acre amusie mu wɔ Harare.
Wɔ nsɛm foforɔ mu no, aban no se basabasayɛ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ South Africa no aka Zimbabwefoɔ 178, na Zimbabwefoɔ mmienu na wɔawuwu wɔ basabasayɛ no mu.
Moyo kaa sɛ aban no reyɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ ɔde wɔn a wɔn ho aka no bɛba fie na wɔde amu no akɔ.
Aban kyerɛ nso sɛ akwahosan adwumayɛfoɔ, a nnuruyɛfoɔ ka ho, atua wɔn mfasoɔ ɔha mu nkyem 60 aka ho, na ɛnnɛ aban asi gyinaeɛ sɛ apɔmuden ne sikasɛm ho adwumayɛfoɔ no bɛtena aseɛ ahwɛ ahu sɛ wɔbɛtua adwumayɛfoɔ no ka yie.
Akwahosan Soafoɔ Dr Obadiah Moyo aka sɛ ɔbɛtena ɔman no sikasɛm asoeɛ mu ahwɛ sɛ ɔbɛdi ɔman no tirimbɔ so.
Nnuruyɛfo kɔɔ so yɛɛ basabasa dapɛn a etwaam no nwiinwii sɛ wɔn akatua sua dodo.
Ahyehyɛde bi a wɔtee sɛ wɔde bɛhyɛ nnipa ahofadi ho nkuran, ne kan Occupy Africa Unity Square kannifo Itai Dzamara, Itai Dzamara, a ɔyɛ Amanaman Ntam Mmea Da no fã nnɛ.
Wɔyɛɛ dwumadi no wɔ Highfield, baabi a wɔmaa mmea ne mmeawa a wɔbaa dwumadi no ase no nneɛma a wɔde bedi dwuma, nneɛma a wɔde siesie wɔn ho ne nea ɛkeka ho.
Dzamara abusua no kasamafoɔ a ɔno nso yɛ Itai Dzamara Ahotosoɔ panin, Owura Partson Dzamara ka kyerɛɛ studio 7 sɛ ɔhuu sɛ ɛfata sɛ ɔda ɔdɔ adi kyerɛ mmea ɔsram yi, ɔsram a ne nuabarima Itai yeraa mfeɛ anum a atwam no.
Ɔkaa sɛ, ɛwom sɛ na ne nua no de ne ho ahyɛ amanyɔsɛm, hokwan a nnipa wɔ ne sɛnkyerɛw mu de, nanso ɔdɔ nti na ɔyɛɛ ne nyinaa na Itai Dzamara Ahyehyɛde no bɛkɔ so ada ayamye adi akyerɛ no.
Ɔkaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛde no ayɛ adwuma wɔ Highfields akuraa no ase, efisɛ ɛhɔ na wɔwoo Itai nanso ɔkaa sɛ wɔbɛkɔ mmea ne ahiafo nkyɛn akɔboa wɔn a wɔwɔ nimdeɛ ne osuahu wɔ nneɛma pii mu te sɛ mmara, nhomasua ne akwahosan.
Wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ nnɛyi dwumadi no mu bi ne Rememberance Zuze a ɔkaa sɛ ɛwom sɛ wonnya nhuu Owura Dzamara deɛ, nanso n’ani agye ahyehyɛde no nneyɛe a ɛhyɛ n’asetra ho nkuran no ho.
Abeawa bi a wɔammɔ ne din ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ wanya mfaso pii nnɛ.
Ne nyinaa mu no, Partson Dzamara abɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ ne nuabarima mfirihyia nnum mmerɛ a nnipa a wonnim wɔn a wɔwɔ Glen View kyeree no Benada wɔ Harare.
Ɔkaa saa de besi nnɛ no, na wonnim baabi a ne nua no wɔ anaa sɛ ɔte ase.
Ɔkaa sɛ polisifo, wɔn a wɔsɔre tia hokwan a nnipa wɔ, Zimbabwe Nnipa Ahofadi Asoeɛ ne afoforo a wɔne Itai Dzamara yɛɛ adwuma no ka wɔn a wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ wɔn baa dwumadie no ase no ho.
Bere a wiase no di aguanfo da ɔkyena no, Zimbabwefo bi a wɔte South Africa sɛ aguanfo no ka sɛ biribiara nni hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ wodi sɛnea South Africa wɔ ahohia mu no.
Zimbabwefo binom ka sɛ South Africa nkyerɛ obu mma nhyehyɛeɛ a wɔne ahyehyɛde ahodoɔ te sɛ Amanaman Nkabom ayɛ wɔ atubrafoɔ ahofadi ho no.
Zimbabwe Migrant Support Network kyerɛwfoɔ panin, Shelton Chi Yangwa, ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ ɛwom sɛ aguanfoɔ da no ho hia deɛ, nanso wɔkyeree South Africa aguanfoɔ.
Chi Yangwa kaa sɛ Zimbabwe abusua a ɛwɔ South Africa no nso ne nnipa atitiriw a wohuu amane.
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ na n’ahyehyɛde no ne Zimbabwefo ne aman foforo reyɛ adwuma de aboa wɔn ma wɔn nsa aka akwantu nkrataa
Zimbabwe Exemption Permits Gladys Mangwende a ɔyɛ abadiakyire no kaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛde no ani gye aguanfo adwene nhyehyɛe no ho nanso na ɛhaw adwene wɔ hokwan a nnipa nni ho.
Nnipa Ahofadi Ɔwɛn a ɛwɔ Afrika Atifi fam, Dewa Mavhinga, se aguanfoɔ da no ho hia wɔ South Africa sɛnea Zimbabwefoɔ pii te sɛ aguanfoɔ no.
Owura Mavhinga kɔɔ so hyɛɛ South Africa aban no nkuran sɛ ɔmfa mmara no nyɛ adwuma, titiriw wɔ baabi a atubrafoɔ wɔ no.
Zimbabweani foforo a wɔfrɛ no George Manyika nso gyinaa Mavhinga asɛm no akyi.
Gabriel Shumba, a ɔyɛ Zimbabwe Exiles Forum no panin no akɔ Amanaman Nkabom, AU ne SADC nkyɛn sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ sɛnea SA ne aguanfo di nsɛm, titiriw Zimbabwefo.
Agyata no san srɛɛ Aaron Motseledi a ɔyɛ South Africa ɔsoafoɔ a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ɔman no mu sɛ ɔnka n’adwumayɛbea mmara no nkyerɛ wɔn sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛho nhia sɛ aguanfoɔ bɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛnya nkrataa.
Ɔhyɛɛ nnipa ahofadi akuw nkuran sɛ wɔne n’ahyehyɛde no nyɛ adwuma na wɔnko mma atubrafoɔ nyinaa.
Aguanfoɔ no mu baako a wɔfrɛ no Francis Mukono kaa sɛ wammu aguanfoɔ da no sɛ ɛho nhia sɛnea ɛyɛ den ma wɔn wɔ South Africa.
Ɔkɔmfo foforo a wɔfrɛ no Steven Chiweshe nso kae sɛ onnim adewia no.
Mandela Madumise, South Africa kwankyerɛfoɔ panin a ɔhwɛ aguanfoɔ nsɛm so no kaa sɛ n’adwumakuo no akɔ Amanaman Nkabom Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa wɔ so sɛ wɔmmoa wɔn mma wɔnni ɔhaw ahodoɔ a wɔrehyia wɔ asoeɛ hɔ no ho dwuma.
Ɔsram a ɛdi hɔ no awiei no, Maame kae sɛ, n’adwumayɛbea no behu nea ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ de di saa nsɛm yi ho dwuma.
Wobu akontaa sɛ Zimbabwefo bɛboro ɔpepem abiɛsa aguan afi South Africa akɔ South Africa, na wɔabɔ aban no sobo sɛ wɔateetee wɔn.
Nanso Zimbabwe aban se nnipa bi aguan akɔ nkuraase akɔhwehwɛ adidibea papa.
Ayaresabea adwumayɛfoɔ, a ayarehwɛfoɔ ne nnuruyɛfoɔ ka ho, de bɛboro nnafua 33 ayɛ adwuma, na wɔka sɛ wɔn akatua nnɔɔso sɛ wɔbɛkɔ adwuma a wɔnni anidasoɔ biara.
Tebea no mu ayɛ den wɔ ɔmanfo ayaresabea ahorow, na wɔde ayarefo binom kɔ fie a wɔnsa wɔn yare.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ tebea a ɛwɔ ayaresabea ahorow mu no bɛsɛe koraa bere a Senior Health Doctors Association de ato dwa dedaw sɛ, sɛ nnuruyɛfo nkumaa ne mpanyimfo no ansiesie wɔn sikasɛm ne wɔn haw ahorow a, wɔn nso bɛkɔ so ayɛ saa ara. Oduruyɛfo Aaron Musara a ɔyɛ ayaresabea ahorow no kasamafo no ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ nneɛma nkɔ yiye wɔ ayaresabea ahorow no mu.
Ɛwom sɛ na Oduruyɛfo Musara aka akyerɛ aban sɛ wabɔ ne tirim sɛ ɔbɛfa nkrataa so akɔ adwumayɛbea ahodoɔ no deɛ, nanso wannya mmuaeɛ.
Ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ aban ayaresabea ahodoɔ nkɔ adwuma, na wɔrehyɛ aban sɛ ɔmfa US sika a wɔnyaeɛ wɔ October 2018 mu no ntua wɔn ka na ɔmma wɔn nneɛma a ɛbɛbɔ wɔn ho ban afi yareɛ ho berɛ a wɔwɔ adwuma no.
Zimbabwe Ayarehwɛ Fekuw no titrani, ZINA, Enock Dongo, se ɔkasa a ɔne aban no bɔ no yɛ abirekyi ti.
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Nkabom Kuo (ZHDA) kasamafoɔ Dr Tapiwa Mungifa nso kaa sɛ ayarefoɔ a aban nsa wɔn yareɛ no ama ayarefoɔ nni ayaresa.
Owura Mungofa kae nso sɛ berɛ a mmofra ayarehwɛfoɔ no kɔɔ so yɛɛ basabasa no, na wɔn mu bebree wɔ fie sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a COVID-19 remma wɔn ho so.
Nhwehwɛmu dwumadie a ɛtɔ so nson no antumi antie aban nsɛm a ɛfa apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ ho no, berɛ a kan akwahosan soafoɔ Ɔbenfoɔ Amon Murwira antie ne frɛ a ɔfrɛɛ no wɔ fon so no.
Nanso nnawɔtwe a etwaam no, Owura Murwira bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ ɔne ɔyarehwɛfo bi afi nkɔmmɔbɔ ase. Ne nanmusini John Mangwiro nso ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ wonni adagyew koraa a wɔde bɛkasa.
Apɔmuden Adwumayɛfoɔ panin, Dr. Paulinus Sikosana nso kaa sɛ wɔakɔ nhyiamu wɔ COVID-19 nsanyareɛ no ho ma enti wɔantumi ne yɛn ankasa.
Akwahosan ho abenfoɔ nso kyerɛ sɛ sɛ aban anka ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔresan akɔ wɔn adwuma ho asɛm ankyerɛ wɔn na wamma nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔhwɛ mmofra no annyae sɛ wɔbɛgya wɔn ho atuo, ɛnkanka seesei a COVID-19 yareɛ no akunkum nnipa 25 deɛ ɛwɔ ɔman no mu.
Chinhoyi Kuropɔn mu Bagua no se wayɛ krado sɛ ɔbɛdi asɛm a Asɛnnibea Kɛseɛ no de too dwa Dwoda sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ bagua no san sisi adan a ɛsɛee no wɔ kuropɔn no mu no so.
Berɛ a ɔne aguadifoɔ a Chinhoyi bagua no sɛee wɔn adan no rekasa no, Abel Gotora, a ɔyɛ bagua no kyerɛwfoɔ no kaa sɛ wɔbɛdi ahyɛdeɛ a asɛnnibea no de ama wɔn sɛ wɔnsi adan a aguadifoɔ bi asɛe no no so.
Nanso Owura Gotora kaa sɛ ɛnyɛ adan a wɔasɛe no nyinaa na bagua no bɛsan asi, na mmom adan a asɛnnibea kɛse no hyɛ maa nnipa baasia a wɔde bagua no kɔɔ asɛnnibea no nkutoo.
Tafadzwa Marimo, Emmanuel Ngwaru, Richard Svosve, Pepukayi Marega ne Devis Shopo ka wɔn a wɔde Chinhoyi kɔɔ asɛnnibea no ho.
Nnipa baasia no mu baako a wɔfrɛ no Emmanuel Gwaru kaa sɛ ɔde anigyeɛ kɛseɛ penee asɛnnibea atɛn no so berɛ a aban no aka akyerɛ mmaranimfoɔ sɛ wɔnsiesie mpɔtam hɔ nko na ɛnyɛ adan a wɔresɛe no.
Owura Gwaru kaa sɛ n’awerɛhosɛm a ɛsen biara no mu biako ne sɛ na ɔretua sika ama bagua no sɛ wɔmfa nsisi adan. Nanso wɔkyerɛ sɛ MDC akyitaafoɔ a wɔkyeree wɔn no botaeɛ ne sɛ wɔbɛkasa atia amanyɔkuo no mansoɔ a ɛwɔ ɔman no nyinaa mu no.
Sikhala a wɔkyeree no ɔsram a etwaam no berɛ a wɔbɔɔ no soboɔ sɛ wabɔ pɔ sɛ ɔbɛsɛe Emmerson Mnangagwa aban no, ɔka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ nnipa pii reguan afi wɔn afie sɛ wɔmpɛ sɛ wɔkyere wɔn.

MDC no pɛ sɛ wɔkasa tia wɔ nkurow akɛseɛ mu wɔ ɔman no mu nanso polisifoɔ de wɔn ho rehyɛ Ɔmanfoɔ Ahyɛdeɛ ne Ahobammɔ Mmara no mu sɛ wɔmmara amanyɔkuo no sɛ ɔntoa n’asɛm no so.
Polisifo abara MDC no sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔsɔre tia Harare, Bulawayo, Gweru ne Masvingo.
Amanyɔsɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo kyerɛ sɛ eyi betumi asi wɔ Mutare baabi a MDC ayɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ wɔbɛyɛ ɔsɔretia no Yawda no.
Asɛnnibea Kɛseɛ no ayi Ɔtemmufoɔ Ziyambi Ziyambi ne Sikasɛm Soafoɔ Mthuli Ncube afi MDC-T a Thokozani Khupe di anim wɔ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie sikasɛm mmara ase.
Asɛnnibea Kɛseɛ Temmufoɔ Priscilla Munangati Manongwa buu atɛn Yawda sɛ ɔde asɛm too Ziyambi ne Ncube anim sɛ wɔmfa MDC-T akuw a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔyɛ amanyɔkuo a wɔwɔ hokwan sɛ wɔyɛ amanyɔkuo wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie ase.

Chamisa MDC - T kasamafo abadiakyire, Luke tamborinyoka kaa sɛ n’ani agye atemmuo no ho.
Nanso Morgen Komichi a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no guamtenani a ɔredi Asɛnnibea Kunini atɛmmuo a ɛse Chamisa nnii amanyɔkuo no amanyɔ mmara so sɛ ɔmmɛyɛ MDC kannifoɔ no kaa sɛ ɔbɛfa akwan bi so anya sika no sɛ amanyɔkuo no panin.
Nanso Owura tamborinyoka kaa sɛ ɔwɔ sika no berɛ a MDC Mmarahyɛbɛdwani no de ne din kɔɔ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no.
Nanso Komichi kae sɛ Owura Chamisa ne afoforo nni mmara no so.
Harare mmaranimfoɔ Kudzai Kadzere kaa sɛ nnafua du ntam no, wɔbɛtumi de asɛm no akɔdan asɛnnibea.
Ziyambi nam telefon so ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔkasa tia atɛmmuo no sɛnea asɛnnibea no hyɛeɛ no a, wɔn nso bɛtumi de wɔn nkrataa akɔ asɛnnibea wɔ nnafua du ntam.
Yɛne Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie kasamafoɔ, Jacob Mudenda, anaa Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ sikasɛm so no nkasaeɛ sɛnea wɔabɔ ne din wɔ asɛnnibea nkrataa mu no.
Mmara ho abenfo bi kyerɛ sɛ asɛnnibea no hyɛɛ mmara sɛ, sɛ wɔannye Chamisa MDC asɛm no antom a, asɛnnibea no betumi ayɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔde sika no bɛkɔ Chamisa MDC.
Ɛnyɛ eyi ne bere a edi kan a MDC ako ama saa sika yi.

Akatua no kyerɛ sɛ mmea a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa da akokoduru adi, na United States Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Amanaman Ntam Nkitahodie so na ɛde ama.
Oduruyɛfo Nyampinga kaa sɛ wansusuw da sɛ ɔbɛnya nidi a ɛte saa, na ɔkae sɛ n’ani agye sɛ wɔahu ɔne mmea foforo 11 a wofi wiase afanan nyinaa.
Oduruyɛfo Nyampinga se wɔbɛtu kwan akɔ United States mmeae ahorow akosua afiase tebea ho ade sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi ahyɛ wɔn adwuma mu den wɔ fie.
Oduruyɛfo Nyampinga se egye akokoduru na wɔn ani agye sɛ afoforo ahu adwuma a wɔreyɛ wɔ fie no.
Bere a ɔrekasa wɔ dwumadie no ase no, Ɔman Soafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Amanaman Ntam Nkitahodie so, Michael Pompeo kaa sɛ adwuma a mmea 12 no reyɛ no yɛ fɛ na ɛhwehwɛ sɛ wonya akokoduru.
Wofii dwumadi no ase mfeɛ 14 a atwam ni.
Mmea foforo a wɔanya saa abasobɔdeɛ yi ne Afghanistan, Armenia, Azerbaijan, Bolivia, Burkino Faso, Kazakhstan, Malaysia, Nicaragua, Pakistan, Syria, Yemen ne Zimbabwe.
Owura Pompey kaa sɛ dwumadie a ɛtete saa no ho hia efisɛ ɛmaa mmea nyaa hokwan yɛɛ adwuma maa afoforɔ a wɔwɔ wiase nyinaa.
Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ dwumadie no ase no, ɔbaa a ɔdi kan wɔ United States, Melania Trump, kaa sɛ n’ani gye adwuma a mmea reyɛ wɔ wiase nyinaa no ho.
Ɔkae sɛ efi bere a edi kan a wohyiaa mmea a wɔapaw wɔn sɛ wonnye wɔn ntom mfe anan a atwam ni no, wɔakɔ so ahyia mmea a wɔreyɛ adwuma pa wɔ wiase nyinaa ɛwom sɛ wɔn mu binom yɛ saa nnwuma yi na wɔhyia ɔhaw nanso wɔda so ara yɛ saa de.
Oduruyɛfo Nyampinga se ɔfii n’adwuma ase sɛ obi a ɔhwehwɛ hokwan a nnipa wɔ mu mfeɛ aduasa a atwam ni.

Aban no ahyɛ mmara sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ hyɛntiafoɔ fa nnipa wɔ Covid-19 ɔyaredɔm no mu sɛ ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so asiw ɔyare mmoawa no ano, na ɔkyerɛ sɛ bɔs ahodoɔ a ZUPCO wɔ no nkutoo na ɛsɛ sɛ ɛsoa akwantufoɔ.

Adwumayɛ Fekuw a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe (ABuz) Victor Nyoni, a ɔyɛ ɔpanyin no kaa sɛ, saa dwumadie yi ama nnipa bebree adwuma asɛe, efisɛ na wɔn mu binom hia nsu na wɔatumi ayɛ wɔn da biara da dwumadi ahodoɔ.
Owura Nyoni kaa sɛ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mpanyimfoɔ a ɔhyiaa wɔn no ama no awerɛhyɛ sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ nsuo kwan nnawɔtwe a ɛreba no mfiaseɛ, berɛ a mmarahyɛbɛdwafie hwɛ kwan sɛ ebedu nnawɔtwe no awieeɛ no.

Wɔkyerɛ sɛ eyi nso fi nsu a ɛso retew wɔ Criterion ne Magwegwe nsu fibea titiriw a ɛwɔ kuropɔn mu ne anyinam ahoɔden dwumadibea a ɛwɔ nsu a wɔde popa nsu no.

Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Kuo a ɛgyina nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔn ho yɛ nwonwa ananmu no kaa sɛ ɛretwɛn sɛ Ɔmanpanin Emmerson Mnangagwa bɛte wɔ nhyiamu a ɔne n’ananmusifoɔ yɛeɛ Wukuada no akyi.
Dɔkota Prince Butau a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ nhyiamu yi ase no kaa sɛ ɔrehwɛ kwan sɛ obetie Owura Mnangagwa asɛm Yawda anaa Fida biara.
Owura Mnangagwa a na ɔrefi hɔ no san bae ntɛm ara sɛ ɔrebɛbɔ mmɔden asiesie nnuruyɛfoɔ no.
Nneɛma a ɛwɔ ɔmanfo ayaresabea nyinaa ayɛ basaa fi bere a nnuruyɛfo kɔɔ so yɛɛ saa wɔ December 1 afe a etwaam no.
Nanso ɔpanyin a ɔda Community Working Group on Health ano, Owura Itai Rusike, kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aban no di ɔhaw no ho dwuma ntɛm so na ɔma nnuruyɛfo sika a ɛbɛbɔ wɔn ho ban afi ntɛtea ano a wɔbɛfa ho.
Zimbabwefoɔ bi a wɔwɔ South Africa akasa atia wɔ Groote Schuur Ayaresabea a ɛwɔ Cape Town, baabi a wɔrehwɛ Ɔmanpanin abadiakyire Constantino Chiwenga, na wɔrehyɛ Chiwenga sɛ ɔnsan nkɔ ayaresabea a ɛwɔ hɔ no nkɔsa no yareɛ.
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔpamoo Owura Chiwenga fii ɔman no mu dapɛn awiei kɔhwɛɛ no wɔ South Africa, ɛwom sɛ Studi 7 annya adanse biara a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔwɔ South Africa ayaresabea a ɛso sen biara no de.
Nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ soafoɔ Monica Mutsvangwa ne nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ soafoɔ Nick Mangwana ampene so sɛ ɔbɛma asɛm no ho mmuaeɛ Kwasida berɛ a Voice Study 7 kɔɔ Zimbabwe no. Ɔhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnkyere George Charamba.
Nanso Studi 7 ankɔ Charamba nkyɛn anhu sɛ ɛyɛ nokware sɛ Chiwenga yare na wɔrehwɛ no wɔ ayaresabea hɔ anaa.
Zimbabweani foforo a wɔfrɛ no Carlos Chimbi a ɔte Cape Town kɔkaa Zimbabwefo afoforo ho wɔ ɔsatu no mu.
Chimbi kaa sɛ, “ɛyɛɛ no yaw paa” sɛ ɔmampanyin abɛdiakyire no abu hokwan a nnipa a wɔadi dɛm wɔ ɔman no mu no so, efisɛ na onim sɛ sɛ ɔyare a ɔbɛkɔ akɔhwehwɛ ayaresa wɔ amannɔne.
Ɔkae sɛ n’ani agye sɛ otumi de n’asɛm no kɔɔ ayaresabea hɔ sɛnea ayaresabea no panyin aka akyerɛ no sɛ ɔne no nkasa no, ɛwom sɛ wanka sɛ Owura Chiwenga wɔ ayaresabea hɔ anaa ɔnkae de.
Chimbi kae sɛ ayaresabea panyin no aka akyerɛ no sɛ mmara mma no kwan sɛ ɔnka ayarefo a sɛ wɔnni ayaresabea hɔ a wɔbɛba ayaresabea hɔ no ho asɛm.
Afe a etwaam no, Chiwenga hyɛɛ nkurɔfo abufuw bere a nnuruyɛfo kɔɔ so yɛɛ adwuma, na ɔkae sɛ wɔnyɛ adwumayɛfo a wɔn ho akokwaw, na mmom wɔyɛ adwumayɛfo mpapahwekwa, ne sɛ aban no nyɛɛ nhyehyɛe biara mfa nnii ɔhaw ahorow a ɛwɔ ayaresabea ahorow a ɛmma nkurɔfo nnya ayaresa pa no ho dwuma.
Groote Schurr Ayaresabea yɛ nea wonim no yiye sɛ ɛno ne komayare ayaresa a edi kan wɔ wiase.
Polisifo abara MDC amanyɔkuo no sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ amanneɛbɔ bi ɔkyena berɛ a wɔhwɛɛ kwan sɛ amanyɔkuo no kannifo, Nelson Chamisa bɛbɔ ne amanyɔkuo no akwankyerɛ ne nhyehyɛeɛ ama afe yi no.
Berɛ a ɔrekasa wɔ amanyɔkuo no Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie nhyiamu ase wɔ Harare no, MDC kasamafoɔ abɛdiakyire, Luke tamborinyoka kaa sɛ polisifoɔ abara mmarahyɛbɛdwafie adwuma no, na ɔkaa sɛ wɔn ani abere rebue sukuu ahodoɔ.
Tamborinyoka kaa sɛ wɔrenyɛ nhyiamu yi ɔkyena efisɛ na MDC pɛ sɛ n’akyitaafoɔ kwati sɛ polisifoɔ bɛhwe wɔn anaa wɔbɛtow ahyɛ wɔn so.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɛda adi pefee sɛ polisifoɔ rebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtow ahyɛ amanyɔkuo no akyitaafoɔ so sɛnea wɔyɛeɛ berɛ a amanyɔkuo no bɔɔ pɔ sɛ wɔbɛsɔre atia wɔ nkuro ne nkuro a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa mu no.
Ɔkaa sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nhyiamu a ɛfa 2020 dwumadie ho no wɔ Awuraa Musodzi Hall wɔ Mbare na wɔbɛyɛ no Benada nnawɔtwe a ɛdi hɔ no wɔ baabi a wɔbɛbɔ amanneɛ akyiri yi.
Owura tamborinyoka kaa sɛ MDC no abrɛ sɛ wobu no sɛ amumɔyɛfoɔ ahyehyɛdeɛ na ɔresusuw ho sɛ ɔbɛkɔ so adi mmara no so anaasɛ ɔbɛsesa ne nhyehyɛeɛ.
Yɛante sɛ Zimbabwe Republic Polisifo, ZRP kasamafo, Asoafoɔ panin abɛdiakyire Paul Nyathi rete sɛ wɔn telefon a wokura kyin no nyɛ adwuma.
Amanyɔsɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo Masimba Kuchera ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ ɔte nka sɛ polisifo rehunahuna MDC man no.
Afe a etwaam wɔ August mu no, ZRP baraa MDC sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ɔsɔretia wɔ nkuropɔn ne nkurow a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa mu. Wɔkae sɛ osuro sɛ ɔsɔretia no bɛkɔ akowie basabasayɛ mu sɛnea ɛkɔɔ so wɔ January mu no.
Wɔapaw Etiopiani Ɔman soafoɔ panin Abiy Ahmed sɛ ɔmma wɔn Nobel Asomdwoeɛ Akyɛdeɛ a ɛbɛba afe yi. Norway de saa abasobɔdeɛ yi ma.
Wɔkamfoo Ahmed sɛ ɔde asomdwoe aba ne man ne Eritrea ntam wɔ mfe 20 akodi a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ aman abien no ntam no akyi.
Abibini a odii kan nyaa abasobɔde no ne Albert Luthuli a ofi South Africa wɔ 1960 mu.
Wɔn a wɔde maa wɔn no bi ne Nelson Mandela a ofi South Africa, Anwar Sedat a ofi Egypt ne Kofi Annan a ofi Ghana.
Nnipa foforɔ a wɔdii nkonim no bi ne Ɔsɔfopɔn Desmond Tutu ne Liberia Ɔmanpanin Ellen Johnson Sirleaf ne Wangari Maathai a ɔwɔ Kenya a ɔyɛ obibini a ɔdi kan wɔ Afrika a ɔnyaa abasobɔdeɛ no.
Wɔ Zimbabwe wɔ afe 2011 mu no, wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ Ɔman soafoɔ panin Morgan Tsvangirai sɛ ɔmmɔ nkonim boɔ ɛwom sɛ wantumi.
Ɔbenfo Pedzisayi Ruhanya a ɔyɛ amanyɔsɛm mu nyansahufoɔ wɔ Johannesburg Sukuupɔn mu no se Ɔmanpanin Emmerson Mnangagwa wɔ nneɛma pii a ɛsɛ sɛ osua fi Ahmed akwankyerɛ mu.
Asono ne mmoa foforo pii na ɔkɔm ne nsu rekunkum wɔn wɔ Hwange National Park, na ɛrekanyan aban no ma wayere ne ho atew asono no dodow so.
Wɔ Studi7 nsrahwɛ mu wɔ Hwange National Park mpɔtam no, yehuu asono pii a aduan pa a wonnya nni akunkum wɔn wɔ mmeae bi afe yi.
Zimbabwe Parks and Wildlife Management Authority (ZimParks) kasamafo, Tinashe Farawo ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ asono 85 awuwu fi September na bɛboro 200 awuwu afe yi esiane ɔkɔm nti.
Faraonom kae nso sɛ ɔkɔm no akyi no, nneɛma atitiriw a ekunkum nnipa no mu biako ne aduan ne nsu a ɛho ayɛ na, na ama asono ne mmoa foforo dodow so atew.
Sɛ ɔsono biako redidi a, wɔkyerɛ sɛ ohia aduan bɛboro kilogram 500, na ohia nsu galɔn abien.
Nanso seesei ZimParks bu akontaa sɛ asono bɛboro 45,000 na wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ.
Wɔn a wɔhwehwɛ mmoa ho kwan no bi ka sɛ akontaabu a ZimParks de mae no yɛ atoro, na wɔka sɛ wɔreyɛ eyi sɛ ɔkwan a wɔnam so nya mmoa na ama wɔatumi atɔn asono.
Adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔdɔm asase no, Lenin Chisaira gye tom sɛ ɔkɔm de asono ne mmoa foforɔ a wɔnnya aduan pa nni, nanso ɔyɛ wɔn a wɔtaa ZimParks akyi.
Sɛdeɛ Chisaira kyerɛ no, adeɛ baako a ɛma mmoa ho kɔm de wɔn wɔ Hwange National Park ne gyinaeɛ a aban no asi sɛ ɔbɛma nnipa kwan ma wɔayɛ nneɛma te sɛ fagudeɛtu a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔ mpɔtam hɔ.
Nanso Owura Farawo kaa sɛ adwene a wɔn a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔde mmoa yɛ adwuma no wɔ no haw no, na ɔkaa sɛ wɔmpɛ sɛ wogye nokwasɛm a ɛyɛ sɛ asono ne mmoa foforo renya nkɔanim esiane adwuma pa a ne dwumadibea no reyɛ nti no tom, na ɔde kaa ho sɛ dwumadibea no abue kwan ama obiara a ɔpɛ sɛ ohu mmoa yɛmmea tebea no.
Zimbabwe ne Afrika atifi fam aman foforo, a Botswana ka ho, kyerɛ sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ Amanaman Ntam Nhyiam a ɛfa Aguadi a ɛwɔ Endagered ho no ma wɔn kwan ma wɔtɔn wɔn asono bere a mmoa no dodow anya nkɔanim, na ɛde ɔhaw ahorow pii aba, a nnipa ne mmoa a wɔtow hyɛ nkurɔfo so ka ho.
Afe yi nko ara, ahyehyɛde no mu mmoa akunkum nnipa aduasa abiɛsa.
Wɔ CITES nhyiamu bi ase wɔ Geneva, Switzerland, wɔ August mu no, ahyehyɛde no ampene so sɛ wɔbɛma wɔagyae asono ne wɔn asonse tɔn.
Ɔpanyin a ɔda Akwantuo Asoeɛ a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe ano, Emmanuel Fundira kaa sɛ ɛhia sɛ CITES ne wɔn a wɔhwehwɛ mmoa ho kwan no te ɔhaw ahodoɔ a Zimbabwe ne aman foforɔ rehyia wɔ asono pii a ɛwɔ saa aman yi mu no ase.
Wim tebea ne Nsrahwɛ Soafoɔ, Nqobizitha Ndlovu ka kyerɛɛ studio 7 sɛ aban no rebɔ mmɔden biara sɛ ɔne aman foforɔ bɛyɛ adwuma ama CITES anya adwene foforɔ.
Nanso wɔkae sɛ wobetumi atu akɔ baabi a wɔfrɛ hɔ reservation a ɛbɛma wɔatumi de asono akɔ CITES aman foforo a wɔayɛ saa ara.
Hwange National Park buei wɔ 1928 mu na ɛyɛ ɔman mmoa yɛmmea a ɛso sen biara wɔ ɔman no mu.
Ahyehyɛde no kɛse bɛboro kilomita ahinanan14,000, na bere a wɔhyɛɛ aseɛ no wobu akontaa sɛ asono bɛyɛ 2,000 pɛ na wɔwɔ.
Zimbabwe Footballers Union kyerɛwfoɔ panin, Fuz, Paul Gundani wui Wukuada awia bere a na yareɛ bi abɔ no.
Nanso yennim nea ɛyɛe a nneɛma kɔɔ so.
Sɛdeɛ FUZ kyerɛ no, Gundani wuiɛ wɔ Topomasi Private Hospital a ɛwɔ Kwekwe.
Bɔɔlbɔkuo no san ka sɛ, sɛ wɔgyae bɔɔlbɔ a, ɛbɛyɛ den ama wɔn sɛ wɔbɛtoto mu.
Gundani a kan no na ɔyɛ Zisco Steel bɔɔl maa Mmofra Akofofoɔ no, na ɔbɔɔl maa Akofoɔ no berɛ a na wɔfrɛ kuw no “Dream Team” wɔ Reinard Fabisch a wawie no akwankyerɛ ase.
NSƐM ho amanneɛbɔfo panyin Marlene Gadzirayi kaa sɛ ɛyɛɛ no ahodwiriw sɛ ɔtee sɛ Gundani awu.
“Meda so ara di awerɛhow bere a me ne wɔn kasae nnɛra na yɛreyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ dedaw sɛ yɛbɛyɛ saa adwuma yi. Nanso ɛnnɛ metee sɛ wɔayera, nanso saa bere yi deɛ mennim nea Owura Gundani bɛdi,” Awuraa Gadzirayi ka kyerɛɛ Studio.
Awuraa Gadzirayi se ɔman no ahwere bɔɔlbɔ mu dɔmmarima kɛseɛ. Awuraa Gadzirayi nso kaa sɛ wɔnyɛɛ nhyehyɛeɛ biara sɛ wɔbɛyɛ Owura Gundani ayi bere a na ɔretwɛn sɛ ɔbɛte n’abusuafoɔ nka sɛ ɔbɛgye n’ahome no.
Zimbabwe Football Association (ZIFA) de ato dwa wɔ ne wɛbsaet so sɛ Gundani wu no ama ne werɛ ahow na abusua no bɛgyina n’ayi ho nhyehyɛe nyinaa mu.
Zifa nkitahodie sohwɛfo Xolisani Gwesele kaa sɛ Gundani wu no yɛ ɔman no awerɛhosɛm, na ɛbɛyɛ den sɛ wobenya ɔbarima bi a n’ani gye bɔɔlbɔ ho.
“Asomdwoeɛ nka Paul Gundani,” Gwesela kyerɛwee wɔ Zifa wɛbsaet no so.
Bere a kan Ɔmanpanin Robert Mugabe yere Grace Mugabe yaree no, na wontumi mfa ne funu nkɔ ne fie wɔ Zvimb ɛnnɛ.
Abusuafo binom ka sɛ amu no bɛba Zvimba Dwoda.
Nnipa bɛyɛ 1,000 na wɔretwɛn Ɔmanpanin Mugabe funu da koro wɔ Zvimba awia yi.
Mugabe abusua no kasamafoɔ a ɔno nso yɛ owufoɔ no banana, Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ wɔrenhu Mugabe amu no nnɛ, efisɛ ɔkaa sɛ ɔnnim sɛnea Ɔhene Zvimba somaa no no.
Leo Mugabe kae sɛ amu no bɛba fie anɔpatutuutu.
Nanso Ɔhene Katizagombo a wɔsan frɛ no Gibson Jenami kaa sɛ amu no rensan nkɔ Zvimba sɛnea na wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ ɛbɛyɛ esiane sɛ Awuraa Grace Mugabe yare nti.
Ɔhene Katizagombo nso kaa sɛ nnipadua no bɛhyɛ aban nsa akosi da a wɔde bɛhome.
Nanso eyi ne Leo Mugabe a ɔkaa sɛ n’abusua bɛkora Mugabe amu so akosi sɛ wobewie ɔdamoa a ɛkorɔn mu no bɔ abira.
Adwenem naayɛ a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Ɔmampanyin Mugabe ayi ase no ama nnipa pii ho adwiriw wɔn wɔ sɛ ebia Mugabe amu no bɛba bere a aka bɛyɛ nnafua 30 ma wɔasie no no ho.
Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ Mugabe amu no bɛtena Zvimbar da koro, na afei wasan akɔ Harare akogye n’ahome.
Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ nnipa ahyiam wɔ baabi wɔ Ɔmanpanin Mugabe fie wɔ Harare.
MDC-T ɔsɔretiafoɔ a Nelson Chamisa di n’anim a na wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ ɔno nso bewu wɔ Zvimbase nnɛ, Lloyd Tarubwa a ɔwɔ Banket a wɔkyeree no too afiase asram akron a wɔanni n’asɛm no kaa sɛ wɔaba abɛhwɛ sɛ Ɔmanpanin Mugabe awu ampa.
Sɛnea wɔyɛɛ Owura Mugabe ayi no ama nnipa pii ho adwiriw wɔn wɔ ɔman no mu, na wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔhaw a Owura Mugabe hyiae wɔ ne mmerɛ mu no na ɛma owui.
Owura Mugabe wui wɔ Singapore wɔ September 6 bere a na ɔyare kyɛ no.
Amalgamated Rural Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ Kuo a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe, anaa ARTUZ, se wɔn akannifoɔ, Godfrey Chanda, bɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛkyere no na wɔde no too afiase nnɔnhwere mmienu wɔ Gweru a ɔmanfoɔ nnim.
Nanso, wɔayi Chanda a ɔyɛ ARTUZ boayikuw a ɛwɔ Midlands mantam mu no mu biako no adi berɛ a wɔhyɛɛ no sɛ ɔne agumadi akyerɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ Gweru nkɔ nhyiamu no.
ƆMAMPANYIN Obert Masaraure kaa sɛ woyii Chanda adi bere a wɔn a wɔkyerɛ agumadi wɔ ne nnanu sɔhwɛ ase no kɔɔ so sɔre tiaa nnansa sɔhwɛ no.
Masaraure se nnamfo a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ hɔ no bi nso yɛ ɔkwan titiriw a wɔfa so boa wɔn nkabom.
Ɔyɛkyerɛ no baa awiei Wukuda.
Nanso Masaraure kaa sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nhyiamu bi wɔ ɔsɔretia no akyi de ayɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ wɔbɛyɛ ho biribi.
Yɛantumi ne Adwumayɛ Soafoɔ, Awuraa Sekai Nzenza anhu aban gyinabea wɔ asɛm no ho nanso yɛannya ne telefon a wokura kyin no ho mmuaeɛ.
FC Platinum apue afi Caf Champions League no ama Zimbabwe bɔɔlbɔ ho nsɛmmisa pii asɔre.
Ɛwom sɛ wɔda so ara wɔ agumadi abien wɔ akansi no mu de, nanso FC Platinum ntumi nnyina Esperance a ɔwɔ nɔma awotwe no ano, na saa ara nso na wontumi mmoro Horoya Agumadi Kuw a wɔwɔ nɔma ason no bere a Horoya hwee wɔn wɔ fie ne abɔnten a ɛno ne nea edi kan a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwɛ bere a saa akuw yi awie agumadi no pɛpɛɛpɛ no.
Mprempren, FC Platinum agodie anan no mu biako pɛ na ɔwɔ, enti wɔredi agoru kɛkɛ de awie wɔn agodie a aka no sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a Spencer Mushambadope foforo bɛkyerɛ obu ama wɔn.
Mushambadope se biribiara remfi mu mma wɔn a wɔaka no.
Afe a etwaam no, Angola Mampanyin de August gyaee saa kuw koro no ara wɔ ɔfã a edi kan no mu bere a Lunda hwee wɔn wɔ fie bio no.
Wɔ afe 2017 mu no, Caps United duu akansi no fã ketewaa bi nanso wantumi annu akansi no fã a ɛtɔ so anan no mu bere a Al Ahli Tripoli a ofi Libya hwee no 4 - 2 wɔ fie no.
Afe koro no ara mu no, wɔbɔɔ Ngezi Platinum Nsoromma a na wogyina Zimbabwe ananmu wɔ Kaf Confederation mu no hwee wɔn wɔ ɔfã a edi kan no mu bere a Angolani Libolo hwee wɔn no.
Wɔ afe 2016 mu no, Zanaco a ofi Zambia no hwee Harare City a na ɛwɔ akansi koro no ara mu no wɔ mmirika a edi kan no mu bere a wɔhwee wɔn 2 - 3 wɔ Rufaro Agumadibea na wowiee 3 - 1 wɔ Zambia no.
Eyi kyerɛ sɛ akuw a ɛwɔ hɔ no ntumi nnyina Afrika akuw afoforo akyi sɛnea na ɛte wɔ mfe bi a atwam mu bere a Dynamos si akan wɔ ɔkwan a etu mpɔn so sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobedu Caf Champions League a etwa to wɔ 1998 mu ne nea etwa to wɔ 2008 mu no.
Nea ɛyɛ yaw kɛse ne sɛ FC Platinum wɔ agumadi anan mu nkyerɛkyerɛmu biako pɛ, wɔnnhyɛɛ mu nkyerɛkyerɛmu biako pɛ, bio nso, wɔde agumadi anan mu nkyerɛkyerɛ asia ama.
Asɛmmisa no ne sɛ, sɛ kuw bi reboro akuw a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe no nyinaa na wɔredi agoru te sɛ eyi wɔ Afrika a, dɛn na ɛkyerɛ ma ɔman bɔɔl?
Ɔpanyin a ɔtaa United States akyi, Tinashe Musebi ka sɛ bɔɔl agye nsam araa ma ɛho abehia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakrae pii ansa na Zimbabwe akuw ahodoɔ no atɔ fam asen Lesotho, Botswana ne Swaziland.
Bɔɔlbɔ ho sɛnkyerɛwfo Farai Kambamura se Zimbabwe akuw ntumi nni nkonim wɔ Afrika, efisɛ wɔn a wɔboaa wɔn ma wodii nkonim wɔ Zimbabwe no rekɔ amannɔne, titiriw wɔ South Africa bere a wɔresi akan wɔ Afrika no.
Afe a etwaam no, FC Platinum hweree Gerald Takwara, Elvis Chipezeze ne Talent Chawapiwa afe yi maa Rodwell Chinyafanere a odii nkonim wɔ bɔɔlbɔ mu nkonimdi mu wɔ afe a ɔkɔɔ Baroka no.
Nanso John Chikochi a ɔdii Lengthens bɔɔlbɔkuo no anim wɔ Premier Soccer League mu no kaa sɛ ɛhia sɛ Zimbabwe bɔɔlbɔkuo no tu mpɔn wɔ ɔman no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a bɔɔlbɔkuo no betumi atua sika a ɛbɛma wɔaguan akɔ South Africa ne Zambia.
Mprempren, Zimbabwe wɔ akuw abien pɛ, Castle Lager Premier Soccer League ne Chibuku Super League. Wɔbɔɔ Zifa League afe 2005 mu nea etwa to.
Musa Masepe a ɔpɛ bɔɔl no se Zimbabwe nni bɔɔlbɔ ho nimdeɛ biara bere a wɔn a wɔbɔ bɔɔl no pɛ sɛ wɔto dwom anaa wɔyɛ biribi foforo bere a wɔn akatua wɔ bɔɔlbɔ mu no nni ano.
Sɛ eyi kɔ so a, ebegye bere ansa na akuw a ɛwɔ hɔ no ne Afrika akuw foforo asi akan.
Abatoɔ a wɔde bɛgyina Democratic Party ananmu wɔ US ɔmampanyin abatoɔ mu wɔ November mu no resɔre wɔ kan New York kuropɔn Michael Bloomberg abatoɔ no akyi.
Bloomberg a wabɛyɛ ɔdefo kɛseɛ no antu mmirika amfa annyina ne amanyɔkuo ananmu wɔ ɔmampanyin abatoɔ a ɔmampanyin Donald Trump bɛko no mu.
Owura Bloomberg bɔɔ amanneɛ wɔ November afe a etwaam no mu sɛ ɔde ne ho rehyɛ amanyɔkuo no mu, na ɔsɛee bɛboro dɔla ɔpepem anan wɔ aguade ho dawurubɔ ho.
Ɔdefoɔ yi antu mmirika no wɔ Iowa ne New Hampshire, na saa ara nso na ɔntu mmirika no wɔ Navada ne South Carolina, berɛ a ɔretwɛn March abatoɔ no, berɛ a amantam 14 bɛpaw obi a ɔbɛgyina Democratic Party ananmu wɔ US aban abatoɔ mu.
Bere a Bloomerg de ne nan sii fam sɛ ɔrekɔyɛ adwuma no, wɔn a na wɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no mufo te sɛ Bernie Sanders a ɔgyina Vermont ananmu wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu ne Elizabeth Warren a ɔgyina Massachusetts ananmu wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu no fii ase sɛee Bloomberg kyerɛwtohɔ no.
Bere a Owura Sanders redi kan akasa wɔ Nevada amanyɔkuo anim no, ɔkaa sɛ nea ɛbɛyɛ na ne amanyɔkuo no adi Owura Trump so nkonim no, ɛhia obi a ɔbɛtumi aboa nnipa pii ano asen bere biara wɔ Amerika abakɔsɛm mu.
Owura Sanders kaa sɛ Owura Bloomberg yɛ obi a wonim no yiye wɔ gyinaeɛ a New York kurow sohwɛfoɔ sii sɛ ɔde abibifoɔ bɛto hɔ na wahwehwɛ wɔn, ne Latinosfoɔ a na wɔreyɛ saa wɔ ɔkwan a ɛmfata so. Ɔkaa sɛ saa akwantuo no ntumi mma nnipa pii ntow aba mma Owura Trump wɔ November mu.
Nanso Bloomerg twitwaa Owura Sanders nsɛm no mu, na ɔkae sɛ Owura Sanders a ɔredi nhwehwɛmu no anim no apaw Democratic Party candidate wɔ ɔmampanyin abatoɔ mu a ɔne Owura Trump bɛtra mfeɛ anan a ɛreba no.
Amanyɔsɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo ne Zanu PF panin, Frank Guni, kae sɛ ɛda adi pefee sɛ na ɛda Sanders ne Bloomberg ntam, ɛwom sɛ na ɛda adi pefee sɛ mprempren Sanders wɔ akyitaafo bebree de.
Guni se, wɔ n’adwenem no, ɛsɛ sɛ Sanders ne Bloomberg bom tu mmirika wɔ aban abatoɔ no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛdi Trump so nkonim.
Nnipa bi a wɔwɔ Democratic Party mu se; Barack Obama nanmusini, Joe Biden; Minnesota mmarahyɛ baguani Amy Klobuchar ne kan South Bend kurow sohwɛfo a ɔwɔ Indiana, ne ɔbarima a ɔne mmarima da, Pete Buttigieg.
Ananmusifoɔ 3,979 na wɔwɔ Democratic Amanyɔkuo no mu, na sɛ wɔbɛpaw obi sɛ ɔmfa ne ho nhyɛ amanyɔkuo no abatow ase a, ɛsɛ sɛ ɔwɔ ananmusifoɔ 1,990.
Ananmusifoɔ yi akyi no, ananmusifoɔ a wɔdɔɔso nso wɔ hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a sɛ wɔyɛ Democratic Convention wɔ Wisconsin wɔ July mu a, ananmusifoɔ ne ahwɛfoɔ 4,750 na ɛwɔ hɔ, na ɛsɛ sɛ onipa a wɔreyi no aba wɔ nhyiamu yi ase no nso nya nnipa 2,200. Ananmusifoɔ aduɔson nsia na ɛwɔ hɔ.

Ahyehyɛde no bɔ amanneɛ sɛ nnipa pii a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔanya kokoram no di kan kɔ adwenem ɔyaresafo anaa adwenem ɔyaresafo nkyɛn, na afei wɔkɔ yareɛ a emu yɛ den ho ɔbenfo nkyɛn, na ɛma ɛyɛ den sɛ wɔbɛsa.
Kokoram Fekuw a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe ɔbenfo Priscilla Mangwiro kaa sɛ ɛho hia sɛ nkurɔfo kɔ oduruyɛfo a ɔfata hɔ, sɛ wɔwɔ ɔhaw no bi a.
Awuraa Mangwiro se ɛho hia sɛ wɔyɛ nnipa mu nhwehwɛmu na wɔanya kokoram, titiriw nufu mu kokoram.
Awuraa Mangwiro se nufu mu kokoram ne ade a ɛto so abien a ɛma mmea wuwu wɔ Zimbabwe.
Awuraa Mangwiro se efi October da a ɛhyɛɛ aseɛ sɛ ɔbɛhyɛ October agyiraeɛ sɛ Cancer Awareness Month no, n’ahyehyɛde no asɔ mmea bɛboro aduonum ahwɛ, na nnipa dodoɔ no bɛkɔ so akɔ soro akɔsi ɔsram yi awieɛ.
Bere a ɔtee Zimbabwe Kokoram Fekuw dwumadie no ho asɛm wiei no, ɔbea bi a wɔfrɛ no Gertrude Magwaniza kae sɛ ɔde ne babea kɔhyɛ ne nufu mu.
Awuraa Mangwiro se nneɛma pii na ɛma mmea nya nufu mu kokoram.
Awuraa Mangwiro se ɛhia sɛ wɔhwɛ mmea sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔn nufu bɛsesa, na sɛ ɛba saa a, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwɛ wɔn ntɛm ara.
Awuraa Mangwiro se nnipa pii susuw sɛ sɛ wohu sɛ wanya kokoram a, ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔrewu, nanso nneɛma pii wɔ hɔ a wobetumi ayɛ de aboa mmea ma wɔanyin akyɛ.
Awuraa Mangwiro se nneɛma a ɛde kokoram ba no mu biako ne sradeduan a srade ne asikre wom.
Awuraa Mangwiro rehyɛ mmea nkuran sɛ wɔmfa hokwan a wɔanya sɛ wɔbɛyɛ kokoram mu nhwehwɛmu wɔ October mu no nni dwuma na wɔnkyerɛkyerɛ wɔn ɔyare no ho.

Bere a ɔretie mmarahyɛbɛdwafie adwenkyerɛ bi a ɛfa pɛtro bo ho no, kan Petrotrade panin Godfrey Ncube kaa sɛ, sɛ wɔma nnwumakuo kwan sɛ wɔn ankasa bɛtɔ pɛtro na wɔatɔn no a, ɛnna ɛbɛyɛ yiye.
Owura Ncube gye toom sɛ saa a ɔbɛyɛ no bɛma ne bo akɔ soro, nanso ɔkae sɛ ɛno nkutoo ne ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so ayi fango ho haw a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu bere tenten no afi hɔ.

Abibifo tumidi a ɛbaa hɔ no maa nnipa pii nyaa anidaso sɛ awiei koraa no wɔn nsa bɛka aborɔfo tumidi a aborɔfo de wɔn mu pii guu bun no mu bere a wɔfaa wɔn asase pa no nyinaa no.

Chirisa a ɛbɛyɛ sɛ ɔno nso ne oduruyɛfoɔ panin no kaa sɛ adwuma no adɔɔso ama nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔn mfe akɔ anim, berɛ a nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔn mfe nkɔɔ anim ayɛ adwuma bosome baako no.
Chirisa kae sɛ, sɛ wobetumi ayɛ wɔn adwuma yiye a, ehia sɛ nnuruyɛfo nkumaa ne wɔn yɛ adwuma.
Owura Chirisa kaa sɛ ayarefoɔ a wɔwɔ aban ayaresabea ahodoɔ no yɛɛ kɛseɛ berɛ a nnuruyɛfoɔ nkumaa ne nnuruyɛfoɔ nnum3333 a apɔmuden Asoeɛ Asoeɛ Asoeɛ Asoeɛ no yɛɛ wɔn adwuma no.
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Fekuw no kyerɛkyerɛfoɔ panin, Mthabisi Anele Bhe kaeɛ sɛ n’ani nnye asɛm a kan ɔmampanyin Constantino Chiwenga kaeɛ nnɛra sɛ nnuruyɛfoɔ nkumaa da so ara kɔ sukuu no ho.
Chiwenga a ɔman no paw no sɛ ɔnni nkitahodie a ɛda aban ne nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔn ho yɛ hu ntam no anim no yii ayarehwɛfoɔ no adi wɔ ɔko no akyi.
Nnipa pii a wɔkyerɛ sɛ Owura Chiwenga de asraafo redi dwuma wɔ nsɛm a ɛhwehwɛ sɛ wɔne wɔn di nkitaho no akasa atia wɔn nneyɛe.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ nkumaa ka sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ aban ma wɔn nnwinnadeɛ, nnuru ne ntadeɛ a ɛbɛbɔ wɔn ho ban bere a wɔreyɛ adwuma no, ne akatua a ɛbɛdɔɔso a wɔka sɛ ɛte sɛ ɔkraman tow.
Nanso aban no san ka sɛ ne nnwuma ayɛ basaa araa ma ɛrentumi nnya sika a ɛde bɛdɔɔso.
Yɛante apɔmuden soafoɔ panin Owura Obadiah Moyo nka bere a ɔkɔɔ nhyiamu bi a ɔne nnuruyɛfoɔ a ɔhwɛ mmofra yɛeɛ berɛ a yɛdii kan kɔɔ wim no.
Adwumayɛ Asɛnnibea no apoo aban abisadeɛ a ɛne sɛ aban nni nkrataa biara a ɛfa nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔnkɔ adwuma ho no.
Doug Coltart a ɔyɛ mmaranimfoɔ a ɔda Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Dɔkotafoɔ Fekuw ano wɔ Adwumayɛban mu no kaa sɛ, kyerɛwtohɔ a efi Apɔmuden Adwumayɛfoɔ Panin,HSB hɔ no nnɔɔso, enti yɛrentumi nni asɛm no ho dwuma wɔ mmara kwan so.
Asɛnnibea no hyɛɛHSB mmaranimfoɔ sɛ ɔmfa nkrataa a ayera no mma ɔkyena, Wukuada.
Nanso nnuruyɛfo aka nso sɛ ɛnyɛ kɔ a wɔbɛkɔ asɛnnibea no ne ade a ɛbɛma wɔakɔ adwuma, enti entumi nni ɔhaw no ho dwuma.
Kan Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Fekuw no panin abɛdiakyire, Oduruyɛfo Masimba Ndoro kaa sɛ n’adwuma hwehwɛ sɛ ɔyɛ daa adwuma, na ɛsɛ sɛ wotua no ka wɔ eyi ho.
Nnuruyɛfo nkumaa no kɔɔ so yɛɛ adwuma wɔ September da a ɛto so abiɛsa no. Wɔkae sɛ wonni sika a wɔde bɛyɛ adwuma.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔn mfe akɔ anim a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Kuo mu nso kɔɔ so yɛɛ adwuma Yawda a etwaam no, na wɔnwiinwii wɔ akatua pa ne ayaresa a ɛmfata ho.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔn mfe akɔ anim no nso kyerɛw krataa kɔbɔɔ wɔn amanneɛ sɛ mfasoɔ biara nni so sɛ nnuruyɛfoɔ bɛkɔ ayaresabea ahodoɔ a wɔnni ayaresabea ahodoɔ a ɛbɛgye ayarefoɔ nkwa.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ no kasa tiaa aban no sɛ sika no akɔ soro ɔha mu nkyem 60, na wɔkaeɛ sɛ wɔne no nyɛ adwene.
Ne nyinaa mu no, Zimbabwe Sukuupɔn no abɔ nnuruyɛfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ baanu nso soboɔ sɛ wɔde wɔn ho ahyɛ atuateɛ no mu na wɔrehyɛ afoforɔ ma wɔagyae adwuma.
Wɔn a wɔato wɔn asaworam ne Dr. Bothwell Mbuvayesango a ɔwɔ mmofra ayaresa ho nimdeɛ ne Dr. David Chimuka a ɔwɔ komayare ayaresa ho nimdeɛ.
Ɔbenfo Mbuvayesangano gyee din wɔ ɔman no mu berɛ a ɔyɛɛ ntafoɔ oprehyɛn maa wɔwoo wɔn wɔ afe 2014 mu na Ɔbenfo Wake yɛɛ komayare oprehyɛn kɛseɛ no.
Zimbabwe Nnuruyɛfoɔ Fekuw a ɛhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ so no akasa atia Dr. Mbuvayesangano ne Dr. Get up.
Yɛntee akwahosan ho nsɛm biara mfii Zimbabwe Sukuupɔn mu, na saa ara nso na yɛntee akwahosan ho nsɛm biara mfii aban hɔ.
Nanso asɛm bi a efi Akwahosan Soafoɔ Obadiah Moyo hɔ kyerɛɛ sɛ nnuruyɛfoɔ antie aban frɛ a ɛne sɛ wɔnsan nkɔ adwuma no.
Moyo kaa sɛ aban no retwɛn sɛ asɛnnibea asɛnni no bɛba awie, na ɛno akyi no ɔkaa tebea no kyerɛɛ ɔman no.
Nnuruyɛfo kɔɔ so yɛɛ adwuma wɔ September 3, na wɔkae sɛ wonni sika a ɛdɔɔso a wɔde bɛkɔ adwuma.
Aban no ne adwumakuo bi a ɛwɔ amannɔne ayɛ apam sɛ wɔbɛboa ma wɔde nnyansramma akɔ amannɔne te sɛ India ne Japan.
Berɛ a ɔne Victoria Consulting rekasa no, Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ fagudeɛtu so, Winston Chitant, kaa sɛ aban no adwene ne sɛ ɔbɛma ɔman no anya sika de ayɛ fagudeɛtu adwuma wɔ India.
Chitant kae sɛ wobu akontaa sɛ Zimbabwe wɔ nnyansramma tɔn ɔpepepem 25, nanso wotu biriw tɔn ɔpepem 2 kosi ɔpepem 3 afe biara.
Chitant san kaa sɛ India ne beae a wɔtɔn gyabiriw sen biara afe biara sɛ wɔde toto aman foforo ho.
Wɔ saa nhyiamu koro no ara ase no, ɔmampanyin Emmerson Mnangagwa kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ Zimbabwe de abusuabɔ pa a ɛda ɔman no ne India ntam no di dwuma.
studio7 ntumi nkyerɛɛ adwuma a Victoria Consulting adwumakuo no ayɛ mu adwuma ne adwumam mpanyimfoɔ.

Sikasɛm ho nimdefoɔ, Nyasha Muchichwa nso kaa sɛ wahu sɛ ɛho nhia sɛ Zimbabwe kɔhwehwɛ adwumakuo bi a ɛwɔ amannɔne a ɛpɛ sɛ wɔtɔn biriw wɔ Zimbabwe.
Owura Muchichwa kaa sɛ ɛyɛ papa nso sɛ yɛne aman foforo bedi nkitaho.
Ministry of Minerals wɛbsaet no se Zimbabwe wɔ nnyansramma a ɛsen biara, na ɛwɔ mmeae 29 a wotu biriw.
Nnwumakuo mmienu pɛ na ɛwɔ ɔman no mu a wɔfrɛ wɔn Hwange Colliery ne Mountain Resources.
Wɔayi MDC-T amanyɔkuo no mufo baasia a Nelson Chamisa di wɔn anim a wɔkyeree wɔn wɔ Harare Fida no mu biara dɔla 1,000 afi wɔn afie mu.
Magistrate Chancellor Bianca Makwande, Chamisa adwumayɛfoɔ baanu, Tendai Biti ne Awuraa Lynett Karenyi Korea; ɔman soafoɔ, Awuraa Gladys Hlatywayo; ɔman soafoɔ abadiakyire, Owura Lovemore Chinoputsa; ɔyɛ Ɔman Gyinabea Boayikuo no muni, na ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no kyerɛwfoɔ abadiakyire, David Chimhini ne Ms Vongai Tome.
Wɔhyɛɛ mmarima yi sɛ sɛ wɔkyere wɔn wie a, wɔn mu biara ntua dɔla 1,000 nnansa yi ara wɔ MDC mansini Morgan Tsvangirai Fie ho akyinnyegyeɛ no akyi.
Awuraa Makwande kaa sɛ nneduafoɔ no bɛsan akɔ asɛnnibea wɔ July 24 na wɔakɔ so atena address a wɔde ahyɛ polisifoɔ nsa no so akosi sɛ wɔbɛdi wɔn asɛm no.
Bere a wɔrekasa akyerɛ Studi 7 wɔ atɛmmuo no akyi no, mmaranimfoɔ baasia no mu baako, Alec Muchadehama, kaa sɛ asɛnnibea no hyɛɛ nnipa a wɔregyina wɔn ananmu no sɛ wɔnsiw nhwehwɛmuo no kwan wɔ asɛm no mu.
Owura Muchadehama nso kaa sɛ ɛwom sɛ nnansa yi ara wɔbɔɔ nnipa baasia no soboɔ sɛ wɔyɛ basabasa wɔ Criminal Law (Codification and Reform) Act ase deɛ, nanso wɔde nneduafoɔ a wɔbaa asɛnnibea anɔpa yi no san kɔɔ polisifoɔ adwumayɛbea a wɔbɔɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔato COVID-19 Prevention Act no.
Mmaranimfoɔ baasia no nso abɔ asɛnnibea no soboɔ wɔ sɛnea wɔyɛɛ nneduafoɔ no ho.
Owura Muchadehama kaa sɛ wɔn a wɔda afiase no nni ahobammɔ papa, na wontumi nkyere COVID-19 bere a ɔda afiase no.
Amanyɔkuo no mampanyin, Nelson Chamisa aka sɛ ɔbɛkɔ so ako ama nsakraeɛ wɔ ɔman no mu ɛmfa ho sɛ wɔbɛkyere emufoɔ no.
Awuraa Makwande aka sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ amanyɔkuo no kasamafo abadiakyire, Womberaishe Nhende a wɔrehwɛ no wɔ ayaresabea no da hɔ.
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ Owura Nhende pirapirae nnansa yi ara bere a wɔkyeree no de no kɔɔ ayaresabea no.
Wɔ asɛnnibea foforɔ mu no, Zimbabwe Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa Wɔ so no kyerɛ sɛ polisifoɔ bi a ɔde Ɔmanpanin Emmerson Mnangagwa totoo kɔndɔm a wɔde dii dwuma ho no, ɔkyeree no, na ɔgyee dɔla 300.

Nkɔmhyɛ kwan so Ayaresa ne Ogye (P HD) Asoeɛ panin, Walter Magaya asi ne bo sɛ wɔde no ato afiase wɔ Zimbabwe sɛ ɔne aman foforɔ reyɛ adwuma sɛ ɔbɛyɛ Aguma aduru a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔde sa HIV / AIDS, kokoram ne nea ɛkeka ho.
Wukuada anadwo a yɛrekasa akyerɛ Studio7 wɔ mpaebɔ dwumadie bi a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Francistown, Botswana awieɛ no, Owura Magaya kaa sɛ ɔrennyae nhyehyɛeɛ a wayɛ sɛ ɔbɛma polisifoɔ akyere no wɔ November 2018 mu berɛ a ɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wanya HIV / AIDS ano aduru no.
Bere a ɔsrɛɛ Owura Magaya sɛ ɔntɔn HIV / AIDS no, wɔbɔɔ no ka dɔla 700 wɔ February mu afe a etwaam no.
Nanso asɛm no amma Owura Magaya annyae a ɔka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ wɔne aman foforɔ a wɔmpɛ sɛ wɔbɔ wɔn din reyɛ adwuma, na ɔkaa sɛ wɔahu sɛ Aguma ayaresa no yɛ HIV / AIDS haw no ano aduru.
Owura Magaya kaa sɛ HIV / AIDS yɛ ɔhaw a ɛwɔ Afrika, enti ɛsɛ sɛ aman nyinaa bom yɛ adwuma na ama wɔanya ɔhaw no ano aduru.
Owura Magaya kaa sɛ ohui sɛ ɛfata sɛ ɔne aman foforo yɛ adwuma, efisɛ na Zimbabwe nni ahotoso sɛ aduru no bɛsa ɔman no mu nyarewa a edi awu no.
Nanso, wɔ asɛm a ɛtoo Magaya a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe no mu no, wohui sɛ Aretha Medical Company adwumakuo no nni Zimbabwe Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Nnuru so no tumi krataa, na wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ Apɔmuden Asoeɛ Asoeɛ no nhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnyɛ nhwehwɛmu nhu sɛ ebia Aguma aduru no yɛ adwuma anaa.
Dɔkota bi a ɔwɔ ayaresabea bi a ɛwɔ Francistown, Sengaphi Khuzwayo, kasa tiaa Magaya sɛ ɔrehwehwɛ sika.
Bere bi a atwam no na Owura Magaya ama akasakasa aba ɔman no mu bere a wɔkyeree no sɛ ɔreto ɔbaa foforo mmonnaa no, nanso akyiri yi, asɛm no kɔɔ asɛnnibea bere a wɔn a wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo no buu asɛm no gui wɔ mmara kwan so no.

Awuraa Lisa Sibanda yɛ ɔbea a wanya awo akyi adwenemhaw.
Awuraa Sibanda kaa sɛ ne ba a ɔda so ara yɛ ɔpatuwu no wui wɔ yafunu mu bere a wɔde no maa no Benada no, nanso dɔkota biara antumi ammoa no kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔyarehwɛfo bi a ɔmaa abofra no wui no boa no.
Awuraa Sibanda se ɔhaw a ɛsen biara ne sɛ wɔbɛhohoro wɔn ntini mu ntɛm araa ma ebetumi asɛe wɔn akwahosan.
Awuraa Sibanda se wɔn nso rehyia nsu ho nsɛnnennen na wɔrennya ayaresabea agyananbea na wɔreboaboa nsu ano dedaw.

Kokoram Fekuw a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe no hyɛ ɔmanfoɔ nkuran sɛ wɔnhwɛ sɛ wɔanya nufu mu kokoram ntɛm ansa na yareɛ no mu ayɛ den.
Nnipa bɛboro 5,000 na wohu sɛ wɔanya kokoram ahorow wɔ Zimbabwe afe biara, nanso wɔn mu bebree hu oduruyɛfo a ɔhwɛ mmofra wɔ saa yare a emu yɛ den yi ho.
Ahyehyɛde no titrani, Junior Mavhu se mprempren wɔayɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ wɔbɛhwɛ mmea ne mmarima a wɔanya nufu mu kokoram sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi anya mmoa ntɛm.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ kokoram kunkum nnipa pii wɔ ɔman no mu, ɛnkanka mmea, ɛwom sɛ ɛtaa kɔ so wɔ mmarima mu de.
Kokoram Asoeɛ foforɔ nso rehyɛ mmea ne mmarima nkuran sɛ wɔmfa hokwan a wɔanya wɔ October mu sɛ wɔbɛyɛ kokoram mu nhwehwɛmu na wɔnkyerɛkyerɛ wɔn yareɛ no ho pefee bere a wɔredi Wiase Nufu mu Kokoram Ɔsram no.
Wiase no rehwɛ kwan sɛ ɔsram yi bɛyɛ bere a ɛbɛkae nkurɔfo ma wɔahu nufu mu kokoram ne sɛnea wobetumi anya so mfaso.

Asoeɛ no kaa asɛm bi a ɛkyerɛ sɛ asraafoɔ ne polisifoɔ akunkum nnipa baasia no, na ɛkaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde awudifoɔ no kɔ atɛntenenee mu. Ɛsan nso kyerɛɛ sɛ aban no ntua wɔn a wɔakunkum wɔn no abusuafoɔ ka.

Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ sikasɛm so se ɛbɛma wɔanya sika pii, na ɛbɛma wɔanya sika kɛseɛ wɔ ɔman no mu sɛ ɔkwan a wɔbɛfa so adi sikasɛm mu ahokyereɛ a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no ho dwuma.
Ɔrekasa wɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu bi ase wɔ Harare nnɛ no, adwumayɛbea no kyerɛwfoɔ, George Guvamatanga kaa sɛ ɛrentumi nyɛ yie sɛ wɔbɛnya sika kɛseɛ a ɛbɛma wɔabɔ ka dɔla mmienu ne dɔla baako.
Guvamatanga kae nso sɛ n’adwumayɛbea nim sɛ ɔman no sikasɛm nyɛ papa na aban no bedi ɔhaw no ho dwuma.
Bere a wobisaa wɔn akwan a wɔbɛfa so adi sikasɛm ho nsɛnnennen ho dwuma no, Sikasɛm Soafoɔ Abadiakyire Clemence Chiduwa kaa sɛ wɔbɛbisa adetɔfoɔ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ dɛn anya sika no.
Sikasɛm ho nimdefoɔ bi a ɔwɔ Labor and Economic Development Research Institute of Zimbabwe, Nyasha Muchichwa kaa sɛ, sɛ aban no de sika hyɛ ɔman no mu a amannɔne nkitahodie nso ka ho a, ɛnna ɔbɛtumi adi sikasɛm nhyehyɛeɛ no so.
Owura Muchichwa nso kaa sɛ, sɛ wɔkyere sikasesafoɔ a, ɛrenni ɔhaw no ho dwuma sɛnea wɔbɛyɛ no nna kakraa bi na wɔasan afi wɔn dwumadie no ase.
Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ sikasɛm so agye atom nso sɛ sɛ wɔde sika a wɔde boa akwahosan nnwuma no toto akwahosan ho nsɛnnennen a ɛwɔ hɔ seesei no ho a, ɛnnɔɔso nanso wɔaka sɛ ɛbɛkɔ so atu mpɔn.
Sikasɛm Soafoɔ Mthuli Ncube nso ka kyerɛɛ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ wɔ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu ase sɛ n’ani agye akwan a wayɛ a ɛbɛma ɔman no sikasɛm atu mpɔn no ho.
Nanso kan sikasɛm soafoɔ, Tendai Biti, a ɔyɛ MDC-T akannifoɔ baasa no mu baako ka sɛ ɔman no sikasɛm mu ahokyereɛ reyɛ kɛseɛ berɛ a ɔman no sikakorabea kɛseɛ a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe no reyɛ nea ɛnsɛ sɛ ɔyɛ, na ɛresɛe ɔman no sika pii no.
Owura Biti a ɔno nso yɛ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie sikasɛm boayikuo no panin no kaa sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ sikasɛm asoeɛ ne sikakorabea kɛseɛ no yɛ wɔn adeɛ sɛnea ɛho mmara teɛ na amma ɔman no sikasɛm nhyehyɛeɛ anyera sɛnea aban mpanyimfoɔ bi bɔɔ bosea no.
Nanso sikasɛm asoeɛ no se ɛsɛ sɛ ɔmanfoɔ hunu sɛ ɔman no de mfeɛ pii ayɛ adwuma sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛhyehyɛ ɔman no, enti ɛgye berɛ na wɔatumi adi ɔhaw no ho dwuma.
Singer Rise Kagona ka ne abakɔsɛm wɔ sanku so na ɔne Biggie Tembo a waka baabi no na ɛyɛ adwuma.
Mmofra baanan wui anadwo biara wɔ China, na wɔkyerɛ sɛ sɛ ayarehwɛfo reyɛ wɔn adwuma a, ɛntaa nyɛ yiye.

Awuraa Chenai Chihwiti se ne papa, Owura Langton Chihwiti wui Wukuada bere a wɔde no kɔɔ Chinhoyi Ayaresabea a ɛwɔ Harare no.
Matilda Chimbi a ofi Banquet a na ɔreyi ne nuabarima a owui Nnɛra bere a wantumi ammoa no no kae sɛ ne nuabarima afrɛ no akɔ ayaresabea a wohui sɛ wawu no.

Mmofra ayarehwɛfo bɛboro 16,000 a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ aban ayaresabea ahorow de wɔn ho ahyɛ da a ɛtɔ so anum ɔsatu bi a ɛhwehwɛ akatua kɛse mu wɔ ɔman no mu.
Aban no ayi mmofra ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔagyae adwuma no nyinaa adi sɛ wɔda so ara hia sɛ wɔhwehwɛ adwuma.
Ɛwom sɛ nnipa a wɔanya COVID-19 no redɔɔso de, nanso nnipa pii nyɛ ahwɛyiye sɛnea Wiase Nyinaa Akwahosan Ahyehyɛde no kamfo kyerɛ no, te sɛ nkataanim a wɔhyɛ wɔ wɔn anim.
Ɛwom sɛ ɛda adi pefee sɛ ɔmanfoɔ retrɛw yareɛ no mu wɔ ɔman no mu, bɔs ahodoɔ mu ne sikakorabea ahodoɔ a nnipa ahyɛ mu ma, nanso wei ma Covid-19 trɛw yɛ mmerɛ.
Studi7 ahu nnipa pii a na wɔnhyɛ kaakaamotobi bere a na wɔne ɔmanfo hyia wɔ Harare kurow mu no.
Obi a ɔte Harare a wɔfrɛ no Paul Majaira a wɔammɔ ne ho ban no kae sɛ ɛtɔ mmere bi a ne werɛ fi sɛ ɔbɛbɔ ne ho ban.
Ná ɔbarima bi a wɔammɔ ne din retwɛn sɛ obegye sika afi sikakorabea bi a ɛwɔ kuropɔn no mu bere a wɔn a wɔne no di asi no ka kyerɛɛ studio7 sɛ onim sɛ COVID-19 yareɛ no redɔɔso wɔ ɔman no mu.
Nanso bere a na onim sɛ ɛho hia sɛ obi gyina hokwan ahorow a ɔwɔ akyi no, osuro a ɔwɔ sɛ ɔde ne ho begye nsɛm mu no ne ade titiriw a ɛma nnipa yɛ biako wɔ ɔhemmaa mu.
Simon Zhou a na ɔretwɛn bɔs sɛ ɔbɛkɔ Bepɔw a ɛyɛ anigye so no kaa sɛ wɔde nnɔnhwerew anan na akɔ saa beae koro no ara a anka ebetumi aka wɔn.

Apɔmuden Kyerɛwfoɔ a ɔwɔ MDC Apɔmuden kuo mu ne kan apɔmuden soafoɔ a ɔwɔ apɔmuden kuo mu, Dr. Henry Madzorera kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ nnipa bɔ wɔn apɔmuden ho ban na wɔdi akwankyerɛ a apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ de ma no so.
Oduruyɛfo He hyɛɛ wɔn a wɔte hɔ no nkuran nso sɛ wɔntena dan mu wɔ awɔw bere mu.

Ɔrekasa wɔ ne amanyɔkuo Politburo nhyiamu ase no, ɔmampanyin Emmerson Mnangagwa kaa sɛ nnipa a COVID-19 rekunkum wɔn no dodoɔ bɛka wɔn ma wɔasan asusuw bara a wɔabara wɔn no ho.
Nnipa a Covid-19 kunkum wɔn ne wɔn a wowuwu no nyɛ Zimbabwe nko, sɛnea ɛte wɔ aman pii a ɛwɔ wiase nyinaa a nnipa bɛboro ɔpepem 12 na wɔboro 88,212 wɔ Zimbabwe no.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ aban ayaresabea ne ayaresabea adwumayɛfoɔ pii akasa atia mpilo Mfinimfini Ayaresabea a ɛwɔ Bulawayo sɛ wɔn ani nnye ho sɛ wɔbɛkyere wɔn mu baako wɔ Memeneda wɔ Harare.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔn a wɔka United Bulawayo Ayaresabea ho no atoto Mpilo Ayaresabea apon mu, na wɔde nkrataa a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔn ani nnye ɔkyere a wɔkyeree Oduruyɛfo Magombeyi a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ankorɛankorɛ bi a wonnim no kyeree no fii ne fie wɔ Harare no.

KwaZulu-Natal polisi kasamafoɔ Panin Thembeka Mbele kaa sɛ Plessislaer polisifoɔ rehwehwɛ nnipakum mmienu mu.

Awofo yɛɛ basaa na wɔtoo sukuu no mu
AWOFO sɔre tiaa wɔn bere a kar tae bi bui wɔ Putini Ntoaso Sukuu a ɛwɔ Mangweni, Umtshezi anim no.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ awofo no nwiinwii wɔ mmofra no tebea a enye wɔ sukuu no mu no ho.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ mmofra kyere so wɔ sukuu dan mu, na nsu ne anyinam nkanea nni hɔ.
Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Nhomasua so a ɛmpɛ sɛ wɔsi sukuu no kasamafoɔ Panin a ɔwɔ Inkosi Langalibile Mansini a wɔfrɛ no S Prof. Mdakane kaa sɛ na ɔmanfoɔ no nwiinwii wɔ sukuu no ho.
“Yɛreyɛ adesua no wɔ baabi a Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ Nhomasua so no ahyehyɛ bere tiaa mu.
Ɔmanfo ani nnye eyi ho.
Ɔmanpanin Nkosingiphile Mpembe kaa sɛ: "Wɔ 2010 mu no, wɔhyehyɛɛ bere tiaa mu sukuu adan maa nkurɔfo nyaa anidasoɔ sɛ wɔbɛkɔ so asi sukuu no a wɔnyɛɛ bi da.
Mmofra a wɔresua ade no tebea nye, nsu dedaw no kɔhyɛ ntwitwiridii no mu, ɛmfata sɛ sukuufo no nom.
Ɔkaa sɛ, ɔsɔretia no akyi no, ɔpanyin bi baa hɔ a ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ ɛnnɛ adwumakuo bi a ɛfiri Nhomasua Asoeɛ bɛba abɛka asɛm no akyerɛ awofoɔ.

Wɔboro awarefo bi kum wɔn esiane sɛ wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔawia ade nti
AMANYƆFO rehwehwɛ nnipa bi a wɔn adwenem yɛɛ wɔn nãã a wɔbɔɔ awarefo bi wɔ Shayamoya wɔ Mpumuza, a ɛbɛn Pietermaritzburg, esiane sɛ na wosusuw sɛ wɔabɔ korɔn nti.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔmanfoɔ a Kwasida owuiɛ no na wɔboroo Londeka Mvelase ne Mxolisi Mchunu.
Ná awarefo no te faako.
Wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo sɛ wɔawia R2 500 ne ofipamfo bi telefon.
Wɔn a wobisabisaa wɔn nsɛm no hui sɛ bere a wɔpaa kyɛw akyi mpo no, wɔannyae boro a wɔboro wɔn no siw wɔn abo.
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ bere a wɔhwee mmea ne mmarima no, na wɔwɔ hɔ.
Ɔmanfoɔ panin bi a wɔfrɛ no Jabu Zondo kɔɔ mpɔtam hɔ kɔkaa asɛm no.
Bere a ɔrekasa akyerɛ Sol pane no, ɔkae sɛ ɛwom sɛ wɔbɔɔ wɔn sobo sɛ wɔawia ade de, nanso anka ɛnsɛ sɛ wokum wɔn.
“Maba mpɔtam ha.
Nsɛmmɔnedi ho nteɛm wɔ hɔ, ɛhaw yɛn ankasa wɔ saa beae yi, ɛwom sɛ wɔmma kwan mma ɔmanfo no ntua bɔne so ka de.
Ɛsɛ sɛ wofrɛ polisifo na wɔkyere wɔn a wɔyɛɛ saa no.
Ɛdenam nsɛm a me nsa kae so no, wɔbɔɔ wɔn a wɔkyeree wɔn no sobo sɛ wɔrewia ade wɔ sotɔɔ mu.
Seesei yɛwɔ ahotɔ, asomdwoe wɔ hɔ.
Abarimaa no nni baabi a ɔte, ɔbea no wɔ baabi a ɔte.
Mɛkɔ so ahwehwɛ n’abusua, na yebehyia wɔn ɔkyena (t Today) ne wɔn asusuw asɛm no ho.
KwaZulu-Natal polisi kasamafoɔ Panyin Nqobile Gwala kaa sɛ nnipa mmienu na wɔadi awu na polisifoɔ da so ara rehwehwɛ wɔn a wɔasisi wɔn no.
Esiane sɛ na wɔn dodow nni hɔ kosi sɛ nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfoɔ bɛnyaa wɔn nti, wɔantumi anhu wɔn a wohuu amane no mmusua.
Ná Guptafo no de sum ase aguadi rekɔ sikakorabea ahorow
SƐNEA nhwehwɛmu bi kyerɛ no, sɛnea Shadow World kwankyerɛfo, Paul Edward Holden kyerɛ no, wobu akontaa sɛ ɔman no amfa R49 billion anni dwuma ɔkwammɔne so.
Ɔkwankyerɛfoɔ no kaa saa asɛm yi wɔ boayikuo bi a Ɔtemmufo Raymond Zondo di anim.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ wɔhunuu sɛ sika no yɛ R49 157 323 233
Wɔde 68 koguu sikakorabea ahorow daa.
Holden kaa saa asɛm yi de dii sika a wɔde kɔtoo sikakorabea ahodoɔ no ho adanseɛ.
Holden bisabisaa ɔdansefo panyin, Advocate Matthew Chaskalson nsɛm.
Holden ka kyerɛɛ adwumakuo no sɛ n’adanseɛ no gyina amanneɛbɔ ne sɛnea wɔretua sika ama Gupta nnwuma.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ Guptas de R287 faa sum ase fii Estina Dairy Farm Project hɔ.
Na nhyehyɛeɛ no ne sɛ wɔbɛyɛ akuafoɔ wɔ Free State.
Holden kaa sɛ Guptas fii ase de sika faa sum ase afe ansa na Estina dwumadie no refi ase.
Free State aban no fii ase de sika boaa Estina dwumadi no wɔ June 2011 mu nanso Guptas fii ase de sika kɔɔ dwumadi no mu wɔ May 2011 mu.
“Wɔnam Estina nhyehyɛe no so de sika siee sum ase ansa na dwumadie no refi ase,” Holden kae.
Sɛnea amanneɛbɔ no kyerɛ no, aban tuaa R287 million maa Gupta abusua no, na wɔde sika no kɔhyɛɛ adwumakuo ahodoɔ sika mu maa ɛyɛɛ te sɛ nea ɛreyɛ R880 million wɔ afe 2012 ne afe 2016 ntam.
Adwuma no gu so.
Video a ɛka Ayeforokunu no wu ho nsɛm nyinaa
ƐDA a wokum Lindani Myeni wɔ Hawaii, USA, no ho video bi a ɛda nsow aba
Wɔ video no mu no, ayeforokunu no pue wɔ ofie bi mu wɔ Honolulu a ɔhyɛ ahemmotiri na ɔnam nnipa baanu a wɔfrɛ wɔn awarefo no akyi.
Ɛte sɛ nea ɔkɔɔ asɔrefie a ɛbɛn wɔn fie no.
Oyii ne mpaboa fii asɔrefie hɔ na ɔpaa mmarima baanu no kyɛw.
Wɔka sɛ bɛyɛ anibu 40 akyi no, wohuu Ayeforokunu no sɛ ɔrefi fie hɔ akɔpa awarefo no kyɛw.
Saa bere no ara na ɔbea bi baa hɔ bɛfrɛɛ nnipa 9 1911 sɛ ɔrekɔbɔ korɔnbɔ ho amanneɛ.
Ɔbea no ka kyerɛɛ polisifo sɛ ne kunu wɔ wɔn fie reba fie hɔ.
Sɛnea afiewuranom kyerɛ no, wɔamfa hwee amfi wɔn fie.
Wɔn a wɔtaa n’asɛm no akyi rebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛma wɔn nsa aka saa asɛm yi ankasa wɔ Intanɛt so.
Nanso, Ɔtemmufo Jim Bickerton kaa sɛ asɛnnibea no ahyɛ aban mpanimfoɔ sɛ wɔnyi video no nanso wɔnsɔn so.
Wɔka kyerɛɛ polisifo nso sɛ wɔmfa nnipa 911 a wɔfrɛɛ wɔn saa da no ho kyerɛwtohɔ mma.
Wɔ nsɛm a wobisabisaa Bickerton ne Owura William Denselow a ɛwɔ eNCA no mu no, ɔdaa no adi sɛ bere a Ayeforokunu no fii fie hɔ no, ne bo amfuw.
Bickerton kaa sɛ, “Ɔkaa nsɛm a etwa to no, na ɛsɛ sɛ ɔpa kyɛw kosi sɛ obewu.”
Wɔ video a edi kan a woyii polisifo adi mu no, Ayeforokunu no bisaa wɔn nnipa ko a wɔyɛ, wɔn na wɔtoo tuo kum no bere a owui wɔ ayaresabea no.
Ɔkae sɛ wonnim sɛ Myeni yɛ obi a ɔpa kyɛw na polisifo wɔ video no nanso ɔfrɛɛ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ nhyiamu sɛ wɔatow ahyɛ wɔn so sɛnea ɛnsɛ.
Bickerton kae sɛ wɔbɛkɔ so ahwehwɛ nokware no sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobehu nea ɛrekɔ so no.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ IFP mu kyɛfa bi sɔree wɔ Melmoth
Wɔbɔɔ IFP mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ soboɔ sɛ wɔrehaw awɛmfoɔ a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔbɔɔ ɔmanfoɔ baasa tuo kum wɔn wɔ amanyɔkuo nhyiamu bi ase wɔ Thubalethu, Mthonjaneni (Melmoth) Kwasida anwummere.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ awɛmfoɔ a Kurow sohwɛfoɔ no bɔɔ wɔn tuo no bɔɔ ɔmanfoɔ a wɔkaeɛ sɛ bɔɔlbɔfoɔ no too nhyiamu asa no ano kwan mu no gui.
Ɔman no fã bi bɔɔ amanyɔkuo no mpanyimfoɔ soboɔ sɛ wɔbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtwe wɔn nkotodwe berɛ a wɔhyɛɛ ɛhɔ mmarahyɛ baguani bi sɛ ɔnsan nkɔ wɔn man mu.
IFP mpanyimfoɔ a wɔwɔ King Cetshwayo mantam mu na wɔfrɛɛ nhyiamu yi sɛ wɔnkyerɛkyerɛ asɛm a ɛpaapae ɔman no mu, efisɛ nnawɔtwe a etwaam no ɔkasa tiaa mmarahyɛ baguafoɔ a wɔatu wɔn nyinaa, a kan kurow sohwɛfoɔ Bonginkosi Biyela ka ho a wɔasan agye wɔn no.
Ɔmanfoɔ a na ɔka atuo a wɔtotoweeɛ no ho no, ɔbɔɔ IFP mpanyimfoɔ ne mmarahyɛfoɔ a na wɔwɔ hɔ no soboɔ sɛ wɔnka nkyerɛ awɛmfoɔ sɛ wɔntow wɔn tuo sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔnna wɔn abufuo adi.
"Yɛrekasa wɔ abɔnten so efisɛ na wɔmma yɛn kwan mma yɛnkɔ asa no so efisɛ na nnipa a wofi mmeae foforo ayɛ mu ma.
Ɔhaw no fii aseɛ berɛ a yɛkyeree ɔmanfoɔ panin foforɔ a na ɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ ɔbɛfa ɔkwan a wɔato mu no so, na awɛmfoɔ ne mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a na wɔwɔ hɔ no nyaa kwan sɛ wɔbɛtoto tuo no.
IFP kannifoɔ a ɔwɔ Mthonjaneni a ɔmpɛ sɛ wɔbɔ ne din no kaa sɛ ɔmanfoɔ a wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ no mu akyɛ.
Dapɛn a etwaam no, wɔkasa tiaa wɔn sɛ wɔnkyerɛkyerɛ wɔn mannifo a wɔayi wɔn afi afi afiase no mu.
Wɔayɛ nhyiamu ama mmarahyɛ baguafoɔ nyinaa ne IFP mantam mu mpanyimfoɔ sɛ wɔmfa mmuaeɛ mma ɔmanfoɔ.
“Ɔhaw no fii aseɛ berɛ a ɔmanfoɔ bi gyinaa asa no akyi, na berɛ a nhyiamu no hyɛɛ aseɛ no, wɔsiw ɔkwan a ɛda asa no ano, na wɔhyehyɛɛ aboɔ wɔ awɛmfoɔ hɔ, na wɔhyɛɛ wɔn ma wɔtotow atuo, efisɛ na ɔmanfoɔ no rebɛtow ahyɛ wɔn so.
Ɔkaa sɛ, na ɔmanfoɔ binom de tuo akura wɔn ho.
Kurow sohwɛfo a wɔapaw no foforo, Mbangiseni Biyela, ne nanmusini a wɔfrɛ no Phumlani Ntombela ne mmarahyɛ baguafoɔ a wɔwɔ Mthonjaneni Mantam mu nyinaa na ɛbaa nhyiamu no.
Mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wɔbɛma mmuae afi ɔmantam no mu mpanyimfo hɔ no anyɛ yiye efisɛ na wotumi twa wɔn ahunmu nsrahwɛ no mu na wɔantumi ammua nkrasɛm no.
Ɔman no kasamafoɔ Thami Shangase kaa sɛ ɛnyɛ ɔman no na ɔyɛɛ nhyiamu no ho nhyehyɛeɛ, na ɔde kaa ho sɛ ɛyɛ polisifoɔ nsam.

Nea ɛka Cosafa Bɔɔlbɔkuo a wɔde asiesie wɔn ho ama Afcon no ho no, ɛsɛ sɛ Zimbabwe san gyina nkonimdifoɔ a wɔdii nkonim wɔ afe a ɛtɔ so nsia a atwa mu no akyi, a ɛwɔ anidasoɔ sɛ ɛbɛhyɛ din pa a ɔwɔ sɛ Afrika Atifi fam bɔɔlbɔkuo wɔ afe yi mu no mu den.
Esiane sikasɛm mu ahokyere nti, Zimbabwe ntumi nhwehwɛɛ akuw a wɔbɛbɔ wɔn ho mmɔden wɔ akofoɔ a wɔbɔɔ wɔn ho mmɔden ansa na agumadi nhyehyɛeɛ no refi aseɛ ne akofoɔ a wɔbɔɔ wɔn ho mmɔden ansa na agumadi nhyehyɛeɛ no reba a ɛwɔ hɔ ansa na agumadi nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ ansa na agumadi nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ ansa na agumadi nhyehyɛeɛeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ ansa na agumadi nhyehyɛeɛeɛ a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu.

Chidzambwa dii Cosafa cup no so nkonim wɔ 2003 2009, 2017 ne 2018 mu.
Zimbabwe agumadifo afoforo te sɛ Tendai Darikwa, Admiral Muskwe ne Alec Mudimu nso pɛ sɛ wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ Cosafa Bɔɔlbɔ a wɔte nka sɛ wonnim no mu.
Afe yi, Zimbabwe ne bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛyɛ den sen biara wɔ agumadi no nyinaa mu berɛ a wɔn bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛrekɔ Afcon a wɔn a wɔbɔɔlbɔkuo te sɛ Nimdeɛ Musona ne Marvelous Nakamba ka ho.
Zimbabwe Akofo kuo bi muni a wɔfrɛ no Shingirai Miti se biribiara nni hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ osi ma Cosafa, efisɛ wɔn a wɔde wɔn ani asi wɔn so no yɛ Zimbabwefo.
Esiane sɛ akofoɔ yi adi Cosafa Bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu nkonim nti, wɔrehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔbɛfa ɔkwan a ɛdi kan a wɔbɛfa so adi nkonim wɔ Afcon akansi no mu na wɔne Egypt adi nkonim wɔ wɔn akansi no mu.
Bɔɔlbɔkuo no bɔɔlbɔni Ronald Pfumbidzai se wɔnkɔ Egypt nkɔka wɔn a wɔwɔ hɔ no ho.
Zimbabwe ne Kuo A na ɛwɔ, Democratic Republic of Congo ne Uganda, baabi a Akofo adwuma sohwɛfo Wellington Mpandare wɔ ahotoso sɛ ɔbɛkɔ no.
Zimbabwe refi South Africa wɔ Cosafa akansi no awiei wɔ June 8 bere a ɔnam kwan so rekɔ Nigeria wɔ Afcon a ɛwɔ Egypt no.

Amalgamated rural Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ Kuo a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe (ARTUZ) se ɛbɔɔ aban amanneɛ sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ ɔdi n’asɛm no ho dwuma wɔ nnafua nnanum ntam.
Fekuw no se ɛpɛ sɛ akyerɛkyerɛfo akatua yɛ US dɔla ahanum, anaa ɛbɛyɛ US dɔla ahanum.
Wɔde ARTZ amanneɛbɔ no maa aban no Fida ɛdenam aban dwumadie, Ɔmanfoɔ Ɔsom Asoeɛ ne Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ sikasɛm so.
studio7 ntumi ntee asɛm no mfii aban nkyɛn, efisɛ wɔne Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Nkitahodie so Monica Mutsvangwa nni nkitaho wɔ ne telefon a wokura kyin so.
ARTUZ mampanyin Obert Masaraure ka sɛ, sɛ́ agumadi kyerɛfo no, wɔn nso pɛ asetra pa, nanso ɛnyɛ nea wɔpɛ na ɛrekɔ so.
Masaraure se ɛwom sɛ aban se sikasɛm ho asɛm haw no deɛ, nanso sɛ ɔko tia dwowtwa wɔ ne baa dwumadibea na ɔhwɛ ɔmanfoɔ sikasɛm so a, ɛbɛtumi ama nneɛma ayɛ yie.
Masaraure se aban sika no fã kɛse no ara resɛe wɔ nneɛma a ɛho nhia te sɛ amannɔne akwantuo, kar akwanhyia ne nneɛma foforɔ a yɛde bɛto nkyɛn sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛbɛnya akatua pa ama ɔmanfoɔ.
Masaraure ka sɛ, sika wɔ ɔman no mu a ebetumi asiesie ɔhaw no, nanso ɔhaw no ne sɛ ɔman no ntotoeɛ nyɛ adwuma yiye, na wonhu hia a ɛho hia sɛ aban mpanyimfoɔ siesie nneɛma.
Amannɔne aman renwiinwii wɔ akwantu tumi krataa foforo a wɔbɛtɔ anaa apam foforo a wɔbɛyɛ ho.
Eyi akyi no, aban no tui Dwoda nnawɔtwe yi bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔama Kwan sɛ wɔmfa Zimbabwefoɔ a wɔwɔ amannɔne dɔla ɔpepem 388.
Bere a ɔrekasa akyerɛ nsɛnkyerɛwfoɔ no, Ɔman Soafoɔ Kazembe Kazembe kaa sɛ n’adwumakuo no nim sɛ nkurɔfoɔ hwɛ kwan sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka wɔn akwantuo tumi krataa ntɛm ara, na nnipa a wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka saa nkrataa yi, ɛnkanka wɔn a wɔwɔ amannɔne.
Kazembe kaa sɛ, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɔman a ɛwɔ amannɔne no bɛnya mmara mu nkrataa wɔ wɔn man mu no, aban no ahu sɛ ɛfata sɛ ɔma ɛboɔ no kɔ soro, na ɔde saa nkrataa yi bɛma ntɛm ara.
Nanso wɔn a wɔatu akɔ ɔman foforo so no bi te nka sɛ aban ayɛ nhyehyɛe yi sɛ ɔbɛma amannɔne nkitahodie akɔ so.
Sɛ wɔkyekyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a, obi a okura tumi krataa wɔ ɔman no mu tua dɔla 53 wɔ RTGS ho, na obi a ɔpɛ sɛ ofi adi nnansa ntam no tua dɔla 250.
Wɔbɔ ka dɔla 380 wɔ akwantu tumi krataa a wɔde ama wɔ da koro ntam no ho.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie boayikuo a ɛhwɛ amannɔne nsɛm so no guamtrani, Kindness Paradza kaa sɛ, ne boayikuo no agyina akwantuo no akyi denneennen sɛ akwantuo a ɛbɛboa saa nnipa yi ama wɔn nsa aka wɔn nkrataa a ɛwɔ wɔn man mu no.
Paradza kaa sɛ akwantufo pii ate sɛ wɔawia wɔn abusuafo ne wɔn nnamfo, na wotuaa sika bebree wɔ wɔn akwantu tumi krataa ho.

Neymar a wɔwoo no São Paulo, Brazil ne ne din ankasa ne Neymar da Silva Santos Júnior.

Mighty Warriors mmea bɔɔlbɔ kuw no rehyia agumadi kɛse bi wɔ wɔn abakɔsɛm mu a ɔmanfo pɛ sɛ Zimbabwe di nkonim sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛhyɛn ɔman no agumadi abakɔsɛm mu.
Efi afe 1980 reba no, Akofoɔ a wɔyɛ den yi rekɔ Rufaro Agumadibea Kwasida wɔ wɔn akansi a ɛsen biara mu bere a Zimbabwe fii amanaman ntam akansi aseɛ.
Mmea bɔɔlbɔ kuw no rehyia Indomitable Lionesses a ɛwɔ Cameroon no wɔ agumadi bi a ɛbɛkyerɛ sɛ ebia Zimbabwe bɛfata ama afe a ɛreba no Olimpik Agumadi wɔ Rio de Janeiro.
Nnawɔtwe mmienu a atwam no, wɔboroo Akofoɔ Kɛseɛ no 2 - 2 wɔ Yaounde, nanso wɔhia nkonim 1 - 3 pɛ na ama wɔafata ama Wiase Nyinaa Bɔɔlbɔ.
Bere a wɔfata maa akansi no wiei no, Mighty Warriors no de bɛyɛɛ kuw a ɛtɔ so abien wɔ mfeɛ 35 mu sɛ wɔde bɛsi akansi no wɔ 1980 gold hockey mmabea no akyi.
Nanso Mighty Warriors no kɔɔ fam wɔ abakɔsɛm mu sɛ kuw a edi kan a wɔadi nkonim wɔ akansi no mu bere a wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ mmeawa a wɔde wɔn kɔɔ hɔ wɔ Moscow akyi no.
Akorɔmfoɔ panin Zivanai Moroyiwa se wɔretwentwɛn wɔn nan ase sɛ wɔbɛka sɛ Akorɔmfoɔ Kɛseɛ no bɛma ɔmanfoɔ ani agye denam nea bɔɔlbɔkuo no anaa kuw biara nyɛɛ bɛyɛ mfeɛ 35 a atwa mu no so.

Zimbabwe Community a ɛwɔ South Africa, ahyehyɛde bi a ɛgyina Zimbabwefo ananmu a wɔte South Africa na wɔyɛ adwuma, se ɛhaw adwene kɛse wɔ adwowtwa bebrebe a ɛrekɔ so wɔ Johannesburg mmorɔn so a wosusuw sɛ Zimbabwefo na wɔreyɛ no.
Kuo no se nsɛmmɔne a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Hillbrow, Berea ne Yeoville no fa amannɔnefoɔ pii a Zimbabwefoɔ ka ho, a wɔn a wɔkyere nkurɔfoɔ sie, wɔn a wɔkyere nkurɔfoɔ sie ne awudifoɔ ka ho.
Zimbabwe Community a ɛwɔ South Africa kasamafoɔ a wɔfrɛ no Bongani Jánoszi kaa sɛ wɔayɛ nhyehyɛeɛ sɛ wɔbɛhyia polisifoɔ ama asɛm no asɔre na wɔahyɛ polisifoɔ nkuran sɛ wɔnyɛ ho biribi.
Ɔkaa sɛ February 6, a ɛbɛyɛ ɔsram a ɛdi hɔ no, n’ahyehyɛde no rehwɛ kwan sɛ ɔne polisifo a wɔhwɛ amantam no so behyia abom ayɛ adwuma de adi ɔhaw no ho dwuma.

Wɔn a wɔyɛɛ wɔn saa no mu bebree nim wɔn a wɔyɛɛ saa nsɛmmɔne no bi wɔ wɔn ankasa kasa mu, enti ɛsɛ sɛ polisifo a wɔreyɛ saa nsɛmmɔne no ne Zimbabwefo a wɔte saa mmeae yi reyɛ adwuma.

New Patriotic Party (NPP) Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie (MP) a ɛwɔ Dormaa East, Owura Paul Apraku Twum Barimah de asɛmmisa a egye ntɛmpɛ aba Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ wimhyɛn a kan Ɔmampanyin John Mahama de tuu kwan kɔɔ amannɔne wɔ afe 2013 ne 2017 mu no ho ka.
Ɔkaa asɛmmisa a ɔde kɔmaa Sikasɛm Soafoɔ, Owura Ken Ofori-Attah no ho asɛm sɛ ɛbɛboa ɔne Ghanafoɔ ma wɔahwehwɛ kyerɛwtohɔ ahodoɔ a ɛfoa nkɔmmɔbɔ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ aban mpanyimfoɔ nhyehyɛeɛ a kan ɔmampanyin no yɛeɛ no so.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Mebɔɔ asɛmmisa yi ho mmuaeɛ sɛ mɛte ɛka a ɔman yi bɔeɛ afe 2013 kɔsi afe 2017 mu berɛ a kan Ɔmanpanin Mahama de wimhyɛn a wɔahyehyɛ so tutuu akwan no.
Wɔnyɛɛ wɔn ade pɛpɛɛpɛ
Ɔrekyerɛkyerɛ ne botae a ɛne sɛ ɔde asɛmmisa a egye ntɛmpɛ a mprempren ɛwɔ Akasafoɔ Dwumadibea no bɛba no mu no, Owura Barimah kaa sɛ n’asɛmmisa no nni amanyɔsɛm mu nnyinasoɔ biara.
“Yei bɛyɛ berɛ a yɛyɛɛ yɛn adwene sɛ yɛbɛtu aban nhyehyɛeɛ wɔ wimhyɛn mu, na sɛ yɛhu sɛ ɛrekɔ so a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛgyina nea yɛayɛ dedaw no so si saa gyinaeɛ no nkutoo a, ɛnna yɛbɛtumi ayɛ.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “So biribi wɔ hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ? Sɛ biribi wɔ hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ a, dɛn na ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ? Aban akwankyerɛ bi wɔ hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛyɛ? Ɛnde ɛda adi pefee sɛ, mempɛ sɛ yɛde amanyɔsɛm bɛyɛ pɛ.”
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ: “Mepɛ sɛ yɛnya akyinnyegyeɛ ne ɔkasa a ɛfata sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛbɛtumi akyerɛ yɛn adwene. Ɛnnɛ, ɛbɛyɛ me aban, nanso ɔkyena ɛbɛyɛ obi aban, enti sɛ yɛanhwehwɛ nkyerɛkyerɛmu a ɛfata na yɛansɛe akwantuo yi a, yɛbɛkɔ tebea a ɛte saa mu daa.”
Asɛm a egye ntɛmpɛ a Ablakwa bisae
Amannɔne Nsɛm Ho Boayikuo mu panin, Owura Samuel Okudzeto Ablakwa nso bisaa asɛm bi a ɛho hia paa wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie sɛ ɔnkyerɛ nea enti a Ɔmanpanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo-Addo amfa wimhyɛn ankɔ France nnansa yi ara.
