Ɔsan buu akontaa sɛ Ɔmanpanin akwantuo boɔ boro GH ɔpepem mmienu.
Bono Apueɛ Mantam Soafoɔ, Owura Kwasi Adu-Gyan akamfo Amanyɔkuo (NPP) ne National Democratic Congress (NDC) sɛ wɔayɛ biako ama asomdwoeɛ atena ɔmantam no mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “M'ani agye paa sɛ mahu sɛ NPP ne NDC a ɛwɔ Bono East no reyɛ adwuma asomdwoe mu de asiesie amanyɔsɛm mu ntawntawdi a ɛda wɔn ntam no,”
Owura Adu-Gyan kaa sɛ asomdwoeɛ na ɛmaa nkɔsoɔ baeɛ na ɔde kaa ho sɛ sɛ asomdwoeɛ nni hɔ a ɛbɛyɛ den sɛ nkɔsoɔ bɛba ɔmantam no mu.
Ɔmantam soafoɔ no de nkamfoɔ yi too dwa wɔ asɛm bi a ɔde too gua wɔ Techiman akyi.
NPP ne NDC ananmusifoɔ, atumfoɔ ananmusifoɔ, ahobammɔ adwumakuo, Abatoɔ Asoeɛ (EC) Ɔman Asoeɛ anaa Ɔman Adesua (NCCE) ne ɔmanfoɔ ahyehyɛde ahodoɔ (CSO) na ɛbaa nhyiamu no ase.
Ɔman Asomdwoeɛ Bagua na ɛyɛɛ nhyiamu yi ho nhyehyɛeɛ na na asɛmti no ne sɛ: “Countering Post 2020 Election Violence and Building Consensus for Greater Political Tolerance in Ghana”
Nsɛmti a wosusuw ho no fa basabasayɛ a ɛkɔ so wɔ abatow mu ne nsɛm a ɛkɔ so wɔ abatow mu a wosiesie ho.
Owura Adu-Gyan kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ Ghanafo hoahoa wɔn ho sɛ wɔabu ɔman no sɛ ɛno ne ɔman a ɛto so abien a ɛpɛ asomdwoe paa wɔ Afrika wɔ Wiase Nyinaa Asomdwoeɛ Amanneɛbɔ a ɛbaa afe 2021 mu no mu, na ɔkyerɛɛ hia a ɛho hia sɛ NPP ne NDC bom boa ma asomdwoeɛ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ ɔman no mu no kɔ so na ɛhyɛ mu den.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Yei yɛ mmɔden a ahemfoɔ, amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ, bammɔ adwumayɛfoɔ, ne mpanyimfoɔ, Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ, Asɛnnibea ne nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔfoɔ abɔ.
Ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ Ɔmantam Nkitahodie Bagua (RCC) no bɛhwɛ ama asomdwoe a ɛho hia na ama wɔatumi ayɛ adwuma no akɔ so.
Berɛ a ɔrekasa afa Abatoɔ Atɛntrenee ho no, Abatoɔ panin a ɔda Bono Mantam Asomdwoeɛ Asoeɛ ano, Alhaji Suallah Abdallah Quandah kaa sɛ, abatoɔ atɛntrenee dii dwuma titiriw bi maa amammui nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu yɛɛ yie.
“Wom sɛ amanyɔsɛm mu atɛntrenee nyɛ foforɔ deɛ, nanso wɔagye atom sɛ ɛyɛ ade titiriw wɔ amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ nyinaa mu, sɛ ɛwɔ hɔ anaa ɛwɔ hɔ,” ɛkaa sɛ, na ɛkyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ amanyɔsɛm ne amanyɔkuo mu atɛntrenee yɛ adeɛ a ɛho hia a ɛbɛma amanyɔkuo ne amanyɔkuo mu basabasayɛ ho kwan.
Alhaji whenah sii so dua sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔyɛ ɔman no atɛntrenee nhyehyɛe mu nhwehwɛmu bere ne bere mu de hwɛ sɛ ɛbɛyɛ adwuma a ɛne sɛ ɛbɛma wɔato aba a ɛfata na ɛfata.
Mmarahyɛ baguani a ɔwɔ Abuakwa South Samuel Atta Akyea ama Ghanafo awerɛhyem sɛ Nana Akufo - Addo aban no bɛma wɔn tebea no ayɛ yiye bere a NPP di tumi fi January 7, 2017 no.
Ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ Ghanafoɔ bɛnya sikasɛm mu ahofadi wɔ Nana Akufo-Addo akanni ase, ɛnam sikasɛm nhyehyɛeɛ a nyansa wom a ɛbɛgu.
“January 7 bɛyɛ bere foforo a ɛde yɛn yiyedi ne yɛn ahofadi bɛba, ne titiriw no, sikasɛm mu ahofadi a Ghanafo rehwehwɛ no. Ghanafo behu sɛ Onyankopɔn agye ɔman no afi ahokyere mu,” Atta Akyea kae bere a ɔde ntoboa kɔmaa Asiakwa SOS wɔ East Akim Mansini a ɛwɔ Apueɛ Mantam mu no.
Ɔkaa sɛ wayɛ krado sɛ ɔbɛsom sɛ asafo mu ɔmampanyin, Nana Akufo-Addo.
Nneɛma a ɔde kɔe no bi ne ɛmo nkotoku ason, anwa a wɔnoa, nkyene, asikre, nufusu, nsa ne sika a wɔnkyerɛ mu.
Wɔahu anuanom mmea baasa a wɔdaa wɔn maame nsawe mu wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuta wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuaem mansini a ɛwɔ Atɔe fam mantam mu.
Wɔn baasa no wuwui bere a afiri bi a wɔde yɛ adwuma guu wusiw mu no.
Inspector Panin George Sekyi a ɔwɔ Tarkwa-Nsuta adwumayɛbea no kaa sɛ wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ no December 18, sɛ mmofra baasa awuwu wɔ baabi a wɔnom nsa.
Ɔkae sɛ ɔne ne mpanyimfo no de ahopere kɔɔ hɔ nanso wɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ wɔde nea wawu no, Abena Amos, a wɔfrɛ no Arabi Dadzi, a wɔfrɛ no Arabi Dadzi, a wɔfrɛ no 13 ne Akaba Dadzi, a wɔfrɛ no Akaba Dadzi, a wɔde no akogu Tarkwa Aban Ayaresabea dan a ɛretwɛn sɛ wɔbɛyɛ no oprehyɛn no mu.
Wɔ nsɛm a Starr News kyerɛwfo Emmanuel Ohene Gyan Owura Sekyi bisabisaa no mu no, ɔkae sɛ nea wawu no ne wɔn maame a ɔhwɛ ‘Golden City Kitchen’ a ɛwɔ Tarkwa Nsuem mantam mu no na ɛte.
Ɔkae sɛ wɔyɛɛ wɔn adwene sɛ wɔbɛda asanombea anadwo no bere a wɔboaa wɔn maame ma ɔtɔn nsa no.
Dwumadibea sohwɛfoɔ no kaa sɛ bosome da a ɛtɔ so dunson mu no wɔhyehyɛɛ anyinam nkanea firisɛ osu kɛseɛ bi tɔeɛ ɛda no mu, na ɛmaa Madam Dadzi de afidie hyɛɛ adidibea hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a nea wawu no bɛnya hann bere a wada no. Akyire yi mmeawa no maame huu wɔn sɛ wɔawuwu berɛ a ɔkɔɔ sotɔɔ hɔ anɔpa a ɛdi hɔ no.
Onuawa bi a ɔto so anan a wohui sɛ ɔno nso nnim hwee no regye ayaresa. Polisifo a wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ rehwehwɛ asɛm no mu.
National Democratic Congress (NDC) John Mahama ka sɛ ɔbɛdi Menzgold Nana Appiah Mensah panin akyi ama Menzgold Nana Appiah Mensah a nnipa pii frɛ no NAM 1, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a sɛ ɔdi nkonim wɔ December nhwehwɛmu no mu a, ɔbɛtwe adwadifoɔ a wɔde wɔn hyɛɛ mu no aso.
Bere a ɔrekasa wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuaem a ɛwɔ Atɔeɛ Mantam mu no, Owura Mahama dwenee nea enti a ɛte sɛ nea Akufo-Addo aban no ani nnye ho sɛ ɔbɛgye NAM1 agyapadeɛ na mmom ɔde wɔn abufuo bɛhyɛ adetɔfoɔ so.
“Dɛn na ɛda nsow wɔ NAM 1 ho araa ma Akufo-Addo rebɔ ne ho ban? Dɛn nti na wode polisifo gu adetɔfo a wɔn ho nni asɛm so bere a NAM 1 nantew kwa”
Ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ ne nniso a ɛdi hɔ no bɛhwehwɛ NAM1 ne n’akwankyerɛfoɔ no mu yie na ɔde akwan a ɛfata nyinaa ayi sika no.
Ɔmansin Asɛnnibea a ɛwɔ Nkran a Her Her Honour Ellen Asamoah na ɔhwɛ so no dii asɛm a Menzgold Nana Appiah Mensah ( NAM1) panin (CEO) de asɛm no kɔdan October 1, 2020 no ho dwuma wɔ September 7.
Ná Ɔman no adi kan abɔ NAM 1 sobo foforɔ wɔ Nkran Circuit Court wɔ June 24, 2020.
Abɛdiakyire a ɔda Polisifoɔ ano (ASP) Sylvester Asare kaa kyerɛɛ Asɛnnibea no sɛ n’akwankyerɛ ne sɛ ɔbɛkɔ so abɔ wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ no soboɔ.
Wɔ July 20, ASP Asare ka kyerɛɛ asɛnnibea sɛ, wɔreyɛ adwuma anibere so de atu asɛnnibea no fo wɔ asɛm no ho.
Ne saa nti, ɔbɔɔ asɛnnibea no mpae sɛ ɔmma wɔn kwan mma wɔntoa wɔn asɛm no so na ama wɔatumi atu asɛnnibea no fo wɔ adwene a wɔwɔ sɛ wɔde asɛm no bɛkɔ asɛnnibea no ho.
Ɔkae sɛ sɛ afotu no ba awie a, wɔbɛbɔ wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn sobo no amanneɛ sɛ wɔmfa wɔn nkɔ asɛnnibea nkɔyɛ nea ɛho hia no.
Nanso wɔ asɛnnibea hɔ Dwoda no, aban mmaranimfoɔ bɔɔ mpaeɛ sɛ wɔmma no kwan na wɔmaa no kwan.
Ná onipa a wɔabɔ no sobo no din 1 no wɔ asɛnnibea.
Wɔ July 26,201 no, Ɔmansin Asɛnnibea no maa NAM sika a ɛyɛ GH ɔpepepem 1 a ɛwɔ asɛnnibea nnum, abiɛsa a ɛfata.
Ná wadi mfomsoɔ wɔ soboɔ 13 a Ɔman no bɔɔ no no nyinaa ho. Efi saa berɛ no ɔman no ayɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ soboɔ a wɔabɔ no no mu.
Ɛsɛ sɛ ɔbɔ polisifo amanneɛ Wukuda biara nnɔnhwerew 10.
Mfitiaseɛ no, wɔbɔɔ no soboɔ sɛ ɔmfa nsɛmmɔnedi nto hɔ, ɔnam atosɛm so bɔ korɔn, ɔyɛ adwuma a ɛde sika kɔto sikakorabea a tumi krataa nka ho, ɔtɔn fagudeɛtɔn a tumi krataa nka ho, ɔde sika kɔto sikakorabea a mmara mma ho kwan, na ɔhoro sika.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ no agye sika ahodoɔ a ɛyɛ GH ɔpepepem mpem mpem nsia afi adetɔfoɔ hɔ.
Okada a wɔde di dwuma wɔ aguadi mu no redɔɔso ma ɛhaw adwene.
Polisifoɔ ada no adi sɛ nsɛmmɔnedi, akwanhyia, ne kar kwan so ahyɛdeɛ a ɛfa moto ho anya nkɔanim.
Akyinnye biara nni ho sɛ Okada ahunahuna no refi ne nsa na ɛho abehia sɛ wɔyɛ biribi a ɛbɛma ahotew aba ne dwumadi ahorow mu.
Yɛabɔ mmɔden mpɛn pii sɛ yɛde Okada bedi dwuma.
Seisei deɛ ɛyɛ den ma ɔman no sɛ wɔbɛdi moto ne sakre mmiɛnsa a wɔde di dwuma, ɛnkanka nneɛma a wɔde di gua no ho dwuma.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie a ɛwɔ afe 2012 mu no hyɛɛ mmara a ɛfa akwanhyia ho wɔ ɔman no mu.
Nneɛma a ɛka ho no, mmara a ɛto so 128 a ɛwɔ afã anan kosi anan no kyerɛ sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔde moto a wɔtaa frɛ no ‘ Okoda’ ne sakre abiɛsa a wɔde di dwuma wɔ aguadi mu no hyɛ mmara ase, gye sɛ wɔde mena afoforo na wɔde mena afoforo. Afei nso ɛkyerɛ tumi krataa a ɛwɔ hɔ no sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔde hyɛ mmara ase sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔde hyɛ mmara ase sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛbɛma obi atua ne ka.
Ɛmfa ho saa mmara yi no, okada ne sakre abiɛsa (pragya) afa akwantu nhyehyɛe no wɔ ɔman no afã pii.
Wɔ nkuraase no, okada ne Pragya nkutoo ne ɔkwan a wɔfa so kɔ gua so, ayaresabea ne nkurow foforo mu, ne mmeae foforo.
Wɔ nnipa a wɔwɔ nkuropɔn mu fam no, wotumi de sakre no di dwuma de hwe kar akɛse no mu.
Esiane sɛ sakre bo nyɛ den nti, ɛma wotumi tu kwan a ne bo nyɛ den.
Afei nso wɔn ho tɔɔ wɔn esiane sɛ wonni ɔmanfo akwantu nhyehyɛe a edi mu na wotumi de ho to so nti.
Nanso, nnipa bebree kyi okada ne Pragya esiane ɔhaw a wɔde ba akwan so ne ebia obu a wɔnkyerɛ mma karka ho mmara nti.
Akwanhyia ne nnipakum bebrebe a ɛnam Okada a wɔde dii dwuma ɔkwammɔne so no nso haw adwene.
Nokwarem no, ahyehyɛde pii, a Ghana Medical Association ne National Road Safety Authority ka ho, ahyɛ sɛ wɔmmara wɔn dwumadie sɛ ɔkwan a wɔfa so tu kwan wɔ ɔman no mu.
Eyi agyaw ɔman no wɔ ɛpo bun mu.
Nea enti a ɛte saa ne sɛ, ɛmfa ho sɛ mmara no bara sɛ wɔmfa wɔn nni dwuma wɔ aguadi mu no, ɛyɛ ade titiriw a ɛma Ghanafo pii nya ahotɔ.
Wɔ yɛn a yɛwɔ Daily Graphic no fam no, yesusuw sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔman no de ne ho hyɛ mmara mu yiye na wɔyɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛfata a ɛbɛma ɔmanfo no anya nea wohia wɔ ɔkwan a eye sen biara so.
Sɛ nhwɛso no, wɔ India no, Pragya yɛ ɔkwan titiriw a wɔfa so tu kwan nanso yɛntee anwiinwii sɛnea yɛwɔ Ghana no.
Ɛnde, dɛn na yebetumi asua afi India na yɛde ahyɛ yɛn nhyehyɛe yi mu?
Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛma ɛtena yɛn adwenem sɛ, sɛ nnipa pii nnya adwuma nyɛ a, wɔn a wɔyɛ okada ne wɔn a wɔde sakre abiɛsa yɛ adwuma no bebu no sɛ ɛyɛ adwuma a ɛma wɔne wɔn mmusua nya sika.
Nanso sɛnea ɛte nnɛ no, okadas ne pragyas yɛ ɔhaw na yɛn a yɛwɔ Daily Graphic no gye di sɛ ɛdenam nhomasua, ahyɛde ne ahwɛyiye a wɔde bɛma nniso horow a ɛfata so no, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔma wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma no kari pɛ, sɛ wohu sɛ ɔman no ntumi nni wɔn akyi a.
Sɛ yɛresusuw mmara anaa nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ hɔ seesei no ho a, ɛbɛyɛ nea ɛfata koraa sɛ yɛbɛtete wɔn a wɔte sakre so ne wɔn a wɔde moto yɛ adwuma ne wɔn a wɔde moto yɛ adwuma ne wɔn a wotua akwanhyia ho sika.
Esiane sɛ nhyehyɛe a ɛte saa wɔ hɔ nti, ɛbɛyɛ mmerɛ ama Ghana Polisi Adwumayɛkuo no sɛ wɔbɛhwɛ ma mmara no ayɛ adwuma na wɔadi moto ne moto mmiɛnsa a wɔnyɛɛ ho kyerɛwtohɔ ne wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ nsɛmmɔnedi mu nso ho dwuma.
Seisei Ghanafoɔ adwene nhyia wɔ akwan atitiriw mmienu a wɔfa so tu kwan yi ho, efisɛ wɔn ho wɔ mfasoɔ na wɔn ho akyere wɔn.
Daily Graphic no gye di sɛ sɛ yɛpɛ sɛ yɛn akwan yɛ fɛ na yɛn akwantu nhyehyɛe tu mpɔn a, ɛnde ɛsɛ sɛ yeso nantwi no mu yiye na yedi ɔhaw no ho dwuma mprempren anaa bere biara.
Menkae da bi a m’ani gyei kɛse nnansa yi ara wɔ Ghana sen Fida a etwaam no.
Saa da yi na wɔhyɛɛ yɛn nyinaa nkuran sɛ yemfi adi nkɔtɛw dua.
Esiane sɛ mesan baa Ghana mfe 20 a atwam ni na mibehui sɛ yɛn man no tebea yɛ soronko koraa wɔ nea ɛwɔ Asase Ho Nsɛm nhoma mu no ho nti, na eyi ne mmɔden a ɛsen biara a wɔabɔ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ biribi de asiesie ɔsɛe pasaa a aba yɛn nsase so no.
Asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ nsase ne fagudeɛtu ho nsɛm so maa yɛn nsa kaa aba ɔpepem anum sɛ yɛnnua, na anigyeɛ bi wɔ hɔ a na menhyɛɛ no nsow da.
Ɛbɛyɛ sɛ Ghanafoɔ pii huiɛ sɛ adeɛ baako a ɛhia sɛ yɛde yɛn adwene si so kɛseɛ ne ɔman a yɛfrɛ no Ghana no.
Ɔkwan a asɛe, sukuu a asɛe, ayaresabea a mpa nni mu, sukuu mmofra a kɔmputa nni wɔn ho, ɔyare mmoawa a ɛwɔ hɔ no, nea ɛsen biara a ɛsɛ sɛ yɛn nyinaa nya na yɛn bo fuw koraa ne yɛn asase yi tebea, asase a ahwere ne kwae, nsubɔnten a ɛreyow, nea na anka ɛyɛ afɔw bosome wɔ May mu a ɛyɛ hyew na ɛreyow koraa no.
Menhwɛɛ Geography nkyerɛkyerɛ nhoma a wɔde redi dwuma wɔ yɛn sukuu ahorow mu nnɛ no mu, nanso minim sɛ Ghana asase so nnipa dodow no ara su wɔ nhoma ahorow a mede dii dwuma wɔ sukuu mu no nte sɛ ɛnnɛ Ghana.
Yɛda so ara ka kwaebirentuw ahorow ho asɛm, nanso ɛnte saa ankasa wɔ yɛn nsase yi so.
Yɛda so ara ka nkekaboa ho asɛm, nanso na wɔakyere wɔn akyere wɔn akyere wɔn atrae dedaadaw.
Kwaebirentuw ne wuram mmoa a wɔwɔ hɔ seesei no yɛ yɛn kasa fã, na ɛnyɛ yɛn ankasa kasa fã.
Nneɛma a na yesusuw sɛ ɛyɛ kwae mu nneɛma mpo no, wɔakyerɛ sɛ wɔasɛe no wɔ sika kɔkɔɔ ne fagude afoforo a wɔhwehwɛ mu.
Ebia yɛn mu dodow no ara huu yɛn tebea no na merehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔn a wɔamfa wɔn ho anhyɛ mu no wɔ ntease pa nti a wɔanyɛ saa.
